211: 
212: // Custom debug log function
213: function debugLog(...args) {
214:     const msg = args.map(a => typeof a === 'object' ? JSON.stringify(a, null, 2) : String(a)).join(' ');
215:     const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
216:     debugLogs.push(`[${timestamp}] ${msg}`);
217:     if (debugContent) {
218:         debugContent.textContent = debugLogs.join('\n');
219:         debugContent.scrollTop = debugContent.scrollHeight;
220:     }
221:     console.log(...args);
222: }
223: 
224: function debugWarn(...args) {
225:     const msg = args.map(a => typeof a === 'object' ? JSON.stringify(a, null, 2) : String(a)).join(' ');
226:     const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
227:     debugLogs.push(`[${timestamp}] ⚠️ ${msg}`);
228:     if (debugContent) {
229:         debugContent.textContent = debugLogs.join('\n');
230:         debugContent.scrollTop = debugContent.scrollHeight;
231:     }
232:     console.warn(...args);
233: }
234: 
235: // Fallback copy function for CEP environment
236: function fallbackCopyText(text) {
237:     const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
238:     textarea.value = text;
239:     textarea.style.position = 'fixed';
240:     textarea.style.top = '0';
241:     textarea.style.left = '0';
242:     textarea.style.width = '2em';
243:     textarea.style.height = '2em';
244:     textarea.style.padding = '0';
245:     textarea.style.border = 'none';
246:     textarea.style.outline = 'none';
247:     textarea.style.boxShadow = 'none';
248:     textarea.style.background = 'transparent';
249:     document.body.appendChild(textarea);
250:     textarea.focus();
251:     textarea.select();
252:     try {
253:         const successful = document.execCommand('copy');
254:         if (successful) {
255:             setStatus('Debug log copied to clipboard!', 'success');
256:         } else {
257:             setStatus('Copy failed - please select text manually', 'error');
258:         }
259:     } catch (err) {
260:         setStatus('Copy failed - please select text manually', 'error');
261:     }
262:     document.body.removeChild(textarea);
263: }

270: 
271: document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', authBoot);
272: 
273: /**
274:  * Auth-aware boot: checks authentication before initializing app
275:  */
276: async function authBoot() {
277:     // Load API config
278:     await loadAuthConfig();
279: 
280:     // Initialize login UI handlers
281:     initLoginUI();
282: 
283:     // Check if already authenticated
284:     if (isAuthenticated()) {
285:         hideLoginScreen();
286:         await bootApp();
287:     } else {
288:         showLoginScreen();
289:     }
290: }
291: 
292: /**
293:  * Boot the application (called after successful auth)
294:  */
295: async function bootApp() {
296:     try {
297:         // Update user display
298:         updateUserDisplay();
299: 
300:         // Load core ExtendScript from backend (OTA) — skip if local JSX already loaded via ScriptPath
301:         const localScriptLoaded = csInterface && await new Promise(resolve => {
302:             csInterface.evalScript('typeof generateSequence', result => resolve(result === 'function'));
303:         }).catch(() => false);
304: 
305:         if (localScriptLoaded) {
306:             console.log('[Boot] Local ExtendScript already loaded via ScriptPath, skipping OTA');
307:         } else {
308:             try {
309:                 const scriptResult = await loadCoreScript();
310:                 console.log('[Boot] Core script loaded via OTA:', scriptResult);
311:             } catch (scriptErr) {
312:                 if (scriptErr.name === 'AuthError') {
313:                     showLoginScreen();
314:                     return;
315:                 }
316:                 console.warn('[Boot] Core script load failed, continuing anyway:', scriptErr.message);
317:             }
318:         }
319: 
320:         // Check for asset updates (non-blocking)
321:         checkAssetUpdates().catch(err => {
322:             if (err.name === 'AuthError') {
323:                 showLoginScreen();
324:                 return;
325:             }
326:             console.warn('[Boot] Asset update check failed:', err.message);
327:         });
328: 
329:         // Initialize updater UI and auto-check for updates (non-blocking)
330:         if (typeof initUpdaterUI === 'function') {
331:             initUpdaterUI();
332:             autoCheckUpdate().catch(err => {
333:                 console.warn('[Boot] Auto update check failed:', err.message);
334:             });
335:         }
336: 
337:         // Initialize the main app
338:         init();
339: 
340:         // Start Claude Bridge server (local HTTP for skill communication)
341:         if (typeof startBridgeServer === 'function') {
342:             startBridgeServer();
343:         }
344:     } catch (error) {
345:         console.error('[Boot] Failed to boot app:', error);
346:     }
347: }
348: 
349: function init() {
350:     getDOMElements();
351:     bindEvents();
352:     initBriefModal();
353: 
354:     // Removed autoRestoreBoardLayout() to prevent loading old conflicting 4-hand data on restart
355:     loadPokerLayout();
356: 
357:     // Start in Board Setting mode with poker layout visible
358:     setPhase('board-setting');
359: 
360:     // Scan and populate deck dropdown, then auto-load first deck
361:     scanAndPopulateDecks();
362: 
363:     // Initialize Timeline Modules (Phase 1)
364:     initTimelineModulesIntegration();
365: 
366:     updateUI();
367:     setStatus('Ready - Load a deck and setup your cards');
368: 
369:     const user = getUser();
370:     console.log(`Autonim-Poker v2.0 initialized (user: ${user ? user.username : 'unknown'})`);
371: }

373: function initBriefModal() {
374:     if (quangBriefBtn) quangBriefBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
375:         if (briefModal) briefModal.classList.remove('hidden');
376:     });
377: 
378:     const closeDialog = () => {
379:         if (briefModal) briefModal.classList.add('hidden');
380:     };
381: 
382:     if (closeBriefModalBtn) closeBriefModalBtn.addEventListener('click', closeDialog);
383:     if (cancelBriefBtn) cancelBriefBtn.addEventListener('click', closeDialog);
384:     if (closeBriefOverlay) closeBriefOverlay.addEventListener('click', closeDialog);
385:     
386:     if (applyBriefBtn) applyBriefBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
387:         console.log("Applying Brief...", briefInput ? briefInput.value : "");
388:         // Logic will go here
389:         closeDialog();
390:     });
391: }

554: function bindEvents() {
555:     // Deck loading
556:     loadDeckBtn.addEventListener('click', handleLoadDeck);
557:     deckSelect.addEventListener('change', handleDeckSelectChange);
558: 
559:     // Search and filter
560:     cardSearch.addEventListener('input', filterTrayCards);
561:     suitFilterBtns.forEach(btn => {
562:         btn.addEventListener('click', () => handleSuitFilter(btn));
563:     });
564: 
565:     // Phase switching
566:     boardSettingBtn.addEventListener('click', () => setPhase('board-setting'));
567:     setupPhaseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => setPhase('setup'));
568: 
569:     // AI Phase Button
570:     aiPhaseBtn = document.getElementById('aiPhaseBtn');
571:     aiSection = document.getElementById('aiSection');
572:     aiBriefInput = document.getElementById('aiBriefInput');
573:     aiPresetSelect = document.getElementById('aiPresetSelect');
574:     aiGenerateBtn = document.getElementById('aiGenerateBtn');
575:     aiStatus = document.getElementById('aiStatus');
576:     aiError = document.getElementById('aiError');
577:     aiRefImageInput = document.getElementById('aiRefImageInput');
578:     aiRefVideoInput = document.getElementById('aiRefVideoInput');
579:     aiAttachPreview = document.getElementById('aiAttachPreview');
580:     if (aiPhaseBtn) {
581:         aiPhaseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => toggleAIPanel());
582:     }
583:     if (aiGenerateBtn) {
584:         aiGenerateBtn.addEventListener('click', () => handleAIGenerate());
585:     }
586:     if (aiRefImageInput) {
587:         aiRefImageInput.addEventListener('change', handleRefImageAttach);
588:     }
589:     if (aiRefVideoInput) {
590:         aiRefVideoInput.addEventListener('change', handleRefVideoAttach);
591:     }
592:     // AI Example buttons
593:     document.querySelectorAll('.ai-example-btn').forEach(btn => {
594:         btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
595:             if (aiBriefInput) aiBriefInput.value = btn.dataset.brief;
596:         });
597:     });
598:     recordPhaseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => setPhase('record'));
599: 
600:     // Board Setting Controls
601:     if (loadPresetBtn) loadPresetBtn.addEventListener('click', handleLoadPreset);
602:     
603:     // Live Preview using Actual Board
604:         let confirmPresetClick = false;
605: 
606:     // Mini Preview Window Logic
607:     const miniPreviewOverlay = document.getElementById('miniPreviewOverlay');
608:     const miniPreviewTable = document.getElementById('miniPreviewTable');
609:     const miniPreviewTitle = document.getElementById('miniPreviewTitle');
610: 
611:     let miniPreviewTimeout = null;
612:     document.querySelectorAll('.preset-btn').forEach(btn => {
613:         btn.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
614:             if (miniPreviewTimeout) {
615:                 clearTimeout(miniPreviewTimeout);
616:                 miniPreviewTimeout = null;
617:             }
618:             const presetId = btn.getAttribute('data-preset');
619:             const presetLabel = btn.querySelector('.preset-label')?.textContent || presetId;
620:             
621:             if (miniPreviewOverlay && miniPreviewTable) {
622:                 // Backup
623:                 const backupState = JSON.stringify(appState.boardLayout);
624:                 appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces = [];
625:                 appState.boardLayout.slotGroups = [];
626:                 
627:                 // Gen
628:                 if (presetId === 'poker') loadPokerLayout();
629:                 else if (presetId === 'pusoy') loadPusoyMultiLayout(4);
630:                 else if (presetId.startsWith('pusoy-')) loadPusoyMultiLayout(parseInt(presetId.split('-')[1]));
631:                 else if (presetId === 'omaha') loadOmahaLayout();
632:                 else if (presetId === 'array-2') {
633:                     appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces = [...generateArrayHand('bottom', 0), ...generateArrayHand('top', 1)];
634:                 }
635:                 else if (presetId.startsWith('saved:')) {
636:                     const savedJSON = localStorage.getItem('autonim_poker_layout_' + presetId.substring(6));
637:                     if (savedJSON) { try { appState.boardLayout = JSON.parse(savedJSON); } catch(e){} }
638:                 }
639:                 else loadPokerLayout();
640: 
641:                 // Render
642:                 miniPreviewTable.innerHTML = '';
643:                 const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
644:                 wrapper.style.position = 'absolute';
645:                 wrapper.style.top = '0';
646:                 wrapper.style.left = '0';
647:                 wrapper.style.width = '1280px';
648:                 wrapper.style.height = '720px';
649:                 // Increase scale to make the preview nicely fit inside
650:                 wrapper.style.transform = `translate(-50%, -50%) scale(0.5)`;
651:                 wrapper.style.left = '50%';
652:                 wrapper.style.top = '50%';
653:                 wrapper.style.transformOrigin = 'center';
654: 
655:                 const places = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces || [];
656:                 const groups = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || [];
657:                 places.forEach(p => {
658:                     const el = document.createElement('div');
659:                     el.className = 'mini-preview-marker';
660:                     el.style.left = p.x + 'px';
661:                     el.style.top = p.y + 'px';
662:                     let w = 124, h = 172;
663:                     if (p.isCommunityZone) { w = p.czWidth || 300; h = p.czHeight || 120; }
664:                     el.style.width = w + 'px'; el.style.height = h + 'px';
665:                     el.style.transform = `translate(-50%, -50%) rotate(${p.rotation || 0}deg)`;
666:                     el.style.border = '2px dashed rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.4)';
667:                     el.style.background = 'transparent';
668: 
669:                     const g = groups.find(x => x.slotIds && x.slotIds.includes(p.id));
670:                     if (g) {
671:                         el.style.borderColor = `color-mix(in srgb, ${g.color} 80%, black)`;
672:                         el.style.background = `color-mix(in srgb, ${g.color} 20%, transparent)`;
673:                     }
674:                     wrapper.appendChild(el);
675:                 });
676:                 
677:                 miniPreviewTable.appendChild(wrapper);
678: 
679:                 // Restore instantly
680:                 appState.boardLayout = JSON.parse(backupState);
681:                 
682:                 if (miniPreviewTitle) miniPreviewTitle.textContent = `${presetLabel} Preview`;
683:                 miniPreviewOverlay.classList.remove('hidden');
684:                 miniPreviewOverlay.classList.add('visible');
685:             }
686:         });
687: 
688:         btn.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
689:             if (miniPreviewOverlay) {
690:                 miniPreviewOverlay.classList.remove('visible');
691:                 miniPreviewTimeout = setTimeout(() => miniPreviewOverlay.classList.add('hidden'), 200);
692:             }
693:         });
694: 
695:         btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
696:             btn.classList.add('pop-effect');
697:             setTimeout(() => btn.classList.remove('pop-effect'), 300);
698:             if (miniPreviewOverlay) {
699:                 miniPreviewOverlay.classList.remove('visible');
700:                 miniPreviewOverlay.classList.add('hidden');
701:             }
702:             const preset = btn.getAttribute('data-preset');
703:             if (preset && presetSelect) {
704:                 presetSelect.value = preset;
705:                 presetSelect.dispatchEvent(new Event('change'));
706:                 if (loadPresetBtn) loadPresetBtn.click();
707:             }
708:         });
709:     });
710: // Sync button active state with dropdown change
711:     if (presetSelect) {
712:         presetSelect.addEventListener('change', () => {
713:             if (!document.body.classList.contains('previewing-preset')) {
714:                 const val = presetSelect.value;
715:                 document.querySelectorAll('.preset-btn').forEach(b => {
716:                     b.classList.toggle('active', b.getAttribute('data-preset') === val);
717:                 });
718:             }
719:         });
720:     }
721:     if (applyGridBtn) applyGridBtn.addEventListener('click', handleApplyGrid);
722:     if (addCardPlaceBtn) addCardPlaceBtn.addEventListener('click', handleAddCardPlace);
723:     var addCommunityZoneBtn = document.getElementById('addCommunityZoneBtn');
724:     if (addCommunityZoneBtn) addCommunityZoneBtn.addEventListener('click', handleAddCommunityZone);
725:     var addDealingSlotBtn = document.getElementById('addDealingSlotBtn');
726:     if (addDealingSlotBtn) addDealingSlotBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
727:         if (appState.dealingCard.enabled) return; // Max 1
728:         appState.dealingCard.enabled = true;
729:         if (dealingCardToggle) dealingCardToggle.checked = true; // Sync AE toggle
730:         renderDealingSlot();
731:         updateDealingSlotButton();
732:         setStatus('Dealing Card added — drag to reposition');
733:     });
734:     if (clearBoardBtn) clearBoardBtn.addEventListener('click', handleClearBoard);
735:     if (savePresetBtn) savePresetBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSavePreset);
736: 
737:     // Delete saved layout button
738:     const deletePresetBtn = document.getElementById('deletePresetBtn');
739:     if (deletePresetBtn) {
740:         deletePresetBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
741:             const val = presetSelect.value;
742:             if (!val.startsWith('saved:')) return;
743:             const layoutName = val.substring(6);
744:             if (!confirm(`Delete saved layout "${layoutName}"?`)) return;
745:             deleteSavedLayout(layoutName);
746:             presetSelect.value = 'poker'; // Reset to default
747:             deletePresetBtn.classList.add('hidden');
748:             refreshSavedLayoutsDropdown();
749:             setStatus(`Deleted layout: ${layoutName}`);
750:         });
751:     }
752: 
753:     // Show/hide delete button based on dropdown selection
754:     if (presetSelect) {
755:         presetSelect.addEventListener('change', () => {
756:             const btn = document.getElementById('deletePresetBtn');
757:             if (btn) btn.classList.toggle('hidden', !presetSelect.value.startsWith('saved:'));
758:         });
759:     }
760: 
761:     // Populate saved layouts dropdown from localStorage on init
762:     refreshSavedLayoutsDropdown();
763: 
764:     // Initialize CZ settings panel
765:     initCZSettingsPanel();
766: 
767:     // Edit Layout button (in setup/record mode)
768:     if (editLayoutBtn) editLayoutBtn.addEventListener('click', () => setPhase('board-setting'));
769: 
770:     // Table controls
771:     resetTableBtn.addEventListener('click', handleResetTable);
772:     overlapSlider.addEventListener('input', handleOverlapChange);
773: 
774:     // Per-zone flip controls (Poker layout)
775:     document.querySelectorAll('#pokerFlipControls input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(checkbox => {
776:         checkbox.addEventListener('change', handleZoneFlipChange);
777:     });
778: 
779:     // Grid flip controls
780:     if (flipAllFaceUp) flipAllFaceUp.addEventListener('click', () => handleFlipAllCards(true));
781:     if (flipAllFaceDown) flipAllFaceDown.addEventListener('click', () => handleFlipAllCards(false));
782: 
783:     // Assets folder
784:     selectAssetsFolderBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSelectAssetsFolder);
785: 
786:     // Recording controls
787:     addStepBtn.addEventListener('click', handleAddStep);
788:     if (finishStepBtn) finishStepBtn.addEventListener('click', handleFinishStep);
789:

791:     flipCardCheck.addEventListener('change', handlePropertyChange);
792:     slamEffectCheck.addEventListener('change', handlePropertyChange);
793:     spinEffectCheck.addEventListener('change', handlePropertyChange);

797:     exportToAEBtn.addEventListener('click', handleExportToAE);

801:     if (stopReplayBtn) stopReplayBtn.addEventListener('click', stopReplay);

805:     const stepSpeedValue = document.getElementById('stepSpeedValue');
806:     if (stepSpeedSlider) {
807:         stepSpeedSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
808:             replaySpeed = parseFloat(stepSpeedSlider.value);
809:             if (stepSpeedValue) stepSpeedValue.textContent = replaySpeed + 'x';
810:         });
811:     }
812:

815:     const stepBlendingValue = document.getElementById('stepBlendingValue');

817:         stepBlendingSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {

819:             if (stepBlendingValue) stepBlendingValue.textContent = appState.stepBlending + '%';
820:         });
821:     }
822:

824:     const dealSpeedSlider = document.getElementById('dealSpeedSlider');
825:     const dealSpeedValue = document.getElementById('dealSpeedValue');
826:     const dealTimeEstimate = document.getElementById('dealTimeEstimate');
827:     if (dealSpeedSlider) {
828:         dealSpeedSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
829:             appState.dealSpeed = parseInt(dealSpeedSlider.value);
830:             if (dealSpeedValue) dealSpeedValue.textContent = appState.dealSpeed + 'f/card';
831:             updateDealTimeEstimate();
832:         });
833:     }

836:     const saveProjectBtn = document.getElementById('saveProjectBtn');

840:     if (loadProjectBtn) loadProjectBtn.addEventListener('click', () => loadProjectInput.click());

848:                 var slotIds = appState.selectedCardPlaces.map(function (p) { return p.id; });
849:                 var groupNum = (appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || []).length + 1;
850:                 createSlotGroup('Group ' + groupNum, slotIds);
851:                 appState.selectedCardPlaces = [];
852:                 renderCardPlaceMarkers();
853:                 updateGroupPanelVisibility();
854:             }
855:         });

865:     helpModalOverlay = helpModal ? helpModal.querySelector('.help-modal-overlay') : null;
866:     const btnHelp = document.getElementById('btn-help');
867:     if (btnHelp) btnHelp.addEventListener('click', showHelpModal);
868:     if (closeHelpBtn) closeHelpBtn.addEventListener('click', hideHelpModal);
869:     if (helpModalOverlay) helpModalOverlay.addEventListener('click', hideHelpModal);

878:     if (ctxFlipAniBtn) ctxFlipAniBtn.addEventListener('click', handleFlipAni);
879:     if (ctxSlamBtn) ctxSlamBtn.addEventListener('click', toggleCtxSlam);
880:     if (ctxSpinBtn) ctxSpinBtn.addEventListener('click', toggleCtxSpin);
881:     if (ctxFlipAllBtn) ctxFlipAllBtn.addEventListener('click', toggleCtxFlipAll);
882:     if (ctxSlamAllBtn) ctxSlamAllBtn.addEventListener('click', toggleCtxSlamAll);
883:     if (ctxSpinAllBtn) ctxSpinAllBtn.addEventListener('click', toggleCtxSpinAll);
884:     setupCtxMenuDrag();
885:

887:     var showCtxToggle = document.getElementById('showContextMenuToggle');
888:     if (showCtxToggle) {
889:         showCtxToggle.addEventListener('change', function () {
890:             if (!this.checked) {
891:                 hideCardContextMenu();
892:             } else if (appState.selectedCard) {
893:                 showCardContextMenu(appState.selectedCard);
894:             }
895:         });
896:     }

906:         if (e.target === cardArea) {
907:             deselectCard();
908:         }
909:     });
910:

912:     if (slotFillAutoBtn) slotFillAutoBtn.addEventListener('click', fillSlotsAuto);
913:     if (slotFillManualBtn) slotFillManualBtn.addEventListener('click', showManualFillOverlay);
914:     if (manualFillConfirm) manualFillConfirm.addEventListener('click', executeManualFill);
915:     if (manualFillCancel) manualFillCancel.addEventListener('click', hideManualFillOverlay);
916:     if (manualFillInput) {
917:         manualFillInput.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
918:             if (e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); executeManualFill(); }
919:             if (e.key === 'Escape') { e.preventDefault(); hideManualFillOverlay(); }
920:         });
921:     }
922:     // Click outside slot context menu to close it
923:     document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
924:         if (slotContextMenu && !slotContextMenu.classList.contains('hidden')) {
925:             if (!slotContextMenu.contains(e.target)) {
926:                 hideSlotContextMenu();
927:             }
928:         }
929:     });
930:     // Click on overlay background to close manual fill
931:     if (manualFillOverlay) {
932:         manualFillOverlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
933:             if (e.target === manualFillOverlay) hideManualFillOverlay();
934:         });
935:     }
936:     // Escape key to close all slot fill UI
937:     document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
938:         if (e.key === 'Escape') {
939:             if (manualFillOverlay && !manualFillOverlay.classList.contains('hidden')) {
940:                 hideManualFillOverlay();
941:             } else if (slotContextMenu && !slotContextMenu.classList.contains('hidden')) {
942:                 hideSlotContextMenu();
943:                 clearDropZoneSelection();
944:             }
945:         }
946:     });
947:

949:     if (toggleDebugBtn) toggleDebugBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
950:         debugOverlay.classList.toggle('hidden');
951:     });
952:     if (copyDebugBtn) copyDebugBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
953:         const textToCopy = debugLogs.join('\n');
954:         // Try modern clipboard API first
955:         if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText) {
956:             navigator.clipboard.writeText(textToCopy).then(() => {
957:                 setStatus('Debug log copied to clipboard!', 'success');
958:             }).catch(() => {
959:                 // Fallback: use textarea method
960:                 fallbackCopyText(textToCopy);
961:             });
962:         } else {
963:             // Fallback for CEP environment
964:             fallbackCopyText(textToCopy);
965:         }
966:     });
967: 
968:     if (clearDebugBtn) clearDebugBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
969:         debugLogs = [];
970:         if (debugContent) debugContent.textContent = '';
971:     });
972:     if (closeDebugBtn) closeDebugBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
973:         debugOverlay.classList.add('hidden');
974:     });

978:     if (autoRecordToggle) autoRecordToggle.addEventListener('change', handleAutoRecordChange);
979:     if (autoRecordDelay) autoRecordDelay.addEventListener('input', handleAutoRecordDelayChange);
980:     if (cancelCountdownBtn) cancelCountdownBtn.addEventListener('click', cancelAutoRecordCountdown);

990:

993: }

997: // PHASE MANAGEMENT

1000: function setPhase(phase) {
1001:     appState.phase = phase;
1002: 
1003:     // Reset all phase button states
1004:     boardSettingBtn.classList.remove('active');
1005:     setupPhaseBtn.classList.remove('active');
1006:     recordPhaseBtn.classList.remove('active');
1007:     modeBadge.classList.remove('recording', 'board-setting');
1008: 
1009:     // Hide all phase-specific sections
1010:     if (boardSettingSection) boardSettingSection.classList.remove('visible');
1011:     if (boardLayoutInfo) boardLayoutInfo.classList.remove('visible');
1012:     if (stepControlsSection) stepControlsSection.classList.add('hidden');
1013:     gameContainer.classList.remove('board-setting-mode');
1014:     // Auto-save board layout when leaving board-setting phase
1015:     if (document.body.classList.contains('phase-board-setting')) {
1016:         autoSaveBoardLayout();
1017:     }
1018:     document.body.classList.remove('phase-board-setting');
1019:     document.body.classList.remove('phase-setup');
1020:     clearCardDropZones(); // Clear drop zones when switching phases
1021:     clearDropZoneSelection();
1022:     hideSlotContextMenu();
1023:     hideManualFillOverlay();
1024: 
1025:     // Toggle card tray disabled state
1026:     var cardTrayPanel = document.getElementById('cardTrayPanel');
1027:     if (cardTrayPanel) {
1028:         if (phase === 'board-setting') {
1029:             cardTrayPanel.classList.add('tray-disabled');
1030:         } else {
1031:             cardTrayPanel.classList.remove('tray-disabled');
1032:         }
1033:     }
1034:     // Hide recording indicator and border
1035:     const recIndicator = document.getElementById('recordingIndicator');
1036:     if (recIndicator) recIndicator.classList.add('hidden');
1037:     const gameWrapper = document.querySelector('.game-container-wrapper');
1038:     if (gameWrapper) gameWrapper.classList.remove('recording-mode');
1039:     // Note: Don't remove grid-mode here - preserve it across phases
1040: 
1041:     if (phase === 'board-setting') {
1042:         boardSettingBtn.classList.add('active');
1043:         modeBadge.textContent = 'BOARD';
1044:         modeBadge.classList.add('board-setting');
1045:         if (boardSettingSection) boardSettingSection.classList.add('visible');
1046:         gameContainer.classList.add('board-setting-mode');
1047:         document.body.classList.add('phase-board-setting');
1048: 
1049:         // Add grid-mode if layout type is grid
1050:         if (appState.boardLayout.type === 'grid') {
1051:             gameContainer.classList.add('grid-mode');
1052:         } else {
1053:             gameContainer.classList.remove('grid-mode');
1054:         }
1055: 
1056:         // Render card place markers
1057:         renderCardPlaceMarkers();
1058:         
1059:         // Restore visual cards
1060:         appState.tableCards.forEach(card => {
1061:             if (card.zone && card.zone.startsWith('grid-')) {
1062:                 const placeId = card.zone.replace('grid-', '');
1063:                 const zoneElement = document.querySelector(`.card-place-marker[data-place-id="${placeId}"]`);
1064:                 if (zoneElement) createZoneCardElement(card, zoneElement);
1065:             }
1066:         });
1067: 
1068:         updateDealingSlotButton();
1069:         updateGroupPanelVisibility();
1070:         setStatus('Board Setting - Customize card positions');
1071:     } else if (phase === 'setup') {
1072:         setupPhaseBtn.classList.add('active');
1073:         modeBadge.textContent = 'SETUP';
1074:         document.body.classList.add('phase-setup');
1075: 
1076:         // Show board layout info (remove record-mode to show Edit button)
1077:         if (boardLayoutInfo) {
1078:             boardLayoutInfo.classList.add('visible');
1079:             boardLayoutInfo.classList.remove('record-mode');
1080:         }
1081:         updateLayoutInfoDisplay();
1082: 
1083:         // Clear editable markers, render drop zones instead
1084:         clearCardPlaceMarkers();
1085: 
1086:         // Render card drop zones universally in setup
1087:         if (appState.boardLayout.type === 'grid') {
1088:             gameContainer.classList.add('grid-mode');
1089:         } else {
1090:             gameContainer.classList.remove('grid-mode');
1091:         }
1092:         
1093:         renderCardDropZones();
1094:         // Restore visual cards
1095:         appState.tableCards.forEach(card => {
1096:             const zoneElement = document.querySelector(`.card-drop-zone[data-zone="${card.zone}"]`);
1097:             if (zoneElement) createZoneCardElement(card, zoneElement);
1098:         });
1099:         
1100:         if (typeof hideTransformIndicator === 'function') hideTransformIndicator();
1101: 
1102:         setStatus('Setup - Drag cards to the table');
1103:     } else if (phase === 'record') {
1104:         recordPhaseBtn.classList.add('active');
1105:         modeBadge.textContent = 'RECORD';
1106:         modeBadge.classList.add('recording');
1107:         if (stepControlsSection) stepControlsSection.classList.remove('hidden');
1108: 
1109:         // Show board layout info (add record-mode to hide Edit button)
1110:         if (boardLayoutInfo) {
1111:             boardLayoutInfo.classList.add('visible');
1112:             boardLayoutInfo.classList.add('record-mode');
1113:         }
1114:         updateLayoutInfoDisplay();
1115: 
1116:         // Clear card place markers
1117:         clearCardPlaceMarkers();
1118: 
1119:         // Render card drop zones universally in record mode
1120:         if (appState.boardLayout.type === 'grid') {
1121:             gameContainer.classList.add('grid-mode');
1122:         } else {
1123:             gameContainer.classList.remove('grid-mode');
1124:         }
1125:         
1126:         renderCardDropZones();
1127:         // Restore visual cards
1128:         appState.tableCards.forEach(card => {
1129:             const zoneElement = document.querySelector(`.card-drop-zone[data-zone="${card.zone}"]`);
1130:             if (zoneElement) createZoneCardElement(card, zoneElement);
1131:         });
1132: 
1133:         // Save initial state when entering record phase
1134:         saveInitialState();
1135: 
1136:         // Show recording indicator and border
1137:         const recIndicator = document.getElementById('recordingIndicator');
1138:         if (recIndicator) recIndicator.classList.remove('hidden');
1139:         const gameWrapper = document.querySelector('.game-container-wrapper');
1140:         if (gameWrapper) gameWrapper.classList.add('recording-mode');
1141: 
1142:         setStatus('Record - Create animation steps');
1143:         updateGroupOrderSectionVisibility();
1144:     }
1145: 
1146:     // Update grouping section visibility
1147:     updateGroupingSectionVisibility();
1148: 
1149:     updateUI();
1150: }
1151: 
1152: /**
1153:  * Update the layout info display in setup/record modes
1154:  */
1155: function updateLayoutInfoDisplay() {
1156:     if (currentLayoutName) {
1157:         currentLayoutName.textContent = appState.boardLayout.name || 'Poker (4 Players)';
1158:     }
1159: 
1160:     // Toggle flip controls visibility based on layout type
1161:     updateFlipControlsVisibility();
1162: }
1163: 
1164: /**
1165:  * Update flip controls visibility based on board layout type
1166:  */
1167: function updateFlipControlsVisibility() {
1168:     if (appState.boardLayout.type === 'grid' && appState.boardLayout.boardStyle !== 'poker') {
1169:         // Non-poker grid (Pusoy, card-sorting): show grid controls, hide poker controls
1170:         if (pokerFlipControls) pokerFlipControls.classList.add('hidden');
1171:         if (gridFlipControls) gridFlipControls.classList.remove('hidden');
1172:     } else {
1173:         // Poker (including poker-grid) or legacy: show poker controls, hide grid controls
1174:         if (pokerFlipControls) pokerFlipControls.classList.remove('hidden');
1175:         if (gridFlipControls) gridFlipControls.classList.add('hidden');
1176:     }
1177: }
1178: 
1179: /**
1180:  * Flip all table cards face up or face down
1181:  */
1182: function handleFlipAllCards(faceUp) {
1183:     appState.tableCards.forEach(card => {
1184:         card.isFaceUp = faceUp;
1185:         // Update visual representation
1186:         const cardEl = document.querySelector(`.card[data-card-id="${card.id}"]`);
1187:         if (cardEl) {
1188:             if (faceUp) {
1189:                 cardEl.classList.add('face-up');
1190:             } else {
1191:                 cardEl.classList.remove('face-up');
1192:             }
1193:             // Update card image
1194:             const img = cardEl.querySelector('img');
1195:             if (img) {
1196:                 img.src = faceUp ? (card.frontImageUrl || '') : (card.backImageUrl || '');
1197:             }
1198:         }
1199:     });
1200: 
1201:     setStatus(faceUp ? 'All cards flipped face up' : 'All cards flipped face down');
1202:     updateUI();
1203: }
1204: 
1205: // ============================================
1206: // DECK LOADING
1207: // ============================================
1208: 
1209: /**
1210:  * Scan the assets/decks folder and populate the deck dropdown
1211:  */
1212: function scanAndPopulateDecks() {
1213:     // Browser mode - create placeholder cards
1214:     if (!csInterface) {
1215:         createPlaceholderDeck();
1216:         return;
1217:     }
1218: 
1219:     // CEP mode - get extension path
1220:     const extPath = csInterface.getSystemPath(SystemPath.EXTENSION);
1221:     const decksFolder = extPath + '/assets/decks';
1222: 
1223:     if (!fs || !fs.existsSync(decksFolder)) {
1224:         setStatus('Decks folder not found. Use Load button to select a deck folder.');
1225:         createPlaceholderDeck();
1226:         return;
1227:     }
1228: 
1229:     try {
1230:         // Scan for subdirectories in decks folder
1231:         const items = fs.readdirSync(decksFolder);
1232:         const deckFolders = items.filter(item => {
1233:             const itemPath = decksFolder + '/' + item;
1234:             // Check if it's a directory and not a file like README.md
1235:             return fs.statSync(itemPath).isDirectory();
1236:         });
1237: 
1238:         if (deckFolders.length === 0) {
1239:             setStatus('No deck folders found in assets/decks/');
1240:             createPlaceholderDeck();
1241:             return;
1242:         }
1243: 
1244:         // Clear and populate dropdown
1245:         deckSelect.innerHTML = '';
1246:         deckFolders.forEach((folder, index) => {
1247:             const option = document.createElement('option');
1248:             option.value = decksFolder + '/' + folder;
1249:             // Capitalize folder name for display
1250:             option.textContent = folder.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + folder.slice(1);
1251:             deckSelect.appendChild(option);
1252:         });
1253: 
1254:         // Store decks folder path for later use
1255:         appState.decksFolder = decksFolder;
1256: 
1257:         // Auto-load the first deck
1258:         const firstDeckPath = decksFolder + '/' + deckFolders[0];
1259:         loadDeckFromPath(firstDeckPath);
1260: 
1261:         console.log(`Found ${deckFolders.length} deck(s): ${deckFolders.join(', ')}`);
1262: 
1263:     } catch (e) {
1264:         console.error('Error scanning decks folder:', e);
1265:         setStatus('Error scanning decks: ' + e.message, 'error');
1266:         createPlaceholderDeck();
1267:     }
1268: }
1269: 
1270: /**
1271:  * Handle deck selection change from dropdown
1272:  */
1273: function handleDeckSelectChange() {
1274:     const selectedPath = deckSelect.value;
1275:     if (selectedPath) {
1276:         // Reset table before loading new deck
1277:         handleResetTable();
1278:         loadDeckFromPath(selectedPath);
1279:     }
1280: }
1281: 
1282: 
1283: function handleLoadDeck() {
1284:     // Use CEP folder dialog if available
1285:     if (typeof window.cep !== 'undefined' && window.cep.fs) {
1286:         try {
1287:             const result = window.cep.fs.showOpenDialogEx(
1288:                 false,    // allowMultipleSelection
1289:                 true,     // chooseDirectory
1290:                 'Select Deck Folder',
1291:                 '',       // initialPath
1292:                 []        // fileTypes
1293:             );
1294: 
1295:             if (result.err === 0 && result.data && result.data.length > 0) {
1296:                 loadDeckFromPath(result.data[0]);
1297:             }
1298:         } catch (e) {
1299:             console.error('Error opening folder dialog:', e);
1300:             setStatus('Error selecting folder', 'error');
1301:         }
1302:     } else {
1303:         // Browser fallback - use file input
1304:         const input = document.createElement('input');
1305:         input.type = 'file';
1306:         input.webkitdirectory = true;
1307:         input.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
1308:             if (e.target.files.length > 0) {
1309:                 loadDeckFromFiles(e.target.files);
1310:             }
1311:         });
1312:         input.click();
1313:     }
1314: }
1315: 
1316: function loadDeckFromPath(folderPath) {
1317:     if (!fs) {
1318:         setStatus('File system not available', 'error');
1319:         return;
1320:     }
1321: 
1322:     try {
1323:         const files = fs.readdirSync(folderPath);
1324:         const imageFiles = files.filter(f => /\.(png|jpg|jpeg|gif|webp)$/i.test(f));
1325: 
1326:         if (imageFiles.length === 0) {
1327:             setStatus('No image files found in folder', 'error');
1328:             return;
1329:         }
1330: 
1331:         // Find back.png
1332:         const backFile = imageFiles.find(f => f.toLowerCase() === 'back.png');
1333:         if (backFile) {
1334:             appState.backImagePath = folderPath + '/' + backFile;
1335:         }
1336: 
1337:         // Store deck path
1338:         appState.deckPath = folderPath;
1339:         appState.assetsRootPath = folderPath + '/';
1340: 
1341:         // Create card data for each image (except back.png)
1342:         const cardFiles = imageFiles.filter(f => f.toLowerCase() !== 'back.png');
1343: 
1344:         appState.trayCards = cardFiles.map((filename, index) => {
1345:             const baseName = filename.replace(/\.[^.]+$/, '');
1346:             return createCardData(index, filename, baseName, folderPath);
1347:         });
1348: 
1349:         renderCardTray();
1350:         updateAssetsDisplay();
1351:         setStatus(`Loaded ${appState.trayCards.length} cards from deck`, 'success');
1352:         // Enable AI button once deck is loaded
1353:         enableAIButton();
1354: 
1355:     } catch (e) {
1356:         console.error('Error loading deck:', e);
1357:         setStatus('Error loading deck: ' + e.message, 'error');
1358:     }
1359: }
1360: 
1361: function loadDeckFromFiles(files) {
1362:     const imageFiles = Array.from(files).filter(f =>
1363:         /\.(png|jpg|jpeg|gif|webp)$/i.test(f.name)
1364:     );
1365: 
1366:     if (imageFiles.length === 0) {
1367:         setStatus('No image files found', 'error');
1368:         return;
1369:     }
1370: 
1371:     // Find back.png
1372:     const backFile = imageFiles.find(f => f.name.toLowerCase() === 'back.png');
1373:     if (backFile) {
1374:         appState.backImagePath = URL.createObjectURL(backFile);
1375:     }
1376: 
1377:     // Get folder path from first file
1378:     if (nodePath && imageFiles[0].path) {
1379:         appState.deckPath = nodePath.dirname(imageFiles[0].path);
1380:         appState.assetsRootPath = appState.deckPath + '/';
1381:     }
1382: 
1383:     // Create card data
1384:     const cardFiles = imageFiles.filter(f => f.name.toLowerCase() !== 'back.png');
1385: 
1386:     appState.trayCards = cardFiles.map((file, index) => {
1387:         const baseName = file.name.replace(/\.[^.]+$/, '');
1388:         return {
1389:             id: `card-${index}-${baseName.replace(/\s+/g, '_')}`,
1390:             name: baseName,
1391:             filename: file.name,
1392:             frontImageUrl: URL.createObjectURL(file),
1393:             backImageUrl: appState.backImagePath || '',
1394:             isFaceUp: false,
1395:             inTray: true
1396:         };
1397:     });
1398: 
1399:     renderCardTray();
1400:     updateAssetsDisplay();
1401:     setStatus(`Loaded ${appState.trayCards.length} cards`, 'success');
1402:     enableAIButton();
1403: }
1404: 
1405: function createPlaceholderDeck() {
1406:     // Create 52 placeholder cards for browser testing
1407:     appState.trayCards = [];
1408:     let index = 0;
1409: 
1410:     for (const suit of SUITS) {
1411:         for (const rank of RANKS) {
1412:             const name = `${rank}_${suit}`;
1413:             appState.trayCards.push({
1414:                 id: `card-${index}-${name}`,
1415:                 name: name,
1416:                 displayName: `${rank.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + rank.slice(1)} of ${suit}`,
1417:                 filename: `${name}.png`,
1418:                 frontImageUrl: '',  // Will show placeholder
1419:                 backImageUrl: '',
1420:                 suit: suit,
1421:                 rank: rank,
1422:                 isFaceUp: false,
1423:                 inTray: true
1424:             });
1425:             index++;
1426:         }
1427:     }
1428: 
1429:     // Add Joker cards
1430:     const jokers = [
1431:         { name: 'joker_black', displayName: 'Black Joker', color: 'black' },
1432:         { name: 'joker_red', displayName: 'Red Joker', color: 'red' }
1433:     ];
1434:     for (const j of jokers) {
1435:         appState.trayCards.push({
1436:             id: `card-${index}-${j.name}`,
1437:             name: j.name,
1438:             displayName: j.displayName,
1439:             filename: `${j.name}.png`,
1440:             frontImageUrl: '',
1441:             backImageUrl: '',
1442:             suit: 'joker',
1443:             rank: 'joker',
1444:             jokerColor: j.color,
1445:             isFaceUp: false,
1446:             inTray: true
1447:         });
1448:         index++;
1449:     }
1450: 
1451:     renderCardTray();
1452:     enableAIButton();
1453: }
1454: 
1455: function createCardData(index, filename, baseName, folderPath) {
1456:     // Check if this is a Joker card
1457:     const lowerName = baseName.toLowerCase();
1458:     if (lowerName.includes('joker')) {
1459:         const isRed = lowerName.includes('red');
1460:         return {
1461:             id: `card-${index}-${baseName.replace(/\s+/g, '_')}`,
1462:             name: baseName,
1463:             displayName: isRed ? 'Red Joker' : 'Black Joker',
1464:             filename: filename,
1465:             frontImageUrl: `file://${folderPath}/${filename}`,
1466:             backImageUrl: appState.backImagePath ? `file://${appState.backImagePath}` : '',
1467:             suit: 'joker',
1468:             rank: 'joker',
1469:             jokerColor: isRed ? 'red' : 'black',
1470:             isFaceUp: false,
1471:             inTray: true
1472:         };
1473:     }
1474: 
1475:     // Try to parse suit from filename
1476:     let suit = 'unknown';
1477:     let rank = baseName;
1478: 
1479:     for (const s of SUITS) {
1480:         if (baseName.toLowerCase().includes(s)) {
1481:             suit = s;
1482:             rank = baseName.toLowerCase().replace(s, '').replace(/[_-]/g, '').trim();
1483:             break;
1484:         }
1485:     }
1486: 
1487:     return {
1488:         id: `card-${index}-${baseName.replace(/\s+/g, '_')}`,
1489:         name: baseName,
1490:         displayName: baseName.replace(/[_-]/g, ' '),
1491:         filename: filename,
1492:         frontImageUrl: `file://${folderPath}/${filename}`,
1493:         backImageUrl: appState.backImagePath ? `file://${appState.backImagePath}` : '',
1494:         suit: suit,
1495:         rank: rank,
1496:         isFaceUp: false,
1497:         inTray: true
1498:     };
1499: }
1500: 
1501: // ============================================
1502: // CARD TRAY
1503: // ============================================
1504: 
1505: function renderCardTray() {
1506:     cardTrayList.innerHTML = '';
1507: 
1508:     const cardsToShow = getFilteredTrayCards();
1509: 
1510:     if (cardsToShow.length === 0) {
1511:         cardTrayList.innerHTML = '<div class="tray-loading"><p>No cards match filter</p></div>';
1512:         return;
1513:     }
1514: 
1515:     cardsToShow.forEach(card => {
1516:         const cardEl = createTrayCardElement(card);
1517:         cardTrayList.appendChild(cardEl);
1518:     });
1519: 
1520:     trayCardCount.textContent = appState.trayCards.filter(c => c.inTray).length;
1521: }
1522: 
1523: function createTrayCardElement(card) {
1524:     const el = document.createElement('div');
1525:     el.className = 'tray-card';
1526:     el.dataset.cardId = card.id;
1527:     el.draggable = true;
1528: 
1529:     // Card image
1530:     const img = document.createElement('img');
1531:     if (card.frontImageUrl) {
1532:         img.src = card.frontImageUrl;
1533:     } else {
1534:         // Placeholder with suit symbol
1535:         img.src = createPlaceholderCardImage(card);
1536:     }
1537:     img.alt = card.name;
1538:     el.appendChild(img);
1539: 
1540:     // Card name
1541:     const nameEl = document.createElement('div');
1542:     nameEl.className = 'card-name';
1543:     nameEl.textContent = card.displayName || card.name;
1544:     el.appendChild(nameEl);
1545: 
1546:     // Drag events
1547:     el.addEventListener('dragstart', (e) => handleTrayCardDragStart(e, card));
1548:     el.addEventListener('dragend', handleTrayCardDragEnd);
1549: 
1550:     return el;
1551: }
1552: 
1553: function createPlaceholderCardImage(card) {
1554:     // Create simple SVG placeholder
1555:     const suitSymbols = {
1556:         spades: '♠',
1557:         hearts: '♥',
1558:         diamonds: '♦',
1559:         clubs: '♣',
1560:         joker: '🃏',
1561:         unknown: '?'
1562:     };
1563:     const suitColors = {
1564:         spades: '#2c3e50',
1565:         hearts: '#e74c3c',
1566:         diamonds: '#e74c3c',
1567:         clubs: '#2c3e50',
1568:         joker: card.jokerColor === 'red' ? '#e74c3c' : '#2c3e50',
1569:         unknown: '#666'
1570:     };
1571: 
1572:     const symbol = suitSymbols[card.suit] || '?';
1573:     const color = suitColors[card.suit] || '#666';
1574:     const rankDisplay = card.suit === 'joker' ? 'J' : (card.rank ? card.rank.charAt(0).toUpperCase() : '?');
1575: 
1576:     const svg = `
1577:         <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="40" height="56" viewBox="0 0 40 56">
1578:             <rect width="40" height="56" fill="white" rx="3"/>
1579:             <text x="5" y="15" font-size="12" fill="${color}">${rankDisplay}</text>
1580:             <text x="20" y="35" font-size="18" text-anchor="middle" fill="${color}">${symbol}</text>
1581:         </svg>
1582:     `;
1583:     return 'data:image/svg+xml,' + encodeURIComponent(svg);
1584: }
1585: 
1586: function getFilteredTrayCards() {
1587:     const searchTerm = cardSearch.value.toLowerCase();
1588:     const activeFilter = document.querySelector('.suit-btn.active');
1589:     const suitFilter = activeFilter ? activeFilter.dataset.suit : 'all';
1590: 
1591:     return appState.trayCards.filter(card => {
1592:         if (!card.inTray) return false;
1593: 
1594:         // Search filter — supports comma-separated terms (e.g. "10,ace,king")
1595:         if (searchTerm) {
1596:             var searchTerms = searchTerm.split(',').map(function (t) { return t.trim(); }).filter(function (t) { return t.length > 0; });
1597:             var matchesAny = searchTerms.some(function (term) {
1598:                 return card.name.toLowerCase().includes(term);
1599:             });
1600:             if (!matchesAny) return false;
1601:         }
1602: 
1603:         // Suit filter
1604:         if (suitFilter !== 'all' && card.suit !== suitFilter) {
1605:             return false;
1606:         }
1607: 
1608:         return true;
1609:     });
1610: }
1611: 
1612: function filterTrayCards() {
1613:     renderCardTray();
1614: }
1615: 
1616: function handleSuitFilter(btn) {
1617:     suitFilterBtns.forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
1618:     btn.classList.add('active');
1619:     renderCardTray();
1620: }
1621: 
1622: // ============================================
1623: // DRAG & DROP FROM TRAY
1624: // ============================================
1625: 
1626: function handleTrayCardDragStart(e, card) {
1627:     // Block dragging from tray during board-setting phase
1628:     if (appState.phase === 'board-setting') {
1629:         e.preventDefault();
1630:         return;
1631:     }
1632:     e.dataTransfer.setData('text/plain', card.id);
1633:     e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
1634:     e.target.classList.add('dragging');
1635: 
1636:     // Highlight drop zones (both player zones and grid drop zones)
1637:     playerZones.forEach(zone => zone.classList.add('drag-target'));
1638:     document.querySelectorAll('.card-drop-zone').forEach(zone => zone.classList.add('drag-target'));
1639: }
1640: 
1641: function handleTrayCardDragEnd(e) {
1642:     e.target.classList.remove('dragging');
1643:     playerZones.forEach(zone => zone.classList.remove('drag-target', 'drag-over'));
1644:     document.querySelectorAll('.card-drop-zone').forEach(zone => zone.classList.remove('drag-target', 'drag-over'));
1645: }
1646: 
1647: function setupZoneDropTargets() {
1648:     // Setup player zones (for poker layout)
1649:     playerZones.forEach(zone => {
1650:         zone.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
1651:             e.preventDefault();
1652:             e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move';
1653:             zone.classList.add('drag-over');
1654:         });
1655: 
1656:         zone.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
1657:             zone.classList.remove('drag-over');
1658:         });
1659: 
1660:         zone.addEventListener('drop', (e) => handleZoneDrop(e, zone));
1661:     });
1662: 
1663:     // Setup grid drop zones (for grid layout) - handled dynamically in renderCardDropZones
1664:     // Note: Grid zones are created dynamically when entering setup mode
1665: }
1666: 
1667: function handleZoneDrop(e, zone) {
1668:     e.preventDefault();
1669:     zone.classList.remove('drag-over');
1670: 
1671:     const cardId = e.dataTransfer.getData('text/plain');
1672:     console.log('[ZoneDrop] cardId:', cardId, 'groupingMode:', appState.groupingMode, 'groupedCards:', appState.groupedCards.map(c => c.id));
1673: 
1674:     // Check if the dragged card is part of a group - move all grouped cards
1675:     const droppedCard = appState.tableCards.find(c => c.id === cardId);
1676:     const isInGroup = droppedCard && appState.groupedCards.some(c => c.id === cardId);
1677:     console.log('[ZoneDrop] droppedCard found:', !!droppedCard, 'isInGroup:', isInGroup);
1678: 
1679:     if (droppedCard && appState.groupingMode && isInGroup) {
1680:         console.log('[ZoneDrop] Routing to handleGroupedCardsDrop');
1681:         handleGroupedCardsDrop(zone);
1682:         return;
1683:     }
1684: 
1685:     // Try to find card in tray first
1686:     let card = appState.trayCards.find(c => c.id === cardId);
1687:     const fromTray = card && card.inTray;
1688: 
1689:     // If not in tray, look for it in table cards (for moving between zones)
1690:     if (!fromTray) {
1691:         card = appState.tableCards.find(c => c.id === cardId);
1692:         if (!card) return;
1693:     }
1694: 
1695:     // Get zone info
1696:     const zoneName = zone.dataset.zone;
1697:     const rotation = parseInt(zone.dataset.rotation) || 0;
1698: 
1699:     // Check if this is a grid zone with existing cards (for swap/stack logic)
1700:     // Community zones always accept multi-card, skip swap/stack popup
1701:     if (zoneName.startsWith('grid-') && appState.phase === 'record') {
1702:         const placeId = zoneName.replace('grid-', '');
1703:         const place = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.find(p => p.id === placeId);
1704:         const isCZ = place && place.isCommunityZone;
1705: 
1706:         if (!isCZ) {
1707:             const existingCards = appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.zone === zoneName && c.id !== cardId);
1708:             if (existingCards.length > 0 && !fromTray) {
1709:                 // Show swap/stack popup for grid zones with existing cards
1710:                 showSwapStackPopup(card, existingCards[0], zoneName, rotation, zone);
1711:                 return;
1712:             }
1713:         }
1714:     }
1715: 
1716:     if (fromTray) {
1717:         // From tray - place new card in zone
1718:         placeCardInZone(card, zoneName, rotation, zone);
1719:     } else {
1720:         // Moving card between zones (Record mode)
1721:         moveCardToZone(card, zoneName, rotation, zone);
1722:     }
1723: }
1724: 
1725: /**
1726:  * Show popup to choose between swap or stack when dropping card on occupied grid zone
1727:  */
1728: function showSwapStackPopup(movingCard, existingCard, zoneName, rotation, zoneElement) {
1729:     // Remove any existing popup
1730:     const oldPopup = document.querySelector('.swap-stack-popup');
1731:     if (oldPopup) oldPopup.remove();
1732: 
1733:     const popup = document.createElement('div');
1734:     popup.className = 'swap-stack-popup';
1735:     popup.innerHTML = `
1736:         <div class="popup-title">Zone has a card</div>
1737:         <div class="popup-buttons">
1738:             <button class="btn btn-sm btn-swap" title="Swap positions with existing card">🔄 Swap</button>
1739:             <button class="btn btn-sm btn-stack" title="Stack on top of existing card">📚 Stack</button>
1740:             <button class="btn btn-sm btn-cancel">✕</button>
1741:         </div>
1742:     `;
1743: 
1744:     // Position near the zone — use fixed coords (popup appended to body)
1745:     const zoneRect = zoneElement.getBoundingClientRect();
1746:     popup.style.left = `${zoneRect.left + zoneRect.width / 2}px`;
1747:     popup.style.top = `${zoneRect.top - 50}px`;
1748: 
1749:     // Event handlers
1750:     popup.querySelector('.btn-swap').addEventListener('click', () => {
1751:         popup.remove();
1752:         swapCards(movingCard, existingCard);
1753:     });
1754: 
1755:     popup.querySelector('.btn-stack').addEventListener('click', () => {
1756:         popup.remove();
1757:         moveCardToZone(movingCard, zoneName, rotation, zoneElement);
1758:     });
1759: 
1760:     popup.querySelector('.btn-cancel').addEventListener('click', () => {
1761:         popup.remove();
1762:     });
1763: 
1764:     document.body.appendChild(popup);
1765: }
1766: 
1767: /**
1768:  * Swap two cards between their zones (used in Record mode for grid)
1769:  */
1770: function swapCards(card1, card2) {
1771:     // Take snapshot BEFORE the swap
1772:     const snapshotBeforeSwap = (appState.phase === 'record' && !appState.isEditingStep) ? takeSnapshot() : null;
1773: 
1774:     // Store original positions
1775:     const zone1 = card1.zone;
1776:     const zone2 = card2.zone;
1777:     const pos1 = card1.zonePosition;
1778:     const pos2 = card2.zonePosition;
1779: 
1780:     // Remove card elements
1781:     if (card1.element) card1.element.remove();
1782:     if (card2.element) card2.element.remove();
1783: 
1784:     // Find zone elements and get their rotation values
1785:     const zone1Element = document.querySelector(`.card-drop-zone[data-zone="${zone1}"], .player-zone[data-zone="${zone1}"]`);
1786:     const zone2Element = document.querySelector(`.card-drop-zone[data-zone="${zone2}"], .player-zone[data-zone="${zone2}"]`);
1787: 
1788:     // Get rotation from zone data attributes (for Pusoy and other rotated layouts)
1789:     const rotation1 = parseInt(zone1Element?.dataset?.rotation) || 0;
1790:     const rotation2 = parseInt(zone2Element?.dataset?.rotation) || 0;
1791: 
1792:     // Swap zone assignments AND update rotation to match destination zone
1793:     card1.zone = zone2;
1794:     card1.zonePosition = pos2;
1795:     card1.rotation = rotation2;  // Card1 inherits rotation of zone2
1796: 
1797:     card2.zone = zone1;
1798:     card2.zonePosition = pos1;
1799:     card2.rotation = rotation1;  // Card2 inherits rotation of zone1
1800: 
1801:     if (zone1Element) createZoneCardElement(card2, zone1Element);
1802:     if (zone2Element) createZoneCardElement(card1, zone2Element);
1803: 
1804:     // Mark as having changes for recording
1805:     card1.hasChanges = true;
1806:     card2.hasChanges = true;
1807: 
1808:     updateUI();
1809:     setStatus(`Swapped ${card1.displayName || card1.name} with ${card2.displayName || card2.name}`);
1810: 
1811:     // Show auto-step popup if in Record mode
1812:     if (snapshotBeforeSwap && appState.phase === 'record' && !appState.isEditingStep) {
1813:         selectCard(card1);
1814:         showAutoStepPopup(card1, snapshotBeforeSwap);
1815:     }
1816: }
1817: 
1818: /**
1819:  * Move a card from one zone to another (used in Record mode)
1820:  */
1821: function moveCardToZone(card, newZoneName, newRotation, newZoneElement) {
1822:     // Take snapshot BEFORE the move for auto-step feature
1823:     const snapshotBeforeMove = (appState.phase === 'record' && !appState.isEditingStep) ? takeSnapshot() : null;
1824: 
1825:     // Remove card element from old zone
1826:     if (card.element) {
1827:         card.element.remove();
1828:     }
1829: 
1830:     // Update card properties
1831:     const oldZone = card.zone;
1832:     card.zone = newZoneName;
1833:     card.rotation = newRotation;
1834: 
1835:     // In Record mode with flipAction: start face-down, then animate flip
1836:     if (appState.phase === 'record' && card.flipAction) {
1837:         card.isFaceUp = false; // Start face-down for animation
1838:     }
1839:     // When moving cards between zones, PRESERVE the card's current face state.
1840:     // Face state is only set from zone flip checkbox during initial placement (placeCardInZone).
1841:     // Users control flipping explicitly via right-click > flip or the flip checkbox.
1842: 
1843:     // Recalculate zone positions for old zone (fill gaps)
1844:     if (oldZone && oldZone !== newZoneName) {
1845:         const oldZoneCards = appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.zone === oldZone && c.id !== card.id);
1846:         oldZoneCards.forEach((c, idx) => {
1847:             c.zonePosition = idx;
1848:         });
1849:         // Re-render old zone cards
1850:         const oldZoneElement = document.querySelector(`.player-zone[data-zone="${oldZone}"], .community-zone[data-zone="${oldZone}"]`);
1851:         if (oldZoneElement) {
1852:             rerenderZoneCards(oldZone, oldZoneElement);
1853:         }
1854:     }
1855: 
1856:     // Get new position in target zone
1857:     const newZoneCards = appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.zone === newZoneName && c.id !== card.id);
1858:     card.zonePosition = newZoneCards.length;
1859: 
1860:     // Community zone rotation is handled by createZoneCardElement for CZ slots
1861:     // Legacy poker community zone (HTML-based) random rotation:
1862:     if (appState.boardLayout.boardStyle === 'poker' && newZoneName === 'community' && !newZoneName.startsWith('grid-')) {
1863:         const randomCheckbox = document.getElementById('communityRandomRotation');
1864:         if (randomCheckbox && randomCheckbox.checked) {
1865:             card.rotation = Math.round((Math.random() - 0.5) * 30); // ±15°
1866:         }
1867:     }
1868: 
1869:     // Create visual card in new zone
1870:     createZoneCardElement(card, newZoneElement);
1871: 
1872:     // Animate flip after element is created (Record mode with flipAction)
1873:     if (appState.phase === 'record' && card.flipAction) {
1874:         setTimeout(() => {
1875:             flipCard(card);
1876:         }, 150); // Small delay for visual effect
1877:     }
1878: 
1879:     // Mark as having changes for recording
1880:     if (appState.phase === 'record') {
1881:         card.hasChanges = true;
1882:     }
1883: 
1884:     updateUI();
1885:     setStatus(`Moved ${card.displayName || card.name} to ${newZoneName} zone`);
1886: 
1887:     // Show auto-step popup in Record mode (if not manually editing a step)
1888:     if (snapshotBeforeMove && appState.phase === 'record' && !appState.isEditingStep) {
1889:         // Select the card so context menu appears next to it
1890:         selectCard(card);
1891:         showAutoStepPopup(card, snapshotBeforeMove);
1892:     }
1893: }
1894: 
1895: /**
1896:  * Re-render all cards in a zone (used after moving cards)
1897:  */
1898: function rerenderZoneCards(zoneName, zoneElement) {
1899:     const zoneCardsContainer = zoneElement.querySelector('.zone-cards');
1900:     if (!zoneCardsContainer) return;
1901: 
1902:     // Clear zone cards container
1903:     zoneCardsContainer.innerHTML = '';
1904: 
1905:     // Get all cards in this zone and re-create elements
1906:     const zoneCards = appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.zone === zoneName);
1907:     zoneCards.forEach(card => {
1908:         createZoneCardElement(card, zoneElement);
1909:     });
1910: }
1911: 
1912: 
1913: function placeCardInZone(card, zoneName, rotation, zoneElement) {
1914:     // Take snapshot BEFORE placing card (for auto-step feature)
1915:     const snapshotBeforePlace = (appState.phase === 'record' && !appState.isEditingStep && !appState._bulkApplying) ? takeSnapshot() : null;
1916: 
1917:     // Mark as not in tray
1918:     card.inTray = false;
1919:     card.zone = zoneName;
1920:     card.rotation = rotation;
1921: 
1922:     // Determine face up/down state based on layout type
1923:     if (zoneName.startsWith('grid-')) {
1924:         // Grid layout: check if poker-style (has parent zone flip controls)
1925:         if (appState.boardLayout.boardStyle === 'poker' && appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces) {
1926:             const placeId = zoneName.replace('grid-', '');
1927:             const place = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.find(p => p.id === placeId);
1928:             if (place && place.zone) {
1929:                 // Use the parent zone's flip checkbox (e.g. flipTop, flipBottom)
1930:                 const parentZone = place.zone;
1931:                 const flipCheckbox = document.querySelector(`#flip${parentZone.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + parentZone.slice(1)}`);
1932:                 card.isFaceUp = flipCheckbox ? flipCheckbox.checked : false;
1933:             } else {
1934:                 card.isFaceUp = gridDefaultFaceUp ? gridDefaultFaceUp.checked : false;
1935:             }
1936:         } else {
1937:             // Non-poker grid (Pusoy, etc): use gridDefaultFaceUp checkbox
1938:             card.isFaceUp = gridDefaultFaceUp ? gridDefaultFaceUp.checked : false;
1939:         }
1940:     } else {
1941:         // Legacy poker layout: use zone-specific checkbox
1942:         const flipCheckbox = document.querySelector(`#flip${zoneName.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + zoneName.slice(1)}`);
1943:         card.isFaceUp = flipCheckbox ? flipCheckbox.checked : false;
1944:     }
1945: 
1946:     // Get existing cards in zone
1947:     const zoneCards = appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.zone === zoneName);
1948:     const position = zoneCards.length;
1949: 
1950:     // Calculate overlap position
1951:     card.zonePosition = position;
1952: 
1953:     // Community zone rotation is handled by createZoneCardElement for CZ slots
1954:     // Legacy poker community zone (HTML-based) random rotation:
1955:     if (appState.boardLayout.boardStyle === 'poker' && zoneName === 'community' && !zoneName.startsWith('grid-')) {
1956:         const randomCheckbox = document.getElementById('communityRandomRotation');
1957:         if (randomCheckbox && randomCheckbox.checked) {
1958:             card.rotation = Math.round((Math.random() - 0.5) * 30); // ±15°
1959:         }
1960:     }
1961: 
1962:     // Add to table cards
1963:     appState.tableCards.push(card);
1964: 
1965:     // Create visual card in zone
1966:     createZoneCardElement(card, zoneElement);
1967: 
1968:     // Mark as having changes for recording
1969:     if (appState.phase === 'record') {
1970:         card.hasChanges = true;
1971:     }
1972: 
1973:     // Update tray (skip during bulk AI apply for performance)
1974:     if (!appState._bulkApplying) {
1975:         renderCardTray();
1976:         hideInstructions();
1977:         updateUI();
1978:         setStatus(`Placed ${card.displayName || card.name} in ${zoneName} zone`);
1979:     }
1980: 
1981:     // Show auto-step popup in Record mode (if not manually editing a step)
1982:     if (snapshotBeforePlace && appState.phase === 'record' && !appState.isEditingStep) {
1983:         selectCard(card);
1984:         showAutoStepPopup(card, snapshotBeforePlace);
1985:     }
1986: }
1987: 
1988: 
1989: function placeCardOnTable(card, x, y) {
1990:     card.inTray = false;
1991:     card.zone = 'table';
1992:     card.x = x;
1993:     card.y = y;
1994:     card.rotation = 0;
1995: 
1996:     appState.tableCards.push(card);
1997: 
1998:     createTableCardElement(card);
1999: 
2000:     renderCardTray();
2001:     hideInstructions();
2002:     updateUI();
2003: 
2004:     setStatus(`Placed ${card.displayName || card.name} on table`);
2005: }
2006: 
2007: /**
2008:  * Move an existing card to a new position on the table
2009:  * Used in Record mode to reposition cards from zones to free table area
2010:  */
2011: function moveCardToPosition(card, x, y) {
2012:     // Remove existing element
2013:     if (card.element) {
2014:         card.element.remove();
2015:     }
2016: 
2017:     // Update card state
2018:     const wasInZone = card.zone !== 'table';
2019:     card.zone = 'table';
2020:     card.x = x;
2021:     card.y = y;
2022:     card.rotation = 0;
2023:     card.zonePosition = 0;
2024: 
2025:     // Create new table card element
2026:     createTableCardElement(card);
2027: 
2028:     // Mark as having changes for recording
2029:     if (appState.phase === 'record') {
2030:         card.hasChanges = true;
2031:     }
2032: 
2033:     updateUI();
2034:     setStatus(`Moved ${card.displayName || card.name} to table`);
2035: }
2036: 
2037: // ============================================
2038: // CARD ELEMENTS ON TABLE
