2041: function createZoneCardElement(card, zoneElement) {
2042:     const zoneCardsContainer = zoneElement.querySelector('.zone-cards');
2043: 
2044:     // Safety check - if container not found, log and skip
2045:     if (!zoneCardsContainer) {
2046:         debugWarn(`Zone container not found! zone: ${zoneElement?.dataset?.zone}, id: ${zoneElement?.id}`);
2047:         return;
2048:     }
2049: 
2050:     const zoneName = zoneElement.dataset.zone;
2051: 
2052: 
2053:     const cardEl = document.createElement('div');
2054:     cardEl.className = `zone-card ${card.isFaceUp ? 'face-up' : 'face-down'}`;
2055:     if (appState.groupedCards.some(c => c.id === card.id)) {
2056:         cardEl.classList.add('grouped');
2057:     }
2058:     cardEl.id = card.id;
2059:     cardEl.dataset.cardId = card.id;
2060: 
2061:     // Different overlap direction based on zone
2062:     // Check if this is a community zone grid-slot
2063:     let isCZSlot = false;
2064:     if (zoneName && zoneName.startsWith('grid-')) {
2065:         const placeId = zoneName.replace('grid-', '');
2066:         const place = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.find(p => p.id === placeId);
2067:         if (place && place.isCommunityZone) {
2068:             isCZSlot = true;
2069:             const czMode = place.czMode || 'row';
2070:             cardEl.style.position = 'absolute';
2071:             cardEl.style.zIndex = 400 + (card.zonePosition || 0);
2072: 
2073:             // Use actual DOM container dimensions for centering
2074:             // The zoneElement is already scaled to DOM pixels
2075:             const containerW = zoneElement.offsetWidth;
2076:             const containerH = zoneElement.offsetHeight;
2077:             // Get actual card size from CSS (zone-card uses var(--card-width) / var(--card-height))
2078:             const cardW = 70; // CSS --card-width default
2079:             const cardH = 100; // CSS --card-height default
2080: 
2081:             // Center card within zone-cards container
2082:             cardEl.style.left = `${(containerW - cardW) / 2}px`;
2083:             cardEl.style.top = `${(containerH - cardH) / 2}px`;
2084: 
2085:             if (czMode === 'pile') {
2086:                 // Random offset + random rotation within zone bounds
2087:                 const maxOffsetX = Math.max(0, (containerW - cardW) / 2 - 5);
2088:                 const maxOffsetY = Math.max(0, (containerH - cardH) / 2 - 5);
2089:                 const randX = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2 * maxOffsetX;
2090:                 const randY = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2 * maxOffsetY;
2091:                 const randRot = Math.round((Math.random() - 0.5) * 30); // ±15°
2092:                 cardEl.style.transform = `translate(${randX}px, ${randY}px) rotate(${randRot}deg)`;
2093:                 card.rotation = randRot; // Store for AE export
2094:             } else if (czMode === 'stack') {
2095:                 // Perfect stack - all cards centered, no offset
2096:                 cardEl.style.transform = 'none';
2097:                 card.rotation = 0;
2098:             } else {
2099:                 // 'row' mode - horizontal offset per card, centered
2100:                 const totalCards = appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.zone === zoneName).length;
2101:                 const spacing = Math.min(cardW * 0.7, (containerW - cardW) / Math.max(1, totalCards - 1));
2102:                 const totalWidth = (totalCards - 1) * spacing;
2103:                 const startOffset = -totalWidth / 2;
2104:                 const offsetX = startOffset + (card.zonePosition || 0) * spacing;
2105:                 cardEl.style.transform = `translateX(${offsetX}px) rotate(${card.rotation || 0}deg)`;
2106:             }
2107:         }
2108:     }
2109: 
2110:     if (!isCZSlot && appState.boardLayout.boardStyle === 'poker' && zoneName === 'community') {
2111:         // Poker community: pile stacking — cards on top of each other
2112:         cardEl.style.position = 'absolute';
2113:         cardEl.style.zIndex = 400 + (card.zonePosition || 0);
2114: 
2115:         // Apply optional random offset for natural look
2116:         const randomCheckbox = document.getElementById('communityRandomRotation');
2117:         if (randomCheckbox && randomCheckbox.checked) {
2118:             // Random offset slightly so cards don't perfectly overlap
2119:             const offsetX = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 20; // ±10px
2120:             const offsetY = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15; // ±7.5px
2121:             cardEl.style.transform = `translate(${offsetX}px, ${offsetY}px) rotate(${card.rotation || 0}deg)`;
2122:         } else {
2123:             // Neat stack with slight horizontal offset per card
2124:             const offsetX = (card.zonePosition || 0) * 8; // 8px shift per card
2125:             cardEl.style.transform = `translateX(${offsetX}px) rotate(${card.rotation || 0}deg)`;
2126:         }
2127:     } else if (zoneName === 'left') {
2128:         // Left zone: cards stack top-to-bottom, later cards on top
2129:         cardEl.style.marginTop = card.zonePosition > 0 ? `-${CARD_HEIGHT - appState.cardOverlap}px` : '0';
2130:     } else if (zoneName === 'right') {
2131:         // Right zone: cards stack bottom-to-top (reverse), so upper cards overlay lower
2132:         cardEl.style.marginTop = card.zonePosition > 0 ? `-${CARD_HEIGHT - appState.cardOverlap}px` : '0';
2133:         // Use z-index to reverse stacking visually - higher position = lower z-index
2134:         cardEl.style.zIndex = 100 - card.zonePosition;
2135:     } else {
2136:         // Top/Bottom/Community: stack horizontally, use marginLeft
2137:         cardEl.style.marginLeft = card.zonePosition > 0 ? `-${CARD_WIDTH - appState.cardOverlap}px` : '0';
2138:     }
2139: 
2140:     // Inner structure for flip
2141:     const inner = document.createElement('div');
2142:     inner.className = 'card-inner';
2143: 
2144:     // Front face
2145:     const front = document.createElement('div');
2146:     front.className = 'card-face card-front';
2147:     const frontImg = document.createElement('img');
2148:     frontImg.src = card.frontImageUrl || createPlaceholderCardImage(card);
2149:     front.appendChild(frontImg);
2150: 
2151:     // Back face
2152:     const back = document.createElement('div');
2153:     back.className = 'card-face card-back';
2154:     if (card.backImageUrl) {
2155:         const backImg = document.createElement('img');
2156:         backImg.src = card.backImageUrl;
2157:         back.appendChild(backImg);
2158:     }
2159: 
2160:     inner.appendChild(front);
2161:     inner.appendChild(back);
2162:     cardEl.appendChild(inner);
2163: 
2164:     // Click to flip/select
2165:     cardEl.addEventListener('click', () => handleCardClick(card, cardEl));
2166: 
2167:     // Make draggable for Record mode (move cards between zones) and Setup mode (return to tray)
2168:     cardEl.draggable = true;
2169:     cardEl.addEventListener('dragstart', (e) => {
2170:         e.dataTransfer.setData('text/plain', card.id);
2171:         e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
2172:         cardEl.classList.add('dragging');
2173:         // Highlight all zones as potential drop targets
2174:         playerZones.forEach(zone => zone.classList.add('drag-target'));
2175:         document.querySelectorAll('.card-drop-zone').forEach(zone => zone.classList.add('drag-target'));
2176:         // Highlight card tray as return target in Setup phase
2177:         if (appState.phase === 'setup') {
2178:             const trayPanel = document.getElementById('cardTrayPanel');
2179:             if (trayPanel) trayPanel.classList.add('drag-target');
2180:         }
2181:     });
2182:     cardEl.addEventListener('dragend', () => {
2183:         cardEl.classList.remove('dragging');
2184:         // Remove highlight from all zones
2185:         playerZones.forEach(zone => zone.classList.remove('drag-target', 'drag-over'));
2186:         document.querySelectorAll('.card-drop-zone').forEach(zone => zone.classList.remove('drag-target', 'drag-over'));
2187:         // Remove tray highlight
2188:         const trayPanel = document.getElementById('cardTrayPanel');
2189:         if (trayPanel) trayPanel.classList.remove('drag-target', 'drag-over');
2190:     });
2191: 
2192:     zoneCardsContainer.appendChild(cardEl);
2193:     card.element = cardEl;
2194: }
2195: 
2196: function createTableCardElement(card) {
2197:     const cardEl = document.createElement('div');
2198:     cardEl.className = `card ${card.isFaceUp ? 'face-up' : 'face-down'}`;
2199:     if (appState.groupedCards.some(c => c.id === card.id)) {
2200:         cardEl.classList.add('grouped');
2201:     }
2202:     cardEl.id = card.id;
2203:     cardEl.dataset.cardId = card.id;
2204: 
2205:     // Position
2206:     const scaleX = gameContainer.offsetWidth / PROJECT_INFO.width;
2207:     const scaleY = gameContainer.offsetHeight / PROJECT_INFO.height;
2208: 
2209:     cardEl.style.left = '0';
2210:     cardEl.style.top = '0';
2211:     cardEl.style.transform = `translate(${card.x * scaleX}px, ${card.y * scaleY}px) rotate(${card.rotation}deg)`;
2212: 
2213:     // Inner structure for flip
2214:     const inner = document.createElement('div');
2215:     inner.className = 'card-inner';
2216: 
2217:     // Front face
2218:     const front = document.createElement('div');
2219:     front.className = 'card-face card-front';
2220:     const frontImg = document.createElement('img');
2221:     frontImg.src = card.frontImageUrl || createPlaceholderCardImage(card);
2222:     front.appendChild(frontImg);
2223: 
2224:     // Back face
2225:     const back = document.createElement('div');
2226:     back.className = 'card-face card-back';
2227:     if (card.backImageUrl) {
2228:         const backImg = document.createElement('img');
2229:         backImg.src = card.backImageUrl;
2230:         back.appendChild(backImg);
2231:     }
2232: 
2233:     inner.appendChild(front);
2234:     inner.appendChild(back);
2235:     cardEl.appendChild(inner);
2236: 
2237:     // Label
2238:     const label = document.createElement('div');
2239:     label.className = 'card-label';
2240:     label.textContent = card.displayName || card.name;
2241:     cardEl.appendChild(label);
2242: 
2243:     // Click to select/flip
2244:     cardEl.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
2245:         e.stopPropagation();
2246:         handleCardClick(card, cardEl);
2247:     });
2248: 
2249:     // Make draggable
2250:     makeCardDraggable(cardEl, card);
2251: 
2252:     cardArea.appendChild(cardEl);
2253:     card.element = cardEl;
2254: }
2255: 
2256: // ============================================
2257: // CARD INTERACTIONS
2258: // ============================================
2259: 
2260: function handleCardClick(card, element) {
2261:     // Check if grouping mode is active (Record phase only)
2262:     if (appState.groupingMode && appState.phase === 'record') {
2263:         toggleCardGroupSelection(card);
2264: 
2265:         // If card is now in group, also select it to show context menu for flip/slam
2266:         const isInGroup = appState.groupedCards.some(c => c.id === card.id);
2267:         if (isInGroup) {
2268:             selectCard(card);
2269:         }
2270:         return;  // Don't proceed with normal selection flow
2271:     }
2272: 
2273:     // Select the card
2274:     selectCard(card);
2275: 
2276:     // If in setup phase, also flip the card
2277:     if (appState.phase === 'setup') {
2278:         flipCard(card);
2279:     }
2280: }
2281: 
2282: function selectCard(card) {
2283:     // Deselect previous
2284:     if (appState.selectedCard && appState.selectedCard.element) {
2285:         appState.selectedCard.element.classList.remove('selected');
2286:     }
2287: 
2288:     appState.selectedCard = card;
2289: 
2290:     if (card.element) {
2291:         card.element.classList.add('selected');
2292:     }
2293: 
2294:     // Update properties panel
2295:     noCardSelected.classList.add('hidden');
2296:     cardProperties.classList.remove('hidden');
2297:     selectedCardName.textContent = card.displayName || card.name;
2298:     cardFaceState.textContent = card.isFaceUp ? 'Up' : 'Down';
2299: 
2300:     // Update card thumbnail
2301:     const thumbContainer = document.getElementById('selectedCardThumb');
2302:     thumbContainer.innerHTML = '';
2303:     if (card.frontImageUrl) {
2304:         const img = document.createElement('img');
2305:         img.src = card.frontImageUrl;
2306:         img.alt = card.displayName || card.name;
2307:         thumbContainer.appendChild(img);
2308:     }
2309: 
2310:     flipCardCheck.checked = card.flipAction || false;
2311:     slamEffectCheck.checked = card.slamEffect || false;
2312:     spinEffectCheck.checked = card.spinEffect || false;
2313: 
2314:     updateCardPosDisplay(card);
2315: 
2316:     // Show inline context menu next to card (Record mode only)
2317:     showCardContextMenu(card);
2318: }
2319: 
2320: function deselectCard() {
2321:     if (appState.selectedCard && appState.selectedCard.element) {
2322:         appState.selectedCard.element.classList.remove('selected');
2323:     }
2324:     appState.selectedCard = null;
2325: 
2326:     noCardSelected.classList.remove('hidden');
2327:     cardProperties.classList.add('hidden');
2328: 
2329:     // Hide context menu
2330:     hideCardContextMenu();
2331: }
2332: 
2333: function flipCard(card) {
2334:     card.isFaceUp = !card.isFaceUp;
2335: 
2336:     if (card.element) {
2337:         // Add flip animation
2338:         card.element.classList.add('flipping');
2339: 
2340:         setTimeout(() => {
2341:             card.element.classList.remove('face-up', 'face-down');
2342:             card.element.classList.add(card.isFaceUp ? 'face-up' : 'face-down');
2343:             card.element.classList.remove('flipping');
2344:         }, 200); // Half of flip duration
2345:     }
2346: 
2347:     // Update panel
2348:     if (appState.selectedCard === card) {
2349:         cardFaceState.textContent = card.isFaceUp ? 'Up' : 'Down';
2350:     }
2351: }
2352: 
2353: function handleZoneFlipChange(e) {
2354:     const zoneName = e.target.dataset.zone;
2355:     const shouldFaceUp = e.target.checked;
2356: 
2357:     // Find all cards in this zone and flip them accordingly
2358:     appState.tableCards
2359:         .filter(card => card.zone === zoneName)
2360:         .forEach(card => {
2361:             if (card.isFaceUp !== shouldFaceUp) {
2362:                 flipCard(card);
2363:             }
2364:         });
2365: 
2366:     setStatus(`${zoneName.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + zoneName.slice(1)} zone: ${shouldFaceUp ? 'Face up' : 'Face down'}`);
2367: }
2368: 
2369: function updateCardPosDisplay(card) {
2370:     cardPosX.textContent = Math.round(card.x || 0);
2371:     cardPosY.textContent = Math.round(card.y || 0);
2372:     cardRot.textContent = `${Math.round(card.rotation || 0)}°`;
2373: }
2374: 
2375: // ============================================
2376: // DRAGGABLE CARDS ON TABLE
2377: // ============================================
2378: 
2379: function makeCardDraggable(element, card) {
2380:     let isDragging = false;
2381:     let offsetX, offsetY;
2382: 
2383:     element.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
2384:         if (e.button !== 0) return;
2385:         e.preventDefault();
2386: 
2387:         isDragging = true;
2388:         element.classList.add('dragging');
2389: 
2390:         const rect = cardArea.getBoundingClientRect();
2391:         const scaleX = PROJECT_INFO.width / rect.width;
2392:         const scaleY = PROJECT_INFO.height / rect.height;
2393: 
2394:         const mouseX = (e.clientX - rect.left) * scaleX;
2395:         const mouseY = (e.clientY - rect.top) * scaleY;
2396: 
2397:         offsetX = card.x - mouseX;
2398:         offsetY = card.y - mouseY;
2399: 
2400:         element.style.zIndex = 1000;
2401:     });
2402: 
2403:     document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
2404:         if (!isDragging) return;
2405: 
2406:         const rect = cardArea.getBoundingClientRect();
2407:         const scaleX = PROJECT_INFO.width / rect.width;
2408:         const scaleY = PROJECT_INFO.height / rect.height;
2409: 
2410:         const mouseX = (e.clientX - rect.left) * scaleX;
2411:         const mouseY = (e.clientY - rect.top) * scaleY;
2412: 
2413:         card.x = mouseX + offsetX;
2414:         card.y = mouseY + offsetY;
2415: 
2416:         // Update visual position
2417:         const visualX = card.x / scaleX;
2418:         const visualY = card.y / scaleY;
2419:         element.style.transform = `translate(${visualX}px, ${visualY}px) rotate(${card.rotation}deg)`;
2420: 
2421:         updateCardPosDisplay(card);
2422:     });
2423: 
2424:     document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
2425:         if (!isDragging) return;
2426:         isDragging = false;
2427:         element.classList.remove('dragging');
2428:         element.style.zIndex = '';
2429:     });
2430: }
2431:

2436: function handleOverlapChange() {
2437:     appState.cardOverlap = parseInt(overlapSlider.value);
2438:     overlapValue.textContent = `${appState.cardOverlap}px`;
2439: 
2440:     // Re-render zone cards with new overlap
2441:     reRenderZoneCards();
2442: }

2444: function reRenderZoneCards() {
2445:     playerZones.forEach(zone => {
2446:         const zoneName = zone.dataset.zone;
2447:         const zoneCards = appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.zone === zoneName);
2448: 
2449:         zoneCards.forEach((card, index) => {
2450:             if (card.element) {
2451:                 card.element.style.marginLeft = index > 0 ? `-${CARD_WIDTH - appState.cardOverlap}px` : '0';
2452:             }
2453:         });
2454:     });
2455: }

2457: // ============================================
2458: // RESET TABLE
2459: // ============================================
2460: 
2461: function handleResetTable() {
2462:     if (appState.tableCards.length === 0 && !appState._bulkApplying) return;
2463: 
2464:     if (!appState._bulkApplying && !confirm('Return all cards to tray?')) return;
2465: 
2466:     // Remove card elements
2467:     appState.tableCards.forEach(card => {
2468:         if (card.element) {
2469:             card.element.remove();
2470:         }
2471:         card.inTray = true;
2472:         card.zone = null;
2473:         card.element = null;
2474:         card.isFaceUp = false;
2475:     });
2476: 
2477:     appState.tableCards = [];
2478:     appState.selectedCard = null;
2479: 
2480:     renderCardTray();
2481:     showInstructions();
2482:     deselectCard();
2483:     updateUI();
2484: 
2485:     setStatus('All cards returned to tray');
2486: }
2487: 
2488: /**
2489:  * Return a single card from the table back to the tray
2490:  * Only allowed in Setup phase to avoid breaking recording snapshots
2491:  */
2492: function returnCardToTray(card) {
2493:     if (!card) return;
2494: 
2495:     // Remove card element from DOM
2496:     if (card.element) {
2497:         card.element.remove();
2498:     }
2499: 
2500:     // Reset card state
2501:     card.inTray = true;
2502:     card.zone = null;
2503:     card.element = null;
2504:     card.isFaceUp = false;
2505:     card.zonePosition = 0;
2506:     card.rotation = 0;
2507: 
2508:     // Remove from tableCards array
2509:     appState.tableCards = appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.id !== card.id);
2510: 
2511:     // Deselect if this was the selected card
2512:     if (appState.selectedCard && appState.selectedCard.id === card.id) {
2513:         appState.selectedCard = null;
2514:         deselectCard();
2515:     }
2516: 
2517:     // Re-render tray and update UI
2518:     renderCardTray();
2519:     updateUI();
2520: 
2521:     if (appState.tableCards.length === 0) {
2522:         showInstructions();
2523:     }
2524: 
2525:     setStatus(`Returned ${card.displayName || card.name} to tray`);
2526: }
2527: 
2528: /**
2529:  * Setup card tray panel as a drop target for returning cards
2530:  * Only accepts drops during Setup phase
2531:  */
2532: function setupTrayDropTarget() {
2533:     const trayPanel = document.getElementById('cardTrayPanel');
2534:     if (!trayPanel) return;
2535: 
2536:     trayPanel.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
2537:         // Only accept drops in Setup phase
2538:         if (appState.phase !== 'setup') return;
2539: 
2540:         // Only accept cards that are on the table (not from tray itself)
2541:         e.preventDefault();
2542:         e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move';
2543:         trayPanel.classList.add('drag-over');
2544:     });
2545: 
2546:     trayPanel.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
2547:         trayPanel.classList.remove('drag-over');
2548:     });
2549: 
2550:     trayPanel.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
2551:         e.preventDefault();
2552:         trayPanel.classList.remove('drag-over');
2553: 
2554:         // Only accept drops in Setup phase
2555:         if (appState.phase !== 'setup') return;
2556: 
2557:         const cardId = e.dataTransfer.getData('text/plain');
2558:         const card = appState.tableCards.find(c => c.id === cardId);
2559: 
2560:         if (card) {
2561:             returnCardToTray(card);
2562:         }
2563:     });
2564: }
2565: 
2566: // ============================================
2567: // RECORDING LOGIC
2568: // ============================================
2569: 
2570: function handleAddStep() {
2571:     if (appState.isEditingStep) {
2572:         setStatus('Finish current step first', 'error');
2573:         return;
2574:     }
2575: 
2576:     if (appState.tableCards.length === 0) {
2577:         setStatus('Place some cards on the table first', 'error');
2578:         return;
2579:     }
2580: 
2581:     startSnapshot = takeSnapshot();
2582: 
2583:     currentStep = {
2584:         stepId: scenarioData.scenario.length + 1,
2585:         duration: stepDuration ? parseFloat(stepDuration.value) : 1.0,
2586:         actions: []
2587:     };
2588: 
2589:     appState.isEditingStep = true;
2590:     appState.currentStepIndex = currentStep.stepId;
2591: 
2592:     if (finishStepBtn) finishStepBtn.disabled = false;
2593:     addStepBtn.disabled = true;
2594:     recordingIndicator.classList.add('active');
2595:     currentStepNum.textContent = currentStep.stepId;
2596: 
2597:     setStatus(`Editing Step ${currentStep.stepId} - Move cards and set properties`);
2598: }
2599: 
2600: function handleFinishStep() {
2601:     if (!appState.isEditingStep || !currentStep) return;
2602: 
2603:     const endSnapshot = takeSnapshot();
2604:     const actions = computeActions(startSnapshot, endSnapshot);
2605: 
2606:     currentStep.actions = actions;
2607:     currentStep.duration = stepDuration ? parseFloat(stepDuration.value) : 1.0;
2608: 
2609:     // Attach group order overrides if user reordered groups during this step
2610:     if (appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides) {
2611:         currentStep.groupOrderOverrides = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides));
2612:         // Apply overrides to actual group.groupOrder for subsequent steps
2613:         var groups = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || [];
2614:         groups.forEach(function (g) {
2615:             if (appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides[g.id] !== undefined) {
2616:                 g.groupOrder = appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides[g.id];
2617:             }
2618:         });
2619:         appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides = null;
2620:     }
2621: 
2622:     scenarioData.scenario.push(currentStep);
2623: 
2624:     // Save snapshot for replay and edit restore
2625:     stepSnapshots.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(endSnapshot)));
2626: 
2627:     appState.isEditingStep = false;
2628:     currentStep = null;
2629:     startSnapshot = null;
2630: 
2631:     if (finishStepBtn) finishStepBtn.disabled = true;
2632:     addStepBtn.disabled = false;
2633:     recordingIndicator.classList.remove('active');
2634:     currentStepNum.textContent = '-';
2635:     totalSteps.textContent = scenarioData.scenario.length;
2636: 
2637:     renderTimeline();
2638:     renderGroupOrderStrip();
2639:     setStatus(`Step ${scenarioData.scenario.length} saved with ${actions.length} actions`, 'success');
2640:     updateUI();
2641: }
2642: 
2643: /**
2644:  * Save the initial state of all cards when entering Record mode
2645:  * This is used for replay and restore functionality
2646:  */
2647: function saveInitialState() {
2648:     // Skip during AI bulk apply — applyAIScenario manages its own snapshots
2649:     if (appState._bulkApplying) {
2650:         debugLog('[saveInitialState] Skipped — _bulkApplying is true');
2651:         return;
2652:     }
2653: 
2654:     scenarioData.initialState = {};
2655: 
2656:     appState.tableCards.forEach(card => {
2657:         scenarioData.initialState[card.id] = {
2658:             x: card.x || 0,
2659:             y: card.y || 0,
2660:             rotation: card.rotation || 0,
2661:             isFaceUp: card.isFaceUp,
2662:             zone: card.zone,
2663:             zonePosition: card.zonePosition || 0,
2664:             zOrder: computeZOrderForCard(card),
2665:             flipAction: card.flipAction || false,
2666:             slamEffect: card.slamEffect || false,
2667:             isSelected: appState.groupedCards.some(c => c.id === card.id)
2668:         };
2669:     });
2670: 
2671:     // Reset step snapshots when entering record mode
2672:     stepSnapshots = [];
2673: 
2674:     // Save initial state as stepSnapshots[0] - this is "step 0" (before any actions)
2675:     // This ensures replay can properly reset to initial positions on subsequent plays
2676:     stepSnapshots.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(scenarioData.initialState)));
2677: 
2678:     console.log('Initial state saved:', scenarioData.initialState);
2679: }
2680: 
2681: function takeSnapshot() {
2682:     const snapshot = {};
2683:     appState.tableCards.forEach(card => {
2684:         snapshot[card.id] = {
2685:             x: card.x || 0,
2686:             y: card.y || 0,
2687:             rotation: card.rotation || 0,
2688:             isFaceUp: card.isFaceUp,
2689:             zone: card.zone,
2690:             zonePosition: card.zonePosition || 0,
2691:             zOrder: computeZOrderForCard(card),
2692:             flipAction: card.flipAction || false,
2693:             slamEffect: card.slamEffect || false,
2694:             isSelected: appState.groupedCards.some(c => c.id === card.id)
2695:         };
2696:     });
2697:     return snapshot;
2698: }
2699: 
2700: function computeActions(startSnap, endSnap) {
2701:     const actions = [];
2702: 
2703:     appState.tableCards.forEach(card => {
2704:         const start = startSnap[card.id];
2705:         const end = endSnap[card.id];
2706: 
2707:         // Calculate AE positions for zones (since zone cards use x/y = 0 in UI)
2708:         const getAEPosition = (state) => {
2709:             if (state.zone && state.zone !== 'table') {
2710:                 return getAEZonePosition(state.zone, state.zonePosition);
2711:             }
2712:             return { x: Math.round(state.x || 0), y: Math.round(state.y || 0) };
2713:         };
2714: 
2715:         // New card placed from tray (not in start snapshot)
2716:         if (!start && end) {
2717:             const endPos = getAEPosition(end);
2718:             actions.push({
2719:                 targetId: card.id,
2720:                 type: 'PLACE',
2721:                 startPosition: { x: -500, y: PROJECT_INFO.height / 2 }, // Start from far left
2722:                 endPosition: endPos,
2723:                 startRotation: 0,
2724:                 endRotation: Math.round(end.rotation || 0),
2725:                 zone: end.zone,
2726:                 flip: card.flipAction,
2727:                 flipToFaceUp: end.isFaceUp,
2728:                 effect: card.slamEffect ? 'SLAM' : null,
2729:                 spin: card.spinEffect
2730:             });
2731:             return;
2732:         }
2733: 
2734:         if (!start || !end) return;
2735: 
2736:         // Check for SELECT/DESELECT changes (grouping mode)
2737:         const startSelected = start.isSelected || false;
2738:         const endSelected = end.isSelected || false;
2739: 
2740:         if (startSelected !== endSelected) {
2741:             // SELECT uses current/end position (card lifts at its current spot)
2742:             // DESELECT uses START position (card drops at its original spot before moving)
2743:             const pos = endSelected ? getAEPosition(end) : getAEPosition(start);
2744:             actions.push({
2745:                 targetId: card.id,
2746:                 type: endSelected ? 'SELECT' : 'DESELECT',
2747:                 position: pos,
2748:                 zone: endSelected ? end.zone : start.zone,
2749:                 zonePosition: endSelected ? (end.zonePosition || 0) : (start.zonePosition || 0),
2750:                 // SELECT moves Y up by SELECT_OFFSET_Y, DESELECT moves back down
2751:                 selectOffset: endSelected ? -25 : 0
2752:             });
2753:             // If only selection changed, don't process as TRANSFORM
2754:             // (unless there are also position/zone changes)
2755:         }
2756: 
2757: 
2758:         const startPos = getAEPosition(start);
2759:         const endPos = getAEPosition(end);
2760: 
2761:         // Only check position change if zone changed
2762:         // Cards staying in same zone should NOT get new keyframes just from rearrangement
2763:         const zoneChanged = end.zone !== start.zone;
2764:         const posChanged = zoneChanged && (
2765:             Math.abs(endPos.x - startPos.x) > 1 ||
2766:             Math.abs(endPos.y - startPos.y) > 1
2767:         );
2768:         const rotChanged = Math.abs((end.rotation || 0) - (start.rotation || 0)) > 0.5;
2769:         const flipChanged = end.isFaceUp !== start.isFaceUp;
2770: 
2771:         // Standalone flip (face changed but no zone change) → FLIP action
2772:         if (flipChanged && !zoneChanged) {
2773:             const pos = getAEPosition(end);
2774:             actions.push({
2775:                 targetId: card.id,
2776:                 type: 'FLIP',
2777:                 position: pos,
2778:                 zone: end.zone,
2779:                 zonePosition: end.zonePosition || 0,
2780:                 flipToFaceUp: end.isFaceUp
2781:             });
2782:             // Don't fall through to TRANSFORM — this is a standalone flip
2783:             return;
2784:         }
2785: 
2786:         // IMPORTANT: Only apply flipAction/slamEffect if card actually moves (zone changed)
2787:         // These flags are "sticky" on card objects, so we must NOT use them for stationary cards
2788:         const hasFlipAction = zoneChanged && card.flipAction;
2789:         const hasSlam = zoneChanged && card.slamEffect;
2790:         const hasSpin = zoneChanged && card.spinEffect;
2791: 
2792:         if (posChanged || rotChanged || flipChanged || zoneChanged || hasFlipAction || hasSlam || hasSpin) {
2793:             // Get endZOrder using group-aware computation
2794:             var endZOrder = computeZOrderForCard(end);
2795:             actions.push({
2796:                 targetId: card.id,
2797:                 type: 'TRANSFORM',
2798:                 startPosition: startPos,
2799:                 endPosition: endPos,
2800:                 startRotation: Math.round(start.rotation || 0),
2801:                 endRotation: Math.round(end.rotation || 0),
2802:                 startZone: start.zone,
2803:                 endZone: end.zone,
2804:                 endZOrder: endZOrder,
2805:                 flip: hasFlipAction || flipChanged,
2806:                 flipToFaceUp: end.isFaceUp,
2807:                 effect: hasSlam ? 'SLAM' : null,
2808:                 spin: hasSpin
2809:             });
2810:         }
2811:     });
2812: 
2813:     // Detect REMOVED cards (in startSnap but not in endSnap / not in tableCards)
2814:     var currentCardIds = new Set(appState.tableCards.map(function (c) { return c.id; }));
2815:     Object.keys(startSnap).forEach(function (cardId) {
2816:         if (!endSnap[cardId] && !currentCardIds.has(cardId)) {
2817:             var start = startSnap[cardId];
2818:             var startPos = (start.zone && start.zone !== 'table')
2819:                 ? getAEZonePosition(start.zone, start.zonePosition || 0)
2820:                 : { x: Math.round(start.x || 0), y: Math.round(start.y || 0) };
2821:             actions.push({
2822:                 targetId: cardId,
2823:                 type: 'REMOVE',
2824:                 startPosition: startPos,
2825:                 endPosition: { x: PROJECT_INFO.width + 500, y: startPos.y },
2826:                 startRotation: Math.round(start.rotation || 0),
2827:                 endRotation: Math.round(start.rotation || 0),
2828:                 zone: start.zone
2829:             });
2830:         }
2831:     });
2832: 
2833:     return actions;
2834: }
2835: 
2836: 
2837: 
2838: 
2839: function handlePropertyChange() {
2840:     if (!appState.selectedCard) return;
2841: 
2842:     appState.selectedCard.flipAction = flipCardCheck.checked;
2843:     appState.selectedCard.slamEffect = slamEffectCheck.checked;
2844:     appState.selectedCard.spinEffect = spinEffectCheck.checked;
2845: 
2846:     // Sync popup menu button states
2847:     updateContextMenuState(appState.selectedCard);
2848: }
2849: 
2850: // ============================================
2851: // COORDINATE TRANSFORMATION SYSTEM
2852: // UI (1280x720) ↔ AE (1920x1080)
2853: // ============================================
2854: 
2855: /**
2856:  * Transform UI coordinates to AE coordinates
2857:  * @param {number} uiX - X position in UI (1280x720)
2858:  * @param {number} uiY - Y position in UI (1280x720)
2859:  * @returns {object} {x, y} position for AE (1920x1080)
2860:  */
2861: function uiToAEPosition(uiX, uiY) {
2862:     return {
2863:         x: Math.round(uiX * COORD_SCALE),
2864:         y: Math.round(uiY * COORD_SCALE)
2865:     };
2866: }
2867: 
2868: /**
2869:  * Transform AE coordinates to UI coordinates
2870:  * @param {number} aeX - X position in AE (1920x1080)
2871:  * @param {number} aeY - Y position in AE (1920x1080)
2872:  * @returns {object} {x, y} position for UI (1280x720)
2873:  */
2874: function aeToUIPosition(aeX, aeY) {
2875:     return {
2876:         x: Math.round(aeX / COORD_SCALE),
2877:         y: Math.round(aeY / COORD_SCALE)
2878:     };
2879: }
2880: 
2881: /**
2882:  * Get zone position in UI coordinates (relative to poker table)
2883:  * @param {string} zoneName - Zone name
2884:  * @param {number} zonePosition - Position within zone
2885:  * @returns {object} {x, y} position in UI coordinates
2886:  */
2887: function getUIZonePosition(zoneName, zonePosition = 0) {
2888:     const CARD_SPACING_UI = 45; // Card spacing in UI pixels
2889: 
2890:     // Handle grid zones (grid-place-X)
2891:     if (zoneName && zoneName.startsWith('grid-')) {
2892:         const placeId = zoneName.replace('grid-', '');
2893: 
2894:         // Try to get position from boardLayout.cardPlaces
2895:         const place = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.find(p => p.id === placeId);
2896:         if (place) {
2897:             // Community zone: calculate per-card offset based on czMode
2898:             if (place.isCommunityZone) {
2899:                 const czMode = place.czMode || 'row';
2900:                 if (czMode === 'row') {
2901:                     // Horizontal row offset from center
2902:                     const spacing = Math.min(CARD_SPACING_UI, (place.czWidth || 300) / Math.max(1, zonePosition + 1));
2903:                     return {
2904:                         x: Math.round(place.x + (zonePosition * spacing) - (zonePosition * spacing / 2)),
2905:                         y: Math.round(place.y)
2906:                     };
2907:                 } else if (czMode === 'pile') {
2908:                     // Slight deterministic offset per card
2909:                     const seed = zonePosition * 7919; // Simple pseudo-random from position
2910:                     const offsetX = ((seed % 20) - 10);
2911:                     const offsetY = (((seed * 3) % 14) - 7);
2912:                     return {
2913:                         x: Math.round(place.x + offsetX),
2914:                         y: Math.round(place.y + offsetY)
2915:                     };
2916:                 } else {
2917:                     // 'stack' - all at center
2918:                     return { x: place.x, y: place.y };
2919:                 }
2920:             }
2921:             return { x: place.x, y: place.y };
2922:         }
2923: 
2924:         // Fallback: get position from DOM element
2925:         const zoneEl = document.querySelector(`.card-drop-zone[data-zone="${zoneName}"]`);
2926:         if (zoneEl) {
2927:             const pokerTable = document.getElementById('pokerTable');
2928:             if (pokerTable) {
2929:                 const tableRect = pokerTable.getBoundingClientRect();
2930:                 const zoneRect = zoneEl.getBoundingClientRect();
2931:                 return {
2932:                     x: zoneRect.left - tableRect.left + CARD_WIDTH / 2,
2933:                     y: zoneRect.top - tableRect.top + CARD_HEIGHT / 2
2934:                 };
2935:             }
2936:         }
2937: 
2938:         return { x: UI_WIDTH / 2, y: UI_HEIGHT / 2 };
2939:     }
2940: 
2941:     // Zone base positions in UI coordinates (1280x720)
2942:     // These match the visual layout of the web tool
2943:     const zonePositions = {
2944:         'top': { x: UI_WIDTH / 2 - 50, y: 80 },
2945:         'bottom': { x: UI_WIDTH / 2 - 50, y: UI_HEIGHT - 80 },
2946:         'left': { x: 120, y: UI_HEIGHT / 2 },
2947:         'right': { x: UI_WIDTH - 120, y: UI_HEIGHT / 2 },
2948:         'community': { x: UI_WIDTH / 2 - 80, y: UI_HEIGHT / 2 }
2949:     };
2950: 
2951:     const basePos = zonePositions[zoneName] || { x: UI_WIDTH / 2, y: UI_HEIGHT / 2 };
2952: 
2953:     // Calculate offset for multiple cards
2954:     let offsetX = (zonePosition || 0) * CARD_SPACING_UI;
2955:     let offsetY = 0;
2956: 
2957:     // Vertical zones (left/right) use Y offset
2958:     if (zoneName === 'left' || zoneName === 'right') {
2959:         offsetY = (zonePosition || 0) * CARD_SPACING_UI;
2960:         offsetX = 0;
2961:     }
2962: 
2963:     return {
2964:         x: Math.round(basePos.x + offsetX),
2965:         y: Math.round(basePos.y + offsetY)
2966:     };
2967: }
2968: 
2969: /**
2970:  * Get zone position for AE export (transformed from UI to AE coordinates)
2971:  * @param {string} zone - Zone name
2972:  * @param {number} zonePosition - Position within zone
2973:  * @returns {object} {x, y} position for AE (1920x1080)
2974:  */
2975: function getAEZonePosition(zone, zonePosition = 0) {
2976:     const uiPos = getUIZonePosition(zone, zonePosition);
2977:     return uiToAEPosition(uiPos.x, uiPos.y);
2978: }
2979: 
2980: 
2981: function saveInitialStateForExport() {
2982:     // This version calculates positions for AE export
2983:     const exportState = {};
2984: 
2985:     // Card scale for AE - 50% gives good visibility on 1080p
2986:     const aeCardScale = 0.625;
2987: 
2988:     // Get the initial snapshot (step 0) to check which cards existed at start
2989:     const initialSnap = stepSnapshots[0] || {};
2990: 
2991:     appState.tableCards.forEach(card => {
2992:         // Check if card existed in the initial snapshot
2993:         const wasInInitialSnap = initialSnap[card.id] !== undefined;
2994: 
2995:         // Calculate position based on zone
2996:         let posX = card.x || 0;
2997:         let posY = card.y || 0;
2998: 
2999:         if (!wasInInitialSnap) {
3000:             // Card was added from tray during recording - start off-screen left
3001:             posX = -500;
3002:             posY = PROJECT_INFO.height / 2;
3003:         } else if (initialSnap[card.id].zone && initialSnap[card.id].zone !== 'table') {
3004:             // For zone cards, use INITIAL zone and position (not current card.zone which may have changed)
3005:             const aePos = getAEZonePosition(initialSnap[card.id].zone, initialSnap[card.id].zonePosition || 0);
3006:             posX = aePos.x;
3007:             posY = aePos.y;
3008:         }
3009: 
3010:         exportState[card.id] = {
3011:             name: card.name,
3012:             filename: card.filename,
3013:             frontImage: card.filename,
3014:             backImage: 'back.png',
3015:             x: Math.round(posX),
3016:             y: Math.round(posY),
3017:             rotation: wasInInitialSnap ? (initialSnap[card.id].rotation || 0) : 0,
3018:             scale: aeCardScale,
3019:             zone: wasInInitialSnap ? initialSnap[card.id].zone : 'offscreen',
3020:             zonePosition: wasInInitialSnap ? (initialSnap[card.id].zonePosition || 0) : 0,
3021:             zOrder: wasInInitialSnap ? (initialSnap[card.id].zOrder || 0) : 0,
3022:             isFaceUp: wasInInitialSnap ? initialSnap[card.id].isFaceUp : false
3023:         };
3024: 
3025:         // For Pusoy layout: include per-card row/col and rowCount for AE expression sliders
3026:         // Use INITIAL zone (not current card.zone) to get correct row/col if card was swapped
3027:         const pusoyZone = wasInInitialSnap ? initialSnap[card.id].zone : card.zone;
3028:         if (appState.boardLayout.boardStyle === 'pusoy' && pusoyZone && pusoyZone.startsWith('grid-')) {
3029:             const placeId = pusoyZone.replace('grid-', '');
3030:             const place = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.find(p => p.id === placeId);
3031:             if (place) {
3032:                 const rowConfigs = [{ count: 3 }, { count: 5 }, { count: 5 }]; // Pusoy 3-5-5
3033:                 const rowCount = rowConfigs[place.row] ? rowConfigs[place.row].count : 1;
3034:                 exportState[card.id].row = place.row;
3035:                 exportState[card.id].col = place.col;
3036:                 exportState[card.id].rowCount = rowCount;
3037:             }
3038:         }
3039: 
3040:         // Include clonerId if the card's place belongs to a cloner group
3041:         // This helps dealing animation group source cards with their cloner
3042:         var clonerZone = wasInInitialSnap ? initialSnap[card.id].zone : card.zone;
3043:         if (clonerZone && clonerZone.startsWith('grid-')) {
3044:             const placeId = clonerZone.replace('grid-', '');
3045:             const place = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.find(p => p.id === placeId);
3046:             if (place && place.clonerId) {
3047:                 exportState[card.id].clonerId = place.clonerId;
3048:             }
3049:         }
3050:     });
3051: 
3052:     return exportState;
3053: }

3057:     if (appState.tableCards.length === 0) {
3058:         setStatus('No cards on table to export', 'error');
3059:         return;
3060:     }
3061: 
3062:     // Use export version with AE-calculated positions
3063:     const exportData = {
3064:         ...scenarioData,
3065:         initialState: saveInitialStateForExport()
3066:     };
3067: 
3068:     const jsonString = JSON.stringify(exportData, null, 2);
3069:     const blob = new Blob([jsonString], { type: 'application/json' });
3070:     const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
3071: 
3072:     const a = document.createElement('a');
3073:     a.href = url;
3074:     a.download = `poker_scenario_${Date.now()}.json`;
3075:     document.body.appendChild(a);
3076:     a.click();
3077:     document.body.removeChild(a);
3078:     URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
3079: 
3080:     setStatus('Scenario exported!', 'success');
3081: }
3082: 
3083: function handleExportToAE() {
3084:     if (!csInterface) {
3085:         setStatus('After Effects not connected', 'error');
3086:         return;
3087:     }
3088: 
3089:     if (appState.tableCards.length === 0) {
3090:         setStatus('No cards on table', 'error');
3091:         return;
3092:     }
3093: 
3094:     if (!appState.assetsRootPath) {
3095:         setStatus('Select Assets Folder first!', 'error');
3096:         return;
3097:     }
3098: 
3099:     // Use export version with AE-calculated positions
3100:     const exportData = {
3101:         ...scenarioData,
3102:         initialState: saveInitialStateForExport(),
3103:         boardType: appState.boardLayout.boardStyle || appState.boardLayout.type || 'poker',
3104:         stepBlending: appState.stepBlending || 0,  // Overlap % between steps
3105:         enableVisualMouse: true  // Create mouse cursor null for swap animations
3106:     };
3107: 
3108:     // Include dealing card config if enabled
3109:     if (appState.dealingCard.enabled) {
3110:         const aePos = uiToAEPosition(appState.dealingCard.x, appState.dealingCard.y);
3111:         exportData.dealingCard = {
3112:             enabled: true,
3113:             x: aePos.x,
3114:             y: aePos.y,
3115:             staggerFrames: appState.dealSpeed || 3  // Frames between each card deal (1=fast, 5=slow)
3116:         };
3117:     }
3118: 
3119:     // Include Pusoy config for AE expression sliders
3120:     if (appState.boardLayout.boardStyle === 'pusoy') {
3121:         const spacingSlider = document.getElementById('pusoySpacing');
3122:         const curvatureSlider = document.getElementById('pusoyCurvature');
3123:         const layerGapSlider = document.getElementById('pusoyLayerGap');
3124:         exportData.pusoyConfig = {
3125:             defaultSpacing: spacingSlider ? parseInt(spacingSlider.value) : 150,
3126:             defaultCurvature: curvatureSlider ? parseInt(curvatureSlider.value) : 50,
3127:             defaultLayerGap: layerGapSlider ? parseInt(layerGapSlider.value) : 30,
3128:             basePivotY: 645  // 430 UI * 1.5 AE scale
3129:         };
3130:     }
3131: 
3132:     // Include slotGroups for group-aware z-order in AE
3133:     if (appState.boardLayout.slotGroups && appState.boardLayout.slotGroups.length > 0) {
3134:         exportData.slotGroups = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(appState.boardLayout.slotGroups));
3135:     }
3136: 
3137:     setStatus('Sending to After Effects...', 'recording');
3138: 
3139:     const jsonString = JSON.stringify(exportData);
3140:     const assetsPath = escapeForScript(appState.assetsRootPath);
3141: 
3142:     csInterface.evalScript(
3143:         `generateSequence('${escapeForScript(jsonString)}', '${assetsPath}')`,
3144:         (result) => {
3145:             try {
3146:                 const response = JSON.parse(result);
3147:                 if (response.success) {
3148:                     setStatus(`✓ ${response.message}`, 'success');
3149:                 } else {
3150:                     setStatus(`Error: ${response.message}`, 'error');
3151:                 }
3152:             } catch (e) {
3153:                 setStatus('Sent to After Effects', 'success');
3154:             }
3155:         }
3156:     );
3157: }
3158: 
3159: function escapeForScript(str) {
3160:     return str
3161:         .replace(/\\/g, '\\\\')
3162:         .replace(/'/g, "\\'")
3163:         .replace(/"/g, '\\"')
3164:         .replace(/\n/g, '\\n')
3165:         .replace(/\r/g, '\\r');
3166: }

3172: function handleSelectAssetsFolder() {
3173:     if (typeof window.cep !== 'undefined' && window.cep.fs) {
3174:         try {
3175:             const result = window.cep.fs.showOpenDialogEx(
3176:                 false, true, 'Select Assets Folder', '', []
3177:             );
3178: 
3179:             if (result.err === 0 && result.data && result.data.length > 0) {
3180:                 appState.assetsRootPath = result.data[0].replace(/\\/g, '/') + '/';
3181:                 updateAssetsDisplay();
3182:                 setStatus('Assets folder set', 'success');
3183:             }
3184:         } catch (e) {
3185:             setStatus('Error selecting folder', 'error');
3186:         }
3187:     } else {
3188:         const path = prompt('Enter assets folder path:', appState.deckPath || 'D:/Assets');
3189:         if (path) {
3190:             appState.assetsRootPath = path.replace(/\\/g, '/') + '/';
3191:             updateAssetsDisplay();
3192:         }
3193:     }
3194: }

3291: function handleLoadProject(e) {
3292:     const file = e.target.files[0];
3293:     if (!file) return;
3294: 
3295:     const reader = new FileReader();
3296:     reader.onload = (event) => {
3297:         try {
3298:             const projectData = JSON.parse(event.target.result);
3299: 
3300:             // Restore app state
3301:             appState.deckPath = projectData.deckPath || null;
3302:             appState.assetsRootPath = projectData.assetsRootPath || null;
3303:             appState.stepBlending = projectData.stepBlending || 0;
3304:             appState.dealSpeed = projectData.dealSpeed || 3;
3305:             appState.boardLayout = projectData.boardLayout || appState.boardLayout;
3306:             // Fallback for old projects without slotGroups
3307:             if (!appState.boardLayout.slotGroups) {
3308:                 appState.boardLayout.slotGroups = [];
3309:             }
3310: 
3311:             // Restore cards
3312:             appState.tableCards = projectData.tableCards || [];
3313:             appState.trayCards = projectData.trayCards || [];
3314: 
3315:             // Restore scenario
3316:             if (projectData.scenarioData) {
3317:                 scenarioData.initialState = projectData.scenarioData.initialState || {};
3318:                 scenarioData.scenario = projectData.scenarioData.scenario || [];
3319:             }
3320: 
3321:             // Restore snapshots
3322:             if (projectData.stepSnapshots) {
3323:                 stepSnapshots.length = 0;
3324:                 projectData.stepSnapshots.forEach(s => stepSnapshots.push(s));
3325:             }
3326: 
3327:             // Update UI
3328:             updateAssetsDisplay();
3329:             if (projectData.stepBlending) {
3330:                 const slider = document.getElementById('stepBlendingSlider');
3331:                 const value = document.getElementById('stepBlendingValue');
3332:                 if (slider) slider.value = projectData.stepBlending;
3333:                 if (value) value.textContent = projectData.stepBlending + '%';
3334:             }
3335:             if (projectData.dealSpeed) {
3336:                 const dealSlider = document.getElementById('dealSpeedSlider');
3337:                 const dealValue = document.getElementById('dealSpeedValue');
3338:                 if (dealSlider) dealSlider.value = projectData.dealSpeed;
3339:                 if (dealValue) dealValue.textContent = projectData.dealSpeed + 'f/card';
3340:             }
3341: 
3342:             // Re-render cards on table
3343:             restoreFromSnapshot(stepSnapshots[stepSnapshots.length - 1] || {});
3344: 
3345:             // Update tray
3346:             renderCardTray();
3347:             renderTimeline();
3348:             updateUI();
3349: 
3350:             setStatus('Project loaded!', 'success');
3351:         } catch (err) {
3352:             setStatus('Failed to load project: ' + err.message, 'error');
3353:             console.error('Load project error:', err);
3354:         }
3355:     };
3356:     reader.readAsText(file);
3357: 
3358:     // Reset file input
3359:     e.target.value = '';
3360: }

3366: function renderTimeline() {
3367:     // Use new TimelineUI if available
3368:     if (typeof timelineUI !== 'undefined' && timelineUI !== null) {
3369:         // Sync timing data first
3370:         syncTimelineModulesWithSteps();
3371:         return;
3372:     }
3373: 
3374:     // Fallback to old rendering if TimelineUI not loaded
3375:     timelinePreview.innerHTML = '';
3376: 
3377:     scenarioData.scenario.forEach((step, index) => {
3378:         const el = document.createElement('div');
3379:         el.className = 'timeline-step';
3380:         if (step.actions.length > 0) el.classList.add('has-actions');
3381: 
3382:         // Step number
3383:         const stepNum = document.createElement('span');
3384:         stepNum.textContent = step.stepId;
3385:         el.appendChild(stepNum);
3386: 
3387:         // Action buttons container
3388:         const actions = document.createElement('div');
3389:         actions.className = 'step-actions';
3390: 
3391:         // Edit button
3392:         const editBtn = document.createElement('button');
3393:         editBtn.className = 'step-action-btn edit-btn';
3394:         editBtn.innerHTML = '✏️';
3395:         editBtn.title = 'Edit step';
3396:         editBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
3397:             e.stopPropagation();
3398:             handleEditStep(index);
3399:         });
3400:         actions.appendChild(editBtn);
3401: 
3402:         // Delete button
3403:         const deleteBtn = document.createElement('button');
3404:         deleteBtn.className = 'step-action-btn delete-btn';
3405:         deleteBtn.innerHTML = '🗑️';
3406:         deleteBtn.title = 'Delete step';
3407:         deleteBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
3408:             e.stopPropagation();
3409:             handleDeleteStep(index);
3410:         });
3411:         actions.appendChild(deleteBtn);
3412: 
3413:         el.appendChild(actions);
3414:         el.title = `Step ${step.stepId}: ${step.actions.length} actions, ${step.duration}s`;
3415:         timelinePreview.appendChild(el);
3416:     });
3417: 
3418:     // Update replay button state
3419:     if (replayBtn) {
3420:         replayBtn.disabled = scenarioData.scenario.length === 0;
3421:     }
3422: }

3454: // ============================================
3455: // REPLAY FUNCTIONALITY
3456: // ============================================
3457: 
3458: let replayTimer = null;
3459: let isReplaying = false;
3460: let currentReplayStep = 0;
3461: let replaySpeed = 1;  // 1 = normal, 2 = faster, 0.5 = slower
3462: 
3463: function handleReplay() {
3464:     if (scenarioData.scenario.length === 0) {
3465:         setStatus('No steps to replay', 'error');
3466:         return;
3467:     }
3468: 
3469:     if (isReplaying) {
3470:         stopReplay();
3471:         return;
3472:     }
3473: 
3474:     // Check if we have snapshots for replay
3475:     if (stepSnapshots.length === 0) {
3476:         setStatus('No snapshots recorded - please record some steps first', 'error');
3477:         debugWarn('stepSnapshots is empty:', stepSnapshots);
3478:         return;
3479:     }
3480: 
3481:     debugLog('Starting replay with', scenarioData.scenario.length, 'steps');
3482:     debugLog('stepSnapshots:', stepSnapshots);
3483: 
3484: 
3485:     isReplaying = true;
3486:     currentReplayStep = 0;
3487: 
3488:     // Update UI - old controls disabled, using new timeline controls
3489:     // replayBtn.textContent = '⏸️ Pause';
3490:     // replayControls.classList.remove('hidden');
3491:     // replayProgress.textContent = `Initial / ${scenarioData.scenario.length} steps`;
3492: 
3493:     // Update playhead to start
3494:     updateTimelinePlayhead(0);
3495: 
3496:     // Start replay from initial state
3497:     restoreToInitialState();
3498: 
3499:     setStatus('Showing initial state...', 'recording');
3500: 
3501:     // Give user time to see initial state before stepping
3502:     setTimeout(() => {
3503:         if (isReplaying) {
3504:             setStatus('Replaying steps...', 'recording');
3505:             replayNextStep();
3506:         }
3507:     }, 1000);
3508: }
3509: 
3510: 
3511: function replayNextStep() {
3512:     debugLog('=== replayNextStep ===');
3513:     debugLog('isReplaying:', isReplaying);
3514:     debugLog('currentReplayStep:', currentReplayStep);
3515:     debugLog('scenario.length:', scenarioData.scenario.length);
3516: 
3517:     if (!isReplaying || currentReplayStep >= scenarioData.scenario.length) {
3518:         debugLog('Stopping replay - condition met');
3519:         stopReplay();
3520:         return;
3521:     }
3522: 
3523:     const step = scenarioData.scenario[currentReplayStep];
3524:     debugLog('Playing step:', currentReplayStep + 1, 'duration:', step.duration);
3525:     // Old progress display disabled - using playhead now
3526:     // replayProgress.textContent = `Step ${currentReplayStep + 1}/${scenarioData.scenario.length}`;
3527: 
3528:     // Update playhead position (step start time)
3529:     const playheadTime = step.startTime || currentReplayStep;
3530:     updateTimelinePlayhead(playheadTime);
3531: 
3532:     // Get previous snapshot for start positions
3533:     // stepSnapshots[0] = initial state, stepSnapshots[1] = after step 1, etc.
3534:     const prevSnapshot = stepSnapshots[currentReplayStep];  // Start position
3535:     const targetSnapshot = stepSnapshots[currentReplayStep + 1];  // End position
3536: 
3537:     if (targetSnapshot) {
3538:         debugLog('Animating step from snapshot', currentReplayStep);
3539: 
3540:         // IMPORTANT: First restore cards to previous snapshot position
3541:         // This ensures correct start positions on subsequent replays
3542:         restoreFromSnapshot(prevSnapshot);
3543: 
3544:         // Find cards that changed position (zone changed) or are new
3545:         const movingCards = [];
3546:         Object.entries(targetSnapshot).forEach(([cardId, targetState]) => {
3547:             const prevState = prevSnapshot[cardId];
3548: 
3549:             // New card added from tray (not in previous snapshot)
3550:             if (!prevState) {
3551:                 movingCards.push({
3552:                     cardId,
3553:                     fromZone: null,  // Card is new, no previous zone
3554:                     toZone: targetState.zone,
3555:                     targetState,
3556:                     isNew: true
3557:                 });
3558:             } else if (prevState.zone !== targetState.zone) {
3559:                 // Existing card that moved zones
3560:                 movingCards.push({
3561:                     cardId,
3562:                     fromZone: prevState.zone,
3563:                     fromZonePosition: prevState.zonePosition || 0,
3564:                     toZone: targetState.zone,
3565:                     targetState
3566:                 });
3567:             }
3568:         });
3569: 
3570:         debugLog('Moving cards:', movingCards.length);
3571: 
3572:         if (movingCards.length > 0) {
3573:             // Small delay to let DOM settle after restore, then animate
3574:             setTimeout(() => {
3575:                 animateCardsSequentially(movingCards, targetSnapshot, () => {
3576:                     currentReplayStep++;
3577:                     // Schedule next step
3578:                     const duration = ((step.duration || 1) * 1000) / replaySpeed;
3579:                     debugLog('Scheduling next step in', duration, 'ms (speed:', replaySpeed + 'x)');
3580:                     replayTimer = setTimeout(() => replayNextStep(), duration);
3581:                 });
3582:             }, 50);
3583:         } else {
3584:             // No movement, just restore and continue
3585:             restoreFromSnapshot(targetSnapshot);
3586:             currentReplayStep++;
3587:             const duration = ((step.duration || 1) * 1000) / replaySpeed;
3588:             replayTimer = setTimeout(() => replayNextStep(), duration);
3589:         }
3590:     } else {
3591:         debugWarn('No stepSnapshot at index', currentReplayStep);
3592:         currentReplayStep++;
3593:         replayTimer = setTimeout(() => replayNextStep(), 1000);
3594:     }
3595: }
3596: 
3597: /**
3598:  * Animate cards moving to new positions sequentially
3599:  */
3600: function animateCardsSequentially(movingCards, targetSnapshot, onComplete) {
3601:     const ANIMATION_DURATION = 400; // ms per card
3602:     let index = 0;
3603: 
3604:     // Calculate scale factor to convert UI coordinates (1280x720) to actual container size
3605:     const pokerTable = document.getElementById('pokerTable');
3606:     const tableWidth = pokerTable ? pokerTable.offsetWidth : gameContainer.offsetWidth;
3607:     const tableHeight = pokerTable ? pokerTable.offsetHeight : gameContainer.offsetHeight;
3608:     const scaleX = tableWidth / UI_WIDTH;
3609:     const scaleY = tableHeight / UI_HEIGHT;
3610: 
3611:     debugLog('Animation scale factors:', { scaleX, scaleY, tableWidth, tableHeight, UI_WIDTH, UI_HEIGHT });
3612: 
3613:     function animateNext() {
3614:         if (index >= movingCards.length) {
3615:             // All animations complete, restore final state
3616:             restoreFromSnapshot(targetSnapshot);
3617:             onComplete();
3618:             return;
3619:         }
3620: 
3621:         const move = movingCards[index];
3622:         let card = appState.tableCards.find(c => c.id === move.cardId);
3623: 
3624:         // For new cards (from tray), we need to find or create them
3625:         if (move.isNew && !card) {
3626:             // Find card in tray
3627:             card = appState.trayCards.find(c => c.id === move.cardId);
3628:             if (card) {
3629:                 // Add to table cards
3630:                 appState.tableCards.push(card);
3631:                 appState.trayCards = appState.trayCards.filter(c => c.id !== move.cardId);
3632:             }
3633:         }
3634: 
3635:         if (card) {
3636:             // Create element if it doesn't exist
3637:             if (!card.element) {
3638:                 card.isFaceUp = move.targetState.isFaceUp;
3639:                 const element = createTableCardElement(card);
3640:                 card.element = element;
3641:             }
3642: 
3643:             // Get start and end positions in UI coordinates (1280x720)
3644:             // Use zonePosition from state to get correct offset within zone
3645:             const startPos = move.isNew
3646:                 ? { x: -100, y: UI_HEIGHT / 2 }  // Start from left edge
3647:                 : getUIZonePosition(move.fromZone, move.fromZonePosition || 0);
3648:             const endPos = getUIZonePosition(move.toZone, move.targetState.zonePosition || 0);
3649: 
3650:             // Get poker table offset relative to gameContainer
3651:             const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
3652:             const tableRect = pokerTable ? pokerTable.getBoundingClientRect() : containerRect;
3653:             const offsetX = tableRect.left - containerRect.left;
3654:             const offsetY = tableRect.top - containerRect.top;
3655: 
3656:             // Scale card dimensions as well
3657:             const scaledCardWidth = CARD_WIDTH * scaleX;
3658:             const scaledCardHeight = CARD_HEIGHT * scaleY;
3659: 
3660:             // Remove from zone container, add to gameContainer for free movement
3661:             const cardEl = card.element;
3662:             cardEl.style.position = 'absolute';
3663:             // Scale UI coordinates to actual container size
3664:             cardEl.style.left = `${offsetX + (startPos.x * scaleX) - scaledCardWidth / 2}px`;
3665:             cardEl.style.top = `${offsetY + (startPos.y * scaleY) - scaledCardHeight / 2}px`;
3666:             cardEl.style.zIndex = '200';
3667:             cardEl.style.transition = `left ${ANIMATION_DURATION}ms ease, top ${ANIMATION_DURATION}ms ease`;
3668: 
3669:             // Move to gameContainer if not already there
3670:             if (cardEl.parentElement !== gameContainer) {
3671:                 gameContainer.appendChild(cardEl);
3672:             }
3673: 
3674:             debugLog(`Animating ${card.id}: from (${startPos.x}, ${startPos.y}) to (${endPos.x}, ${endPos.y})${move.isNew ? ' [NEW]' : ''}`);
3675: 
3676:             // Trigger animation
3677:             requestAnimationFrame(() => {
3678:                 cardEl.style.left = `${offsetX + (endPos.x * scaleX) - scaledCardWidth / 2}px`;
3679:                 cardEl.style.top = `${offsetY + (endPos.y * scaleY) - scaledCardHeight / 2}px`;
3680:             });
3681: 
3682:             // Wait for animation, then animate next
3683:             setTimeout(() => {
3684:                 index++;
3685:                 animateNext();
3686:             }, ANIMATION_DURATION + 50);
3687:         } else {
3688:             index++;
3689:             animateNext();
3690:         }
3691:     }
3692: 
3693:     animateNext();
3694: }
3695: 
3696: 
3697: function stopReplay() {
3698:     isReplaying = false;
3699: 
3700:     if (replayTimer) {
3701:         clearTimeout(replayTimer);
3702:         replayTimer = null;
3703:     }
3704: 
3705:     // Reset UI
3706:     replayBtn.textContent = '▶️ Replay Steps';
3707:     replayControls.classList.add('hidden');
3708: 
3709:     setStatus(`Replay finished at step ${currentReplayStep}/${scenarioData.scenario.length}`, 'success');
3710: }
3711: 
3712: function restoreToInitialState() {
3713:     debugLog('=== restoreToInitialState ===');
3714:     debugLog('initialState:', scenarioData.initialState);
3715:     debugLog('tableCards:', appState.tableCards);
3716: 
3717:     // First, remove all card elements from zones
3718:     playerZones.forEach(zone => {
3719:         const container = zone.querySelector('.zone-cards');
3720:         if (container) container.innerHTML = '';
3721:     });
3722:     // Also clear grid drop zones
3723:     document.querySelectorAll('.card-drop-zone .zone-cards').forEach(container => {
3724:         container.innerHTML = '';
3725:     });
3726:     // Clear community zone
3727:     const communityZoneContainer = document.querySelector('.community-zone .zone-cards');
3728:     if (communityZoneContainer) communityZoneContainer.innerHTML = '';
3729: 
3730:     // Clear ALL card elements ANYWHERE in gameContainer (nuclear cleanup)
3731:     // This ensures animated cards are removed regardless of DOM location
3732:     // Must include both .card (table cards) and .zone-card (zone cards) classes
3733:     gameContainer.querySelectorAll('.card, .zone-card').forEach(cardEl => {
3734:         cardEl.remove();
3735:     });
3736: 
3737:     cardArea.innerHTML = '';
3738: 
3739:     // Apply initial state to all cards
3740:     Object.entries(scenarioData.initialState).forEach(([cardId, state]) => {
3741:         const card = appState.tableCards.find(c => c.id === cardId);
3742:         if (!card) {
3743:             debugWarn('Card not found in tableCards:', cardId);
3744:             return;
3745:         }
3746: 
3747:         debugLog(`Restoring card ${cardId} to zone: ${state.zone}`);
3748:         card.x = state.x;
3749:         card.y = state.y;
3750:         card.rotation = state.rotation;
3751:         card.isFaceUp = state.isFaceUp;
3752:         card.zone = state.zone;
3753:         card.zonePosition = state.zonePosition || 0;
3754:         card.element = null;
3755:     });
3756: 
3757:     // Re-create elements ONLY for cards in the initial state
3758:     // Filter tableCards to only include those in initialState
3759:     const initialStateCardIds = Object.keys(scenarioData.initialState);
3760:     const cardsInInitialState = appState.tableCards.filter(c => initialStateCardIds.includes(c.id));
3761: 
3762:     // Sort by zone and zonePosition to ensure correct order
3763:     const sortedCards = cardsInInitialState.sort((a, b) => {
3764:         if (a.zone !== b.zone) return (a.zone || '').localeCompare(b.zone || '');
3765:         return (a.zonePosition || 0) - (b.zonePosition || 0);
3766:     });
3767: 
3768:     debugLog('sortedCards for rendering:', sortedCards.map(c => ({ id: c.id, zone: c.zone })));
3769: 
3770:     sortedCards.forEach(card => {
3771:         try {
3772:             if (card.zone && card.zone !== 'table') {
3773:                 // Use specific selectors to target zone divs (including grid drop zones)
3774:                 const zoneElement = document.querySelector(`.player-zone[data-zone="${card.zone}"], .community-zone[data-zone="${card.zone}"], .card-drop-zone[data-zone="${card.zone}"]`);
3775:                 debugLog(`Creating zone card ${card.id} in zone ${card.zone}, element found:`, !!zoneElement);
3776:                 if (zoneElement) {
3777:                     createZoneCardElement(card, zoneElement);
3778:                 }
3779:             } else if (card.zone === 'table') {
3780:                 debugLog(`Creating table card ${card.id}`);
3781:                 createTableCardElement(card);
3782:             } else {
3783:                 debugWarn(`Card ${card.id} has no valid zone:`, card.zone);
3784:             }
3785:         } catch (err) {
3786:             debugWarn(`ERROR creating card ${card.id}:`, err.message);
3787:             console.error('Full error:', err);
3788:         }
3789:     });
3790: 
3791:     debugLog('=== restoreToInitialState COMPLETE ===');
3792:     updateUI();
3793: }

3797: // ============================================
3798: // EDIT/DELETE STEPS
3799: // ============================================
3800: 
3801: let pendingWarningCallback = null;
3802: 
3803: function handleDeleteStep(stepIndex) {
3804:     if (stepIndex < 0 || stepIndex >= scenarioData.scenario.length) return;
3805: 
3806:     const isLastStep = stepIndex === scenarioData.scenario.length - 1;
3807: 
3808:     if (!isLastStep) {
3809:         // Deleting middle step - warn about subsequent steps
3810:         showWarningModal(
3811:             `Deleting step ${stepIndex + 1} will also delete all ${scenarioData.scenario.length - stepIndex - 1} subsequent steps. Continue?`,
3812:             () => {
3813:                 // Delete this step and all after it, keep steps 0..stepIndex-1
3814:                 scenarioData.scenario = scenarioData.scenario.slice(0, stepIndex);
3815:                 // Keep snapshots 0..stepIndex (need stepIndex+1 snapshots for stepIndex steps)
3816:                 stepSnapshots = stepSnapshots.slice(0, stepIndex + 1);
3817:                 renumberSteps();
3818:                 renderTimeline();
3819:                 updateUI();
3820:                 setStatus(`Deleted step ${stepIndex + 1} and subsequent steps`, 'success');
3821:             }
3822:         );
3823:     } else {
3824:         // Deleting last step - just remove it
3825:         scenarioData.scenario.pop();
3826:         stepSnapshots.pop();
3827:         renderTimeline();
3828:         updateUI();
3829:         setStatus(`Deleted step ${stepIndex + 1}`, 'success');
3830:     }
3831: }
3832: 
3833: function handleEditStep(stepIndex) {
3834:     if (stepIndex < 0 || stepIndex >= scenarioData.scenario.length) return;
3835: 
3836:     const isLastStep = stepIndex === scenarioData.scenario.length - 1;
3837: 
3838:     if (!isLastStep) {
3839:         // Editing middle step - warn about subsequent steps
3840:         showWarningModal(
3841:             `Editing step ${stepIndex + 1} will delete all ${scenarioData.scenario.length - stepIndex - 1} subsequent steps. Continue?`,
3842:             () => {
3843:                 // Delete steps from stepIndex onward, keep steps 0..stepIndex-1
3844:                 scenarioData.scenario = scenarioData.scenario.slice(0, stepIndex);
3845:                 // Keep snapshots 0..stepIndex (snap[stepIndex] = state BEFORE step at stepIndex)
3846:                 stepSnapshots = stepSnapshots.slice(0, stepIndex + 1);
3847:                 renumberSteps();
3848: 
3849:                 // Restore to state before this step
3850:                 if (stepIndex === 0) {
3851:                     restoreToInitialState();
3852:                 } else if (stepSnapshots[stepIndex]) {
3853:                     restoreFromSnapshot(stepSnapshots[stepIndex]);
3854:                 }
3855: 
3856:                 renderTimeline();
3857:                 updateUI();
3858:                 setStatus(`Ready to re-record step ${stepIndex + 1}. Click "Add Step" to start.`, 'success');
3859:             }
3860:         );
3861:     } else {
3862:         // Editing last step - just remove it and restore to the state BEFORE this step
3863:         scenarioData.scenario.pop();
3864: 
3865:         if (stepSnapshots.length > 1) {
3866:             // Pop the end-state snapshot of the removed step
3867:             stepSnapshots.pop();
3868:             // Now the last snapshot is the START state of the removed step
3869:             const prevSnapshot = stepSnapshots[stepSnapshots.length - 1];
3870: 
3871:             if (prevSnapshot) {
3872:                 restoreFromSnapshot(prevSnapshot);
3873:             } else {
3874:                 restoreToInitialState();
3875:             }
3876:         } else {
3877:             restoreToInitialState();
3878:         }
3879: 
3880:         renderTimeline();
3881:         updateUI();
3882:         setStatus(`Ready to re-record last step. Click "Add Step" to start.`, 'success');
3883:     }
3884: }
3885: 
3886: function renumberSteps() {
3887:     scenarioData.scenario.forEach((step, idx) => {
3888:         step.stepId = idx + 1;
3889:     });
3890: }
3891: 
3892: function restoreFromSnapshot(snapshot) {
3893:     debugLog('=== restoreFromSnapshot ===');
3894:     debugLog('snapshot:', snapshot);
3895: 
3896:     // First, remove all card elements from zones
3897:     playerZones.forEach(zone => {
3898:         const container = zone.querySelector('.zone-cards');
3899:         if (container) container.innerHTML = '';
3900:     });
3901:     // Also clear grid drop zones
3902:     document.querySelectorAll('.card-drop-zone .zone-cards').forEach(container => {
3903:         container.innerHTML = '';
3904:     });
3905:     // Clear community zone
3906:     const communityZone = document.querySelector('.community-zone .zone-cards');
3907:     if (communityZone) communityZone.innerHTML = '';
3908: 
3909:     // Clear ALL card elements ANYWHERE in gameContainer (nuclear cleanup)
3910:     // This ensures animated cards are removed regardless of DOM location
3911:     // Must include both .card (table cards) and .zone-card (zone cards) classes
3912:     gameContainer.querySelectorAll('.card, .zone-card').forEach(cardEl => {
3913:         cardEl.remove();
3914:     });
3915: 
3916:     cardArea.innerHTML = '';
3917: 
3918:     // Clear and rebuild groupedCards based on snapshot isSelected
3919:     appState.groupedCards = [];
3920: 
3921:     // Restore each card to its saved state
3922:     Object.entries(snapshot).forEach(([cardId, state]) => {
3923:         const card = appState.tableCards.find(c => c.id === cardId);
3924:         if (!card) {
3925:             debugWarn('Card not found in tableCards:', cardId);
3926:             return;
3927:         }
3928: 
3929:         debugLog(`Restoring card ${cardId} to zone: ${state.zone}`);
3930:         // Restore all properties
3931:         card.x = state.x || 0;
3932:         card.y = state.y || 0;
3933:         card.rotation = state.rotation || 0;
3934:         card.isFaceUp = state.isFaceUp;
3935:         card.zone = state.zone;
3936:         card.zonePosition = state.zonePosition || 0;
3937:         card.flipAction = state.flipAction || false;
3938:         card.slamEffect = state.slamEffect || false;
3939:         card.element = null;
3940: 
3941:         // Track selected cards for grouping
3942:         if (state.isSelected) {
3943:             appState.groupedCards.push(card);
3944:         }
3945:     });
3946: 
3947:     // Re-create elements ONLY for cards in the snapshot
3948:     // Filter tableCards to only include those in the snapshot
3949:     const snapshotCardIds = Object.keys(snapshot);
3950:     const cardsInSnapshot = appState.tableCards.filter(c => snapshotCardIds.includes(c.id));
3951: 
3952:     // Sort by zone and zonePosition to ensure correct order
3953:     const sortedCards = cardsInSnapshot.sort((a, b) => {
3954:         if (a.zone !== b.zone) return (a.zone || '').localeCompare(b.zone || '');
3955:         return (a.zonePosition || 0) - (b.zonePosition || 0);
3956:     });
3957: 
3958:     debugLog('sortedCards for rendering:', sortedCards.map(c => ({ id: c.id, zone: c.zone })));
3959: 
3960:     sortedCards.forEach(card => {
3961:         if (card.zone && card.zone !== 'table') {
3962:             // Use specific selectors to target zone divs (including grid drop zones)
3963:             const zoneElement = document.querySelector(`.player-zone[data-zone="${card.zone}"], .community-zone[data-zone="${card.zone}"], .card-drop-zone[data-zone="${card.zone}"]`);
3964:             debugLog(`Creating zone card ${card.id} in zone ${card.zone}, element found:`, !!zoneElement);
3965:             if (zoneElement) {
3966:                 createZoneCardElement(card, zoneElement);
3967:             }
3968:         } else if (card.zone === 'table') {
3969:             debugLog(`Creating table card ${card.id}`);
3970:             createTableCardElement(card);
3971:         } else {
3972:             debugWarn(`Card ${card.id} has no valid zone:`, card.zone);
3973:         }
3974: 
3975:         // Apply .grouped class if card is selected
3976:         const isCardSelected = snapshot[card.id]?.isSelected || false;
3977:         if (isCardSelected && card.element) {
3978:             card.element.classList.add('grouped');
3979:         }
3980:     });
3981: 
3982:     // Update group count display
3983:     updateGroupCount();
3984:     updateUI();
3985: }

4033: // Open video links in system default browser (CEP panels can't embed YouTube)
4034: function initHelpVideoLinks() {
4035:     if (!helpModal) return;
4036:     helpModal.querySelectorAll('.help-video-card[data-url]').forEach(card => {
4037:         card.addEventListener('click', function () {
4038:             const url = this.getAttribute('data-url');
4039:             if (url) {
4040:                 try {
4041:                     var csInterface = new CSInterface();
4042:                     csInterface.openURLInDefaultBrowser(url);
4043:                 } catch (e) {
4044:                     window.open(url, '_blank');
4045:                 }
4046:             }
4047:         });
4048:     });
4049: }
