4055: /**
4056:  * Show auto-step popup when card is moved in Record mode
4057:  */
4058: function showAutoStepPopup(card, previousSnapshot) {
4059:     if (!autoStepPopup) return;
4060:     if (appState._bulkApplying) return; // Suppress during AI scenario apply
4061: 
4062:     // BUG FIX: Only set pendingChangeSnapshot if not already pending.
4063:     // When multiple cards are selected rapidly (grouping mode), each call overwrites
4064:     // the snapshot, losing the first card's SELECT change. Keeping the ORIGINAL snapshot
4065:     // ensures computeActions detects ALL card changes between snapshot and current state.
4066:     if (!pendingChangeSnapshot) {
4067:         pendingChangeSnapshot = previousSnapshot;
4068:     }
4069:     pendingChangeCard = card;
4070: 
4071:     autoStepPopup.classList.remove('hidden');
4072: 
4073:     // If auto-record is enabled, start countdown to auto-accept
4074:     if (appState.autoRecord) {
4075:         startAutoRecordCountdown();
4076:     }
4077: }
4078: 
4079: /**
4080:  * Hide auto-step popup
4081:  */
4082: function hideAutoStepPopup() {
4083:     if (!autoStepPopup) return;
4084: 
4085:     autoStepPopup.classList.add('hidden');
4086:     pendingChangeSnapshot = null;
4087:     pendingChangeCard = null;
4088: }
4089: 
4090: /**
4091:  * Handle Yes button - create new step automatically
4092:  */
4093: function handleAutoStepYes() {
4094:     debugLog('=== handleAutoStepYes ===');
4095:     debugLog('pendingChangeSnapshot:', !!pendingChangeSnapshot);
4096: 
4097:     if (!pendingChangeSnapshot) {
4098:         debugWarn('No pendingChangeSnapshot, aborting');
4099:         hideAutoStepPopup();
4100:         return;
4101:     }
4102: 
4103:     // Create step automatically
4104:     const endSnapshot = takeSnapshot();
4105:     const actions = computeActions(pendingChangeSnapshot, endSnapshot);
4106: 
4107:     debugLog('pendingChangeSnapshot keys:', Object.keys(pendingChangeSnapshot || {}));
4108:     debugLog('endSnapshot keys:', Object.keys(endSnapshot || {}));
4109:     debugLog('actions computed:', actions.length, actions);
4110: 
4111:     if (actions.length > 0) {
4112:         const newStep = {
4113:             stepId: scenarioData.scenario.length + 1,
4114:             duration: stepDuration ? parseFloat(stepDuration.value) : 1.0,
4115:             actions: actions
4116:         };
4117: 
4118:         // BUG #4 fix: attach pending group order overrides
4119:         if (appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides) {
4120:             newStep.groupOrderOverrides = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides));
4121:             var groups = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || [];
4122:             groups.forEach(function (g) {
4123:                 if (appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides[g.id] !== undefined) {
4124:                     g.groupOrder = appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides[g.id];
4125:                 }
4126:             });
4127:             appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides = null;
4128:         }
4129: 
4130:         scenarioData.scenario.push(newStep);
4131: 
4132:         // Save snapshot for replay and edit restore
4133:         stepSnapshots.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(endSnapshot)));
4134: 
4135:         totalSteps.textContent = scenarioData.scenario.length;
4136:         renderTimeline();
4137:         updateUI();
4138:         debugLog('Step created:', newStep.stepId, 'Total steps:', scenarioData.scenario.length);
4139:         setStatus(`Step ${scenarioData.scenario.length} auto-created with ${actions.length} actions`, 'success');
4140:     } else {
4141:         debugWarn('No actions detected between snapshots');
4142:         setStatus('No changes detected', 'info');
4143:     }
4144: 
4145:     hideAutoStepPopup();
4146: }
4147: 
4148: 
4149: /**
4150:  * Handle No button - revert card to previous position
4151:  */
4152: function handleAutoStepNo() {
4153:     if (!pendingChangeSnapshot) {
4154:         hideAutoStepPopup();
4155:         return;
4156:     }
4157: 
4158:     // Revert all cards to previous snapshot
4159:     restoreFromSnapshot(pendingChangeSnapshot);
4160: 
4161:     // Clear sticky flags only on the card(s) involved in the reverted move.
4162:     // These flags are set via UI checkboxes, not stored in snapshots,
4163:     // and can cause spurious TRANSFORM actions in subsequent steps.
4164:     if (pendingChangeCard) {
4165:         pendingChangeCard.flipAction = false;
4166:         pendingChangeCard.slamEffect = false;
4167:     } else if (appState.groupedCards.length > 0) {
4168:         // Grouped move — clear only the grouped cards
4169:         appState.groupedCards.forEach(card => {
4170:             card.flipAction = false;
4171:             card.slamEffect = false;
4172:         });
4173:     }
4174: 
4175:     // Re-apply "grouped" CSS class to restored grouped cards
4176:     appState.groupedCards.forEach(card => {
4177:         if (card.element) {
4178:             card.element.classList.add('grouped');
4179:         }
4180:     });
4181: 
4182:     setStatus('Changes reverted', 'info');
4183:     hideAutoStepPopup();
4184: }

4189:  */
4190: function triggerAutoStepCheck() {
4191:     if (appState.phase !== 'record') return;
4192:     if (appState.isEditingStep) return; // Don't trigger if manually editing a step
4193: 
4194:     // Take snapshot before showing popup (this becomes the "before" state)
4195:     // Note: The snapshot was taken BEFORE the move in moveCardToZone
4196: }

4202: /**
4203:  * Show context menu next to selected card (Record mode only)
4204:  */
4205: function showCardContextMenu(card) {
4206:     if (!cardContextMenu || !card.element) return;
4207: 
4208:     // Only show in Record mode
4209:     if (appState.phase !== 'record') {
4210:         hideCardContextMenu();
4211:         return;
4212:     }
4213: 
4214:     // Check if popup is disabled by user toggle
4215:     var showToggle = document.getElementById('showContextMenuToggle');
4216:     if (showToggle && !showToggle.checked) {
4217:         hideCardContextMenu();
4218:         return;
4219:     }
4220: 
4221:     // Use pinned position (fixed coords) if available, otherwise default to top-right of game area
4222:     const pinned = _ctxMenuPinnedPos;
4223:     if (pinned) {
4224:         cardContextMenu.style.left = pinned.left + 'px';
4225:         cardContextMenu.style.top = pinned.top + 'px';
4226:     } else {
4227:         // Default: top-right corner of game container
4228:         const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
4229:         cardContextMenu.style.left = (containerRect.right - 320) + 'px';
4230:         cardContextMenu.style.top = (containerRect.top + 10) + 'px';
4231:     }
4232: 
4233:     // Update button states
4234:     updateContextMenuState(card);
4235: 
4236:     // Show/hide group action buttons — show if grouping with 2+ grouped, OR if 2+ cards are on the table
4237:     const tableCardsOnBoard = appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.zone && !c.inTray);
4238:     const hasGroupedCards = appState.groupingMode && appState.groupedCards.length > 1;
4239:     const showAllBtns = hasGroupedCards || tableCardsOnBoard.length >= 2;
4240:     if (ctxGroupDivider) ctxGroupDivider.classList.toggle('hidden', !showAllBtns);
4241:     if (ctxFlipAllBtn) ctxFlipAllBtn.classList.toggle('hidden', !showAllBtns);
4242:     if (ctxSlamAllBtn) ctxSlamAllBtn.classList.toggle('hidden', !showAllBtns);
4243:     if (ctxSpinAllBtn) ctxSpinAllBtn.classList.toggle('hidden', !showAllBtns);
4244: 
4245:     cardContextMenu.classList.remove('hidden');
4246: }

4248: /**
4249:  * Hide context menu
4250:  */
4251: function hideCardContextMenu() {
4252:     if (!cardContextMenu) return;
4253:     cardContextMenu.classList.add('hidden');
4254: }
4255: 
4256: /**
4257:  * Setup drag-to-pin for cardContextMenu (position: fixed, body-level).
4258:  * The entire menu bar is draggable (mousedown on menu background or drag handle).
4259:  * Clicking buttons works normally. Position saved in localStorage.
4260:  * Double-click handle or click reset → unpin (back to default corner).
4261:  */
4262: function setupCtxMenuDrag() {
4263:     if (!cardContextMenu) return;
4264: 
4265:     // Load pinned position from localStorage
4266:     try {
4267:         var saved = localStorage.getItem('ctxMenuPinnedPos');
4268:         if (saved) _ctxMenuPinnedPos = JSON.parse(saved);
4269:     } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }
4270: 
4271:     var handle = cardContextMenu.querySelector('.ctx-drag-handle');
4272:     var resetBtn = cardContextMenu.querySelector('.ctx-reset-btn');
4273: 
4274:     var isDragging = false;
4275:     var didDrag = false;
4276:     var dragOffsetX = 0, dragOffsetY = 0;
4277: 
4278:     // Start drag on mousedown anywhere on the menu (except buttons)
4279:     cardContextMenu.addEventListener('mousedown', function (e) {
4280:         // Only start drag from handle, divider, or menu background — not from buttons
4281:         if (e.target.tagName === 'BUTTON') return;
4282:         e.preventDefault();
4283:         isDragging = true;
4284:         didDrag = false;
4285:         var menuRect = cardContextMenu.getBoundingClientRect();
4286:         dragOffsetX = e.clientX - menuRect.left;
4287:         dragOffsetY = e.clientY - menuRect.top;
4288:         cardContextMenu.classList.add('ctx-dragging');
4289:     });
4290: 
4291:     document.addEventListener('mousemove', function (e) {
4292:         if (!isDragging) return;
4293:         didDrag = true;
4294:         var left = e.clientX - dragOffsetX;
4295:         var top = e.clientY - dragOffsetY;
4296:         // Clamp within viewport
4297:         left = Math.max(0, Math.min(left, window.innerWidth - 50));
4298:         top = Math.max(0, Math.min(top, window.innerHeight - 30));
4299:         cardContextMenu.style.left = left + 'px';
4300:         cardContextMenu.style.top = top + 'px';
4301:     });
4302: 
4303:     document.addEventListener('mouseup', function () {
4304:         if (!isDragging) return;
4305:         isDragging = false;
4306:         cardContextMenu.classList.remove('ctx-dragging');
4307:         if (!didDrag) return; // Only pin if actually dragged
4308:         // Save pinned position
4309:         _ctxMenuPinnedPos = {
4310:             left: parseInt(cardContextMenu.style.left),
4311:             top: parseInt(cardContextMenu.style.top)
4312:         };
4313:         try {
4314:             localStorage.setItem('ctxMenuPinnedPos', JSON.stringify(_ctxMenuPinnedPos));
4315:         } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }
4316:         cardContextMenu.classList.add('ctx-pinned');
4317:         if (resetBtn) resetBtn.classList.remove('hidden');
4318:     });
4319: 
4320:     // Double-click handle or click reset → unpin
4321:     function unpinMenu() {
4322:         _ctxMenuPinnedPos = null;
4323:         try { localStorage.removeItem('ctxMenuPinnedPos'); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }
4324:         cardContextMenu.classList.remove('ctx-pinned');
4325:         if (resetBtn) resetBtn.classList.add('hidden');
4326:         if (appState.selectedCard) showCardContextMenu(appState.selectedCard);
4327:     }
4328: 
4329:     if (handle) {
4330:         handle.addEventListener('dblclick', function (e) {
4331:             e.preventDefault();
4332:             e.stopPropagation();
4333:             unpinMenu();
4334:         });
4335:     }
4336: 
4337:     if (resetBtn) {
4338:         resetBtn.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
4339:             e.preventDefault();
4340:             e.stopPropagation();
4341:             unpinMenu();
4342:         });
4343:         if (_ctxMenuPinnedPos) resetBtn.classList.remove('hidden');
4344:     }
4345: 
4346:     if (_ctxMenuPinnedPos) {
4347:         cardContextMenu.classList.add('ctx-pinned');
4348:     }
4349: }
4350: 
4351: /**
4352:  * Update context menu button active states
4353:  */
4354: function updateContextMenuState(card) {
4355:     if (!card) return;
4356: 
4357:     if (ctxFlipBtn) {
4358:         ctxFlipBtn.classList.toggle('active', card.flipAction || false);
4359:     }
4360:     if (ctxSlamBtn) {
4361:         ctxSlamBtn.classList.toggle('active', card.slamEffect || false);
4362:     }
4363:     if (ctxSpinBtn) {
4364:         ctxSpinBtn.classList.toggle('active', card.spinEffect || false);
4365:     }
4366: }

4368: /**
4369:  * Toggle flip action on selected card
4370:  */
4371: function toggleCtxFlip() {
4372:     if (!appState.selectedCard) return;
4373: 
4374:     appState.selectedCard.flipAction = !appState.selectedCard.flipAction;
4375: 
4376:     // Always flip the card visually when toggle changes
4377:     // Enable flipAction: shows END state (flipped)
4378:     // Disable flipAction: flips back to original state
4379:     flipCard(appState.selectedCard);
4380: 
4381: 
4382:     // Sync with properties panel
4383:     flipCardCheck.checked = appState.selectedCard.flipAction;
4384: 
4385:     // Update button state
4386:     if (ctxFlipBtn) {
4387:         ctxFlipBtn.classList.toggle('active', appState.selectedCard.flipAction);
4388:     }
4389: 
4390:     setStatus(appState.selectedCard.flipAction ? 'Flip animation enabled' : 'Flip animation disabled');
4391: 
4392:     // Auto-hide menu after selection (with brief delay to show state change)
4393:     setTimeout(() => {
4394:         hideCardContextMenu();
4395:     }, 300);
4396: }

4416:

4418:     showAutoStepPopup(appState.selectedCard, beforeSnapshot);

4447: /**
4448:  * Toggle flip action on ALL grouped cards
4449:  */
4450: function toggleCtxFlipAll() {
4451:     // Use grouped cards if in grouping mode, otherwise all table cards on board
4452:     const targetCards = (appState.groupingMode && appState.groupedCards.length > 0)
4453:         ? appState.groupedCards
4454:         : appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.zone && !c.inTray);
4455:     if (targetCards.length === 0) return;
4456: 
4457:     // Determine new state: toggle based on majority
4458:     const enabledCount = targetCards.filter(c => c.flipAction).length;
4459:     const newState = enabledCount < targetCards.length / 2;
4460: 
4461:     targetCards.forEach(card => {
4462:         card.flipAction = newState;
4463:         // Flip visually if state changed
4464:         flipCard(card);
4465:     });
4466: 
4467:     // Update properties panel if selected card is in group
4468:     if (appState.selectedCard && targetCards.some(c => c.id === appState.selectedCard.id)) {
4469:         flipCardCheck.checked = appState.selectedCard.flipAction;
4470:         if (ctxFlipBtn) {
4471:             ctxFlipBtn.classList.toggle('active', appState.selectedCard.flipAction);
4472:         }
4473:     }
4474: 
4475:     setStatus(newState
4476:         ? `Flip animation enabled for ${targetCards.length} cards`
4477:         : `Flip animation disabled for ${targetCards.length} cards`
4478:     );
4479: 
4480:     // Auto-hide menu after selection
4481:     setTimeout(() => {
4482:         hideCardContextMenu();
4483:     }, 300);
4484: }

4583: 
4584: // ============================================
4585: // Z-ORDER UTILITY
4586: // ============================================
4587: 
4588: /**
4589:  * Ensure all card places have a valid zOrder for AE Z-positioning.
4590:  * RULE: Cards visually "in front" (lower on screen / higher row) get HIGHER zOrder.
4591:  * Higher zOrder → more negative Z in AE → closer to camera → in front.
4592:  *
4593:  * Priority:
4594:  * 1. If ANY place already has zOrder → skip (layout manages its own, e.g. Poker/Pusoy)
4595:  * 2. If place has row/col → calculate (row * maxCols) + col
4596:  * 3. Fallback → use array index
4597:  */
4598: function ensureZOrder(cardPlaces) {
4599:     if (!cardPlaces || cardPlaces.length === 0) return;
4600: 
4601:     // Check if ANY place already has zOrder (layout self-manages)
4602:     var hasExistingZOrder = cardPlaces.some(function (p) { return p.zOrder !== undefined; });
4603:     if (hasExistingZOrder) return;
4604: 
4605:     // Find max cols for row-based calculation
4606:     var maxCols = cardPlaces.reduce(function (max, p) {
4607:         return Math.max(max, (p.col || 0) + 1);
4608:     }, 1);
4609: 
4610:     cardPlaces.forEach(function (place, index) {
4611:         if (place.row !== undefined && place.col !== undefined) {
4612:             place.zOrder = (place.row * maxCols) + place.col;
4613:         } else {
4614:             place.zOrder = index;
4615:         }
4616:     });
4617: }
4618: 
4619: // ============================================
4620: // BOARD SETTING FUNCTIONS
4621: // ============================================
4622: 
4623: /**
4624:  * Load preset from file or predefined presets
4625:  */
4626: function handleLoadPreset() {
4627:     const presetValue = presetSelect.value;
4628: 
4629:     // Clean up previous layout before loading new one
4630:     deselectCardPlace();
4631:     clearCardPlaceMarkers();
4632:     clearCardDropZones();
4633:     gameContainer.classList.remove('grid-mode', 'poker-grid-mode');
4634: 
4635:     // Determine effective boardStyle for controls visibility
4636:     let effectiveBoardStyle = presetValue;
4637: 
4638:     if (presetValue === 'poker') {
4639:         loadPokerLayout();
4640:     } else if (presetValue === 'pusoy') {
4641:         loadPusoyLayout();
4642:     } else if (presetValue === 'pusoy-2p') {
4643:         loadPusoyMultiLayout(2);
4644:     } else if (presetValue === 'pusoy-4p') {
4645:         loadPusoyMultiLayout(4);
4646:     } else if (presetValue === 'card-sorting') {
4647:         loadGridLayout(4, 3);
4648:     } else if (presetValue === 'custom') {
4649:         // Start with empty grid (no card places)
4650:         appState.boardLayout = {
4651:             type: 'grid',
4652:             name: 'Custom',
4653:             boardStyle: 'custom',
4654:             gridCols: 4,
4655:             gridRows: 3,
4656:             cardPlaces: [],
4657:             slotGroups: []
4658:         };
4659:         gameContainer.classList.add('grid-mode');
4660:         setStatus('Custom layout - Add card places with buttons above');
4661:     } else if (presetValue.startsWith('saved:')) {
4662:         // Load user-saved layout from localStorage
4663:         const layoutName = presetValue.substring(6);
4664:         const savedLayouts = loadSavedLayouts();
4665:         const data = savedLayouts[layoutName];
4666: 
4667:         if (!data || !data.cardPlaces) {
4668:             setStatus(`Layout "${layoutName}" not found`, 'error');
4669:             return;
4670:         }
4671: 
4672:         // Restore board layout (same logic as autoRestoreBoardLayout)
4673:         appState.boardLayout = {
4674:             type: data.type || 'grid',
4675:             name: data.name || layoutName,
4676:             boardStyle: data.boardStyle || 'custom',
4677:             gridCols: data.gridCols || 4,
4678:             gridRows: data.gridRows || 3,
4679:             cardPlaces: data.cardPlaces,
4680:             slotGroups: data.slotGroups || []
4681:         };
4682: 
4683:         // Restore CSS classes based on boardStyle
4684:         if (data.type === 'grid') gameContainer.classList.add('grid-mode');
4685:         if (data.boardStyle === 'poker') gameContainer.classList.add('poker-grid-mode');
4686: 
4687:         // Restore Pusoy slider values
4688:         if (data.pusoyConfig) {
4689:             const s = document.getElementById('pusoySpacing');
4690:             const c = document.getElementById('pusoyCurvature');
4691:             const l = document.getElementById('pusoyLayerGap');
4692:             if (s) s.value = data.pusoyConfig.spacing;
4693:             if (c) c.value = data.pusoyConfig.curvature;
4694:             if (l) l.value = data.pusoyConfig.layerGap;
4695:         }
4696: 
4697:         // Use effective boardStyle for controls visibility (Gap 2)
4698:         effectiveBoardStyle = data.boardStyle || 'custom';
4699: 
4700:         debugLog(`[SaveLayout] Loaded "${layoutName}" with ${data.cardPlaces.length} places, ${(data.slotGroups || []).length} groups`);
4701:         setStatus(`Loaded layout: ${layoutName}`);
4702:     }
4703: 
4704:     // Toggle Grid Size controls visibility using effective boardStyle (Gap 2)
4705:     toggleGridControlsVisibility(effectiveBoardStyle);
4706: 
4707:     updateCardPlacesList();
4708:     renderCardPlaceMarkers();
4709:     updateGroupPanelVisibility();
4710:     // Auto-trigger Transform Indicator on new layout if it has card places
4711:     if (!document.body.classList.contains('previewing-preset')) {
4712:         if (presetValue !== 'custom' && appState.boardLayout && appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.length > 0) {
4713:             appState.selectedCardPlaces = [...appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces];
4714:             setTimeout(() => {
4715:                 if (typeof syncTransformIndicator === 'function') syncTransformIndicator();
4716:             }, 100);
4717:         }
4718:     }
4719: }
4720: 
4721: function renderGroupPencils() {
4722:     // Clear old pencils
4723:     document.querySelectorAll('.group-pencil-btn, .clone-btn, .group-tools-float, .quadrant-number-watermark').forEach(b => b.remove());
4724: 
4725:     const svgOverlay = document.getElementById('tableQuadrantsOverlay');
4726:     if (svgOverlay) {
4727:         svgOverlay.querySelectorAll('text').forEach(t => t.remove());
4728:     }
4729: 
4730:     if (!appState.boardLayout || appState.phase === 'setup' || !appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces || appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.length === 0) return;
4731:     
4732:     const gameContainer = document.getElementById('gameContainer');
4733:     const pokerTable = document.getElementById('pokerTable');
4734:     if (!gameContainer) return;
4735:     
4736:     let scaleX = 1, scaleY = 1, offsetX = 0, offsetY = 0;
4737:     if (pokerTable) {
4738:         const tableRect = pokerTable.getBoundingClientRect();
4739:         const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
4740:         scaleX = pokerTable.offsetWidth / UI_WIDTH;
4741:         scaleY = pokerTable.offsetHeight / UI_HEIGHT;
4742:         offsetX = tableRect.left - containerRect.left;
4743:         offsetY = tableRect.top - containerRect.top;
4744:     }
4745: 
4746:     const Q_CENTERS = {
4747:         1: { x: 640, y: 720 * 0.78, rot: 0 },
4748:         2: { x: 1280 * 0.20, y: 360, rot: 90 },
4749:         3: { x: 640, y: 720 * 0.22, rot: 180 },
4750:         4: { x: 1280 * 0.80, y: 360, rot: -90 }
4751:     };
4752: 
4753:     let baseQuadrant = -1; 
4754:     let quadrantCreationOrder = 1;
4755: 
4756:     // Map quadrant via slotGroup macros to prevent visual spillover generating multiple pencils/clones
4757:     const quadrantCards = { 1: [], 2: [], 3: [], 4: [] };
4758:     const quadrantOrder = []; 
4759:     
4760:     appState.boardLayout.slotGroups.forEach(g => {
4761:         if (!g.slotIds || g.slotIds.length === 0) return;
4762:         const groupPlaces = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.filter(p => g.slotIds.includes(p.id));
4763:         if (groupPlaces.length === 0) return;
4764:         
4765:         let minX = Infinity, maxX = -Infinity, minY = Infinity, maxY = -Infinity;
4766:         groupPlaces.forEach(p => {
4767:             if (p.x < minX) minX = p.x;
4768:             if (p.x > maxX) maxX = p.x;
4769:             if (p.y < minY) minY = p.y;
4770:             if (p.y > maxY) maxY = p.y;
4771:         });
4772:         const cx = minX + (maxX - minX) / 2;
4773:         const cy = minY + (maxY - minY) / 2;
4774: 
4775:         const dx = cx - 640;
4776:         const dy = cy - 360;
4777:         let q = 1;
4778:         if (Math.abs(dy) / 360 > Math.abs(dx) / 640) q = (dy > 0) ? 1 : 3;
4779:         else q = (dx > 0) ? 4 : 2;
4780: 
4781:         quadrantCards[q].push(...groupPlaces);
4782:         if (!quadrantOrder.includes(q)) {
4783:             quadrantOrder.push(q);
4784:         }
4785:     });
4786: 
4787:     [1, 2, 3, 4].forEach(q => {
4788:         const places = quadrantCards[q];
4789: 
4790:         if (places.length > 0) {
4791:             if (baseQuadrant === -1) baseQuadrant = q;
4792: 
4793:             // Draw Dynamic Watermark Number using a DOM DIV to float above cards
4794:             const WatermarkCenters = {
4795:                 1: { x: 640, y: 580 },
4796:                 2: { x: 230, y: 380 },
4797:                 3: { x: 640, y: 180 },
4798:                 4: { x: 1050, y: 380 }
4799:             };
4800: 
4801:             const watermark = document.createElement('div');
4802:             watermark.className = 'quadrant-number-watermark';
4803:             
4804:             // The number is the chronological order this quadrant was discovered
4805:             const orderIndex = quadrantOrder.indexOf(q) + 1;
4806:             watermark.textContent = String(orderIndex);
4807:             
4808:             watermark.style.position = 'absolute';
4809:             watermark.style.left = `${WatermarkCenters[q].x * scaleX + offsetX}px`;
4810:             watermark.style.top = `${WatermarkCenters[q].y * scaleY + offsetY}px`;
4811:             watermark.style.transform = 'translate(-50%, -50%)';
4812:             watermark.style.fontSize = `${150 * scaleY}px`;
4813:             watermark.style.fontWeight = '900';
4814:             watermark.style.color = '#fff';
4815:             watermark.style.opacity = '0.3';
4816:             watermark.style.zIndex = '900000'; // High enough to sit on top of cards
4817:             watermark.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
4818:             watermark.style.fontFamily = 'monospace';
4819:             watermark.style.textShadow = '0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.8)';
4820:             gameContainer.appendChild(watermark);
4821: 
4822:             const allSelected = places.every(p => appState.selectedCardPlaces && appState.selectedCardPlaces.includes(p));
4823:             if (allSelected && document.body.classList.contains('indicator-active')) return; 
4824: 
4825:             let minX = Infinity, maxX = -Infinity, minY = Infinity, maxY = -Infinity;
4826:             places.forEach(p => {
4827:                 if (p.x < minX) minX = p.x;
4828:                 if (p.x > maxX) maxX = p.x;
4829:                 if (p.y < minY) minY = p.y;
4830:                 if (p.y > maxY) maxY = p.y;
4831:             });
4832:             const cx = minX + (maxX - minX)/2;
4833: 
4834:             const editDomX = cx * scaleX + offsetX;
4835:             const editDomY = (maxY * scaleY + offsetY) + 60;  
4836: 
4837:             const pencilBtn = document.createElement('button');
4838:             pencilBtn.className = 'group-pencil-btn';
4839:             pencilBtn.innerHTML = '✏️ Edit Hand';
4840:             pencilBtn.title = `Edit Hand`;
4841:             pencilBtn.style.left = `${editDomX}px`;
4842:             pencilBtn.style.top = `${editDomY}px`;
4843:             pencilBtn.style.transform = 'translate(-50%, -50%)';
4844:             pencilBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
4845:                 e.stopPropagation();
4846:                 appState.selectedCardPlaces = [...places];
4847:                 renderCardPlaceMarkers();
4848:                 if (typeof syncTransformIndicator === 'function') syncTransformIndicator();
4849:                 renderGroupPencils();
4850:             });
4851:             gameContainer.appendChild(pencilBtn);
4852:         }
4853:     });
4854: 
4855:     if (baseQuadrant !== -1) {
4856:         [1, 2, 3, 4].forEach(q => {
4857:             const places = quadrantCards[q];
4858: 
4859:             if (places.length === 0) {
4860:                 const domX = Q_CENTERS[q].x * scaleX + offsetX;
4861:                 const domY = Q_CENTERS[q].y * scaleY + offsetY;
4862: 
4863:                 const cloneBtn = document.createElement('button');
4864:                 cloneBtn.className = 'clone-btn';
4865:                 cloneBtn.innerHTML = '➕';
4866:                 cloneBtn.title = `Clone layout to this area`;
4867:                 cloneBtn.style.position = 'absolute';
4868:                 cloneBtn.style.left = `${domX}px`;
4869:                 cloneBtn.style.top = `${domY}px`;
4870:                 cloneBtn.style.transform = 'translate(-50%, -50%) scale(1.6)';
4871:                 cloneBtn.style.opacity = '0.7';
4872:                 cloneBtn.style.zIndex = '1000001';
4873:                 
4874:                 cloneBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
4875:                     e.stopPropagation();
4876:                     cloneHandToTargetQuadrant(baseQuadrant, q);
4877:                 });
4878:                 gameContainer.appendChild(cloneBtn);
4879:             }
4880:         });
4881:     }
4882: }
4883: 
4884: function cloneHandToTargetQuadrant(sourceQuad, targetQuad) {
4885:     const Q_CENTERS = {
4886:         1: { x: 640, y: 720 * 0.78, rot: 0 },
4887:         2: { x: 1280 * 0.20, y: 360, rot: 90 },
4888:         3: { x: 640, y: 720 * 0.22, rot: 180 },
4889:         4: { x: 1280 * 0.80, y: 360, rot: -90 }
4890:     };
4891: 
4892:     const sourceQuadDef = Q_CENTERS[sourceQuad];
4893:     const targetQuadDef = Q_CENTERS[targetQuad];
4894: 
4895:     const angleDiff = targetQuadDef.rot - sourceQuadDef.rot;
4896:     const angleRad = angleDiff * Math.PI / 180;
4897:     const cosA = Math.cos(angleRad);
4898:     const sinA = Math.sin(angleRad);
4899: 
4900:     // Identify all source groups purely inside sourceQuad
4901:     const sourceGroupsToClone = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups.filter(g => {
4902:         if (!g.slotIds || g.slotIds.length === 0) return false;
4903:         // Check if the FIRST place is in the sourceQuad
4904:         const p1 = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.find(p => p.id === g.slotIds[0]);
4905:         if (!p1) return false;
4906:         const dx = p1.x - 640;
4907:         const dy = p1.y - 360;
4908:         let placeQ = 1;
4909:         if (Math.abs(dy) / 360 > Math.abs(dx) / 640) placeQ = (dy > 0) ? 1 : 3;
4910:         else placeQ = (dx > 0) ? 4 : 2;
4911:         return placeQ === sourceQuad;
4912:     });
4913: 
4914:     if (sourceGroupsToClone.length === 0) return;
4915: 
4916:     // Determine the centroid of all cards in the source quadrant to spin around mathematically
4917:     let minX = Infinity, maxX = -Infinity, minY = Infinity, maxY = -Infinity;
4918:     sourceGroupsToClone.forEach(g => {
4919:         const places = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.filter(p => g.slotIds.includes(p.id));
4920:         places.forEach(p => {
4921:             if (p.x < minX) minX = p.x;
4922:             if (p.x > maxX) maxX = p.x;
4923:             if (p.y < minY) minY = p.y;
4924:             if (p.y > maxY) maxY = p.y;
4925:         });
4926:     });
4927:     const srcCx = minX + (maxX - minX)/2;
4928:     const srcCy = minY + (maxY - minY)/2;
4929: 
4930:     sourceGroupsToClone.forEach(g => {
4931:         const places = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.filter(p => g.slotIds.includes(p.id));
4932:         const clonedPlaces = [];
4933:         const newSlotIds = [];
4934:         let placeCounter = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.length + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000);
4935: 
4936:         places.forEach(p => {
4937:             // Spin around the mathematical center of the entire hand
4938:             let localX = p.x - srcCx;
4939:             let localY = p.y - srcCy;
4940:             
4941:             // Apply orbit spin
4942:             let rotX = localX * cosA - localY * sinA;
4943:             let rotY = localX * sinA + localY * cosA;
4944: 
4945:             let newId = `place-${Date.now()}-${placeCounter++}`;
4946:             newSlotIds.push(newId);
4947: 
4948:             let newRot = (p.rotation || 0) + angleDiff;
4949:             // Normalize
4950:             while (newRot >= 360) newRot -= 360;
4951:             while (newRot < 0) newRot += 360;
4952: 
4953:             clonedPlaces.push({
4954:                 ...p,
4955:                 id: newId,
4956:                 x: targetQuadDef.x + rotX,
4957:                 y: targetQuadDef.y + rotY,
4958:                 rotation: newRot,
4959:             });
4960:         });
4961: 
4962:         appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.push(...clonedPlaces);
4963: 
4964:         // Remove old 'Clone' texts from name if cloning multiple times, then append targetQuad
4965:         let cleanName = g.name.replace(/ Quadrant \d+/g, '').replace(/ Clone/g, '');
4966:         createSlotGroup(cleanName + ` Quadrant ${targetQuad}`, newSlotIds);
4967:     });
4968: 
4969:     // Reorder groups based on Quadrants if they want:
4970:     // But keeping it as is ensures rendering in order of generation.
4971: 
4972:     renderCardPlaceMarkers();
4973:     updateGroupPanelVisibility();
4974:     setStatus(`Cloned hand to quadrant ${targetQuad}`);
4975: }
4976: 
4977: 
4978: /**
4979:  * Load default poker layout with fixed card slots
4980:  * Each player zone has 13 slots, community has 7
4981:  * Uses grid type so all grid infrastructure (drop zones, z-order, AE export) applies
4982:  */
4983: function generateArrayHand(zoneName, packIndex) {
4984:     const places = [];
4985:     let spacing = 68; // Spread pacing
4986:     // Default spread matches a tight horizontal lineup
4987:     let startX = (UI_WIDTH / 2) - (6 * spacing);
4988:     let startY = 130 + (packIndex * 130);
4989:     let isVertical = false;
4990:     let rotation = 0;
4991:     let stepDirX = 1;
4992:     let stepDirY = 1;
4993: 
4994:     const zOrderBase = packIndex * 100;
4995: 
4996:     for (let i = 0; i < 13; i++) {
4997:         places.push({
4998:             id: 'array-' + zoneName + '-' + i,
4999:             zone: zoneName,
5000:             x: isVertical ? startX : startX + (i * spacing * stepDirX),
5001:             y: isVertical ? startY + (i * spacing * stepDirY) : startY,
5002:             rotation: rotation,
5003:             zOrder: zOrderBase + i,
5004:             label: zoneName.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + (i + 1)
5005:         });
5006:     }
5007: 
5008:     const slotIds = places.map(p => p.id);
5009:     const groupName = 'Hand ' + (packIndex + 1);
5010:     const group = {
5011:         id: 'array-' + zoneName,
5012:         name: groupName,
5013:         slotIds: slotIds,
5014:         groupOrder: packIndex,
5015:         color: getGroupColor(packIndex % 8)
5016:     };
5017: 
5018:     return { places, group };
5019: }
5020: 
5021: /**
5022:  * Load default Array layout (creating just Hand 1 at bottom by default per user rules)
5023:  */
5024: function loadPokerLayout() {
5025:     appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces = [];
5026:     appState.boardLayout.slotGroups = [];
5027: 
5028:     // The logic inside handleAddArrayPack will continue adding arrays if user clicks + Array Pack
5029:     const bottomPack = generateArrayHand('bottom', 0);
5030:     appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.push(...bottomPack.places);
5031:     appState.boardLayout.slotGroups.push(bottomPack.group);
5032: 
5033:     appState.boardLayout.type = 'grid';
5034:     appState.boardLayout.name = 'Array (Hand 1)';
5035:     appState.boardLayout.boardStyle = 'poker';
5036: 
5037:     gameContainer.classList.add('grid-mode');
5038:     setStatus('Loaded Array layout (Hand 1)');
5039: }
5040: 
5041: /**
5042:  * Load Pusoy layout (3-5-5 pyramid formation)
5043:  * Row 0 (top): 3 cards
5044:  * Row 1 (middle): 5 cards  
5045:  * Row 2 (bottom): 5 cards
5046:  * 
5047:  * Z-order: 
5048:  * - Within row: left cards behind, right cards in front
5049:  * - Between rows: bottom row in front of middle, middle in front of top
5050:  */
5051: function loadPusoyLayout() {
5052:     const places = [];
5053: 
5054:     // Use UI coordinate system (1280x720) for consistency with animation/export
5055:     // The positions will be scaled down when rendering to actual DOM size
5056:     const tableWidth = UI_WIDTH;  // 1280
5057:     const tableHeight = UI_HEIGHT; // 720
5058: 
5059:     // Read slider values from DOM (with defaults)
5060:     const spacingSlider = document.getElementById('pusoySpacing');
5061:     const curvatureSlider = document.getElementById('pusoyCurvature');
5062:     const layerGapSlider = document.getElementById('pusoyLayerGap');
5063: 
5064:     const baseSpacing = spacingSlider ? parseInt(spacingSlider.value) : 150;
5065:     const curvature = curvatureSlider ? parseInt(curvatureSlider.value) : 50;
5066:     const layerGap = layerGapSlider ? parseInt(layerGapSlider.value) : 30;
5067: 
5068:     // Fan configuration for each row
5069:     // fanRadius decreases for each row (top row biggest, bottom row smallest)
5070:     // angleSpread scales with curvature slider
5071:     // pivotY increases by layerGap for each row
5072:     // basePivotY of 710 places the 3-5-5 pyramid squarely in the Bottom Box (Box 1)
5073:     const basePivotY = 710; // Starting pivot Y position (adjusted for AE centering)
5074:     const rowConfigs = [
5075:         { row: 0, count: 3, fanRadius: baseSpacing + 30, angleSpread: curvature - 20, pivotY: basePivotY },
5076:         { row: 1, count: 5, fanRadius: baseSpacing, angleSpread: curvature, pivotY: basePivotY + layerGap },
5077:         { row: 2, count: 5, fanRadius: baseSpacing - 30, angleSpread: curvature + 5, pivotY: basePivotY + (layerGap * 2) }
5078:     ];
5079: 
5080:     const centerX = tableWidth / 2;
5081:     let placeIndex = 0;
5082: 
5083:     rowConfigs.forEach(config => {
5084:         const { row, count, fanRadius, angleSpread, pivotY } = config;
5085: 
5086:         // Convert to radians
5087:         const spreadRad = (angleSpread * Math.PI) / 180;
5088:         const startAngle = -spreadRad / 2;  // Start from left
5089:         const angleStep = count > 1 ? spreadRad / (count - 1) : 0;
5090: 
5091:         for (let col = 0; col < count; col++) {
5092:             // Calculate angle for this card (from vertical, -90° = up)
5093:             const angle = startAngle + (col * angleStep);
5094: 
5095:             // Position card using polar coordinates from pivot point
5096:             // X = centerX + radius * sin(angle)
5097:             // Y = pivotY - radius * cos(angle)
5098:             const x = centerX + (fanRadius * Math.sin(angle));
5099:             const y = pivotY - (fanRadius * Math.cos(angle));
5100: 
5101:             // Rotation matches the angle (convert to degrees)
5102:             const rotation = Math.round((angle * 180) / Math.PI);
5103: 
5104:             // Z-order: higher row = front, higher col = front within row
5105:             const zOrder = (row * 10) + col;
5106: 
5107:             places.push({
5108:                 id: `place-${placeIndex}`,
5109:                 x: x,
5110:                 y: y,
5111:                 col: col,
5112:                 row: row,
5113:                 rotation: rotation,
5114:                 zOrder: zOrder,
5115:                 label: String(placeIndex + 1)
5116:             });
5117:             placeIndex++;
5118:         }
5119:     });
5120: 
5121:     // Create a single unified slotGroup for the ENTIRE HAND to enable full-hand dragging/editing
5122:     appState.boardLayout = {
5123:         type: 'grid',
5124:         name: 'Pusoy (3-5-5)',
5125:         boardStyle: 'pusoy',
5126:         gridCols: 5,
5127:         gridRows: 3,
5128:         cardPlaces: places,
5129:         slotGroups: [
5130:             { id: 'pusoy-hand', name: 'Pusoy Hand', slotIds: places.map(p => p.id), groupOrder: 0, color: getGroupColor(0) }
5131:         ]
5132:     };
5133: 
5134:     gameContainer.classList.add('grid-mode');
5135:     setStatus('Loaded Pusoy layout (3-5-5 fan)');
5136: }
5137: 
5138: /**
5139:  * Generate a single Pusoy 3-5-5 fan hand at a given position/orientation.
5140:  * Returns an array of card place objects.
5141:  * @param {string} playerPrefix - ID prefix (e.g. 'p1', 'p2')
5142:  * @param {number} centerX - Pivot X in UI coords
5143:  * @param {number} basePivotY - Pivot Y for top row in UI coords
5144:  * @param {number} orientationDeg - Rotation offset for entire hand (0=bottom, 180=top, 90=left, -90=right)
5145:  * @param {number} scale - Scale factor (1.0 = full size, 0.6 = 60%)
5146:  * @param {number} baseZOrder - Starting z-order for this hand
5147:  * @param {number} baseSpacing - Fan radius from slider
5148:  * @param {number} curvature - Angle spread from slider
5149:  * @param {number} layerGap - Gap between rows from slider
5150:  */
5151: function generatePusoyHand(playerPrefix, centerX, basePivotY, orientationDeg, scale, baseZOrder, baseSpacing, curvature, layerGap) {
5152:     const places = [];
5153:     const orientationRad = (orientationDeg * Math.PI) / 180;
5154: 
5155:     // Hardcode base radius to 300 for a flatter, cinematic arc that exactly matches the default transform_indicator logic.
5156:     // We add yCorrection to the pivot so the cards stay visually grounded at the same vertical coordinates as before.
5157:     const baseRadius = 300;
5158:     const originalRadius = 150; // What the Y offset was originally balanced for
5159:     const yCorrection = baseRadius - originalRadius;
5160: 
5161:     const rowConfigs = [
5162:         { row: 0, count: 3, fanRadius: (baseRadius + 30) * scale, angleSpread: curvature - 20, pivotYOffset: 0 },
5163:         { row: 1, count: 5, fanRadius: baseRadius * scale, angleSpread: curvature, pivotYOffset: layerGap * scale },
5164:         { row: 2, count: 5, fanRadius: (baseRadius - 30) * scale, angleSpread: curvature + 5, pivotYOffset: (layerGap * 2) * scale }
5165:     ];
5166: 
5167:     let placeIndex = 0;
5168: 
5169:     rowConfigs.forEach(config => {
5170:         const { row, count, fanRadius, angleSpread, pivotYOffset } = config;
5171:         const spreadRad = (angleSpread * Math.PI) / 180;
5172:         const startAngle = -spreadRad / 2;
5173:         const angleStep = count > 1 ? spreadRad / (count - 1) : 0;
5174: 
5175:         for (let col = 0; col < count; col++) {
5176:             const angle = startAngle + (col * angleStep);
5177: 
5178:             // Local position relative to pivot (before orientation rotation)
5179:             const localX = fanRadius * Math.sin(angle);
5180:             const localY = -(fanRadius * Math.cos(angle)) + pivotYOffset + (yCorrection * scale);
5181: 
5182:             // Rotate local position by orientation
5183:             const rotatedX = localX * Math.cos(orientationRad) - localY * Math.sin(orientationRad);
5184:             const rotatedY = localX * Math.sin(orientationRad) + localY * Math.cos(orientationRad);
5185: 
5186:             const x = centerX + rotatedX;
5187:             const y = basePivotY + rotatedY;
5188: 
5189:             // Card rotation = fan angle + orientation
5190:             const cardRotation = Math.round((angle * 180) / Math.PI) + orientationDeg;
5191: 
5192:             const zOrder = baseZOrder + (row * 10) + col;
5193: 
5194:             places.push({
5195:                 id: playerPrefix + '-' + placeIndex,
5196:                 x: x,
5197:                 y: y,
5198:                 col: col,
5199:                 row: row,
5200:                 rotation: cardRotation,
5201:                 zOrder: zOrder,
5202:                 label: playerPrefix.toUpperCase() + (placeIndex + 1)
5203:             });
5204:             placeIndex++;
5205:         }
5206:     });
5207: 
5208:     return places;
5209: }
5210: 
5211: /**
5212:  * Load multi-player Pusoy layout
5213:  * @param {number} playerCount - 2 or 4 players
5214:  */
5215: function loadPusoyMultiLayout(playerCount) {
5216:     const spacingSlider = document.getElementById('pusoySpacing');
5217:     const curvatureSlider = document.getElementById('pusoyCurvature');
5218:     const layerGapSlider = document.getElementById('pusoyLayerGap');
5219: 
5220:     const baseSpacing = spacingSlider ? parseInt(spacingSlider.value) : 150;
5221:     const curvature = curvatureSlider ? parseInt(curvatureSlider.value) : 50;
5222:     const layerGap = layerGapSlider ? parseInt(layerGapSlider.value) : 30;
5223: 
5224:     let places = [];
5225:     const slotGroups = [];
5226:     const scale = playerCount === 2 ? 0.75 : 0.55;
5227: 
5228:     let playerPositions = [];
5229:     if (playerCount === 1) {
5230:         playerPositions = [
5231:             { prefix: 'p1', label: 'Player 1 (Bottom)', cx: UI_WIDTH / 2, py: 710, orient: 0 }
5232:         ];
5233:     } else if (playerCount === 2) {
5234:         playerPositions = [
5235:             { prefix: 'p1', label: 'Player 1 (Bottom)', cx: UI_WIDTH / 2, py: 710, orient: 0 },
5236:             { prefix: 'p2', label: 'Player 2 (Top)', cx: UI_WIDTH / 2, py: 10, orient: 0 }
5237:         ];
5238:     } else {
5239:         playerPositions = [
5240:             { prefix: 'p1', label: 'Player 1 (Bottom)', cx: UI_WIDTH / 2, py: 590, orient: 0 },
5241:             { prefix: 'p2', label: 'Player 2 (Top)', cx: UI_WIDTH / 2, py: 130, orient: 0 },
5242:             { prefix: 'p3', label: 'Player 3 (Left)', cx: UI_WIDTH / 2, py: 280, orient: 0 },
5243:             { prefix: 'p4', label: 'Player 4 (Right)', cx: UI_WIDTH / 2, py: 430, orient: 0 }
5244:         ];
5245:     }
5246: 
5247:     playerPositions.forEach((pos, idx) => {
5248:         const hand = generatePusoyHand(
5249:             pos.prefix, pos.cx, pos.py, pos.orient, scale,
5250:             idx * 100, baseSpacing, curvature, layerGap
5251:         );
5252:         places = places.concat(hand);
5253: 
5254:         // Create a single unified slotGroup for the ENTIRE player hand
5255:         slotGroups.push({
5256:             id: pos.prefix + '-hand', name: pos.label,
5257:             slotIds: hand.map(p => p.id), groupOrder: idx, color: getGroupColor(idx)
5258:         });
5259:     });
5260: 
5261:     const presetName = 'Pusoy ' + playerCount + 'P';
5262:     appState.boardLayout = {
5263:         type: 'grid',
5264:         name: presetName,
5265:         boardStyle: 'pusoy',
5266:         gridCols: 5,
5267:         gridRows: 3 * playerCount,
5268:         cardPlaces: places,
5269:         slotGroups: slotGroups
5270:     };
5271: 
5272:     gameContainer.classList.add('grid-mode');
5273:     setStatus('Loaded ' + presetName + ' layout (' + places.length + ' slots)');
5274: }

5276: /**
5277:  * Setup Pusoy layout slider controls and visibility toggle
5278:  */
5279: function setupPusoySliderControls() {
5280:     const pusoyControls = document.getElementById('pusoyControls');
5281:     const presetSelect = document.getElementById('presetSelect');
5282:     const loadPresetBtn = document.getElementById('loadPresetBtn');
5283: 
5284:     const spacingSlider = document.getElementById('pusoySpacing');
5285:     const curvatureSlider = document.getElementById('pusoyCurvature');
5286:     const layerGapSlider = document.getElementById('pusoyLayerGap');
5287: 
5288:     const spacingValue = document.getElementById('pusoySpacingValue');
5289:     const curvatureValue = document.getElementById('pusoyCurvatureValue');
5290:     const layerGapValue = document.getElementById('pusoyLayerGapValue');
5291: 
5292:     if (!pusoyControls || !presetSelect) return;
5293: 
5294:     // Function to toggle Pusoy controls visibility
5295:     const togglePusoyControls = () => {
5296:         const isPusoy = presetSelect.value.startsWith('pusoy');
5297:         pusoyControls.classList.toggle('hidden', !isPusoy);
5298: 
5299:         // Add Pusoy Pack: visible for both pusoy and custom presets
5300:         const addPusoyPackSection = document.getElementById('addPusoyPackSection');
5301:         if (addPusoyPackSection) {
5302:             const showPack = isPusoy || presetSelect.value === 'custom';
5303:             addPusoyPackSection.classList.toggle('hidden', !showPack);
5304:         }
5305:     };
5306: 
5307:     // Function to update layout when sliders change
5308:     const updatePusoyLayout = () => {
5309:         // Update display values
5310:         if (spacingSlider && spacingValue) {
5311:             spacingValue.textContent = spacingSlider.value;
5312:         }
5313:         if (curvatureSlider && curvatureValue) {
5314:             curvatureValue.textContent = curvatureSlider.value + '°';
5315:         }
5316:         if (layerGapSlider && layerGapValue) {
5317:             layerGapValue.textContent = layerGapSlider.value;
5318:         }
5319: 
5320:         // Regenerate layout if Pusoy is selected
5321:         if (appState.boardLayout.boardStyle === 'pusoy') {
5322:             const currentPreset = presetSelect.value;
5323:             if (currentPreset === 'pusoy-2p') {
5324:                 loadPusoyMultiLayout(2);
5325:             } else if (currentPreset === 'pusoy-4p') {
5326:                 loadPusoyMultiLayout(4);
5327:             } else {
5328:                 loadPusoyLayout();
5329:             }
5330:             renderCardPlaceMarkers();
5331:             renderCardDropZones();
5332:         }
5333:     };
5334: 
5335:     // Show/hide on preset change
5336:     presetSelect.addEventListener('change', () => {
5337:         togglePusoyControls();
5338:         toggleGridControlsVisibility(presetSelect.value);
5339:     });
5340: 
5341:     // Show controls after preset is loaded
5342:     if (loadPresetBtn) {
5343:         loadPresetBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
5344:             setTimeout(() => {
5345:                 togglePusoyControls();
5346:                 toggleGridControlsVisibility(presetSelect.value);
5347:             }, 100);
5348:         });
5349:     }
5350: 
5351:     // Slider event listeners
5352:     if (spacingSlider) spacingSlider.addEventListener('input', updatePusoyLayout);
5353:     if (curvatureSlider) curvatureSlider.addEventListener('input', updatePusoyLayout);
5354:     if (layerGapSlider) layerGapSlider.addEventListener('input', updatePusoyLayout);
5355: }

5357: /**
5358:  * Load grid layout with specified columns and rows
5359:  * Uses UI coordinates (1280x720) — consistent with loadPokerLayout/loadPusoyLayout
5360:  */
5361: function loadGridLayout(cols, rows) {
5362:     const places = [];
5363: 
5364:     // Use UI coordinate system (1280x720) for consistency with other layouts
5365:     const spacingX = 100;  // Horizontal spacing between cards in UI coords
5366:     const spacingY = 120;  // Vertical spacing between cards in UI coords
5367:     const totalW = cols * spacingX;
5368:     const totalH = rows * spacingY;
5369:     const startX = (UI_WIDTH - totalW) / 2 + spacingX / 2;
5370:     const startY = (UI_HEIGHT - totalH) / 2 + spacingY / 2;
5371: 
5372:     let placeId = 0;
5373:     for (let row = 0; row < rows; row++) {
5374:         for (let col = 0; col < cols; col++) {
5375:             places.push({
5376:                 id: `place-${placeId}`,
5377:                 x: startX + col * spacingX,
5378:                 y: startY + row * spacingY,
5379:                 col: col,
5380:                 row: row,
5381:                 label: String(placeId + 1)
5382:             });
5383:             placeId++;
5384:         }
5385:     }
5386: 
5387:     appState.boardLayout = {
5388:         type: 'grid',
5389:         name: `Card Sorting (${cols}x${rows})`,
5390:         boardStyle: 'card-sorting',
5391:         gridCols: cols,
5392:         gridRows: rows,
5393:         cardPlaces: places,
5394:         slotGroups: []
5395:     };
5396: 
5397:     // Auto-assign zOrder based on row/col
5398:     ensureZOrder(places);
5399: 
5400:     gameContainer.classList.add('grid-mode');
5401:     setStatus(`Loaded ${cols}x${rows} grid layout`);
5402: }
5403: 
5404: /** 
5405:  * Toggle Grid Size / Card Sorting controls visibility based on preset
5406:  */
5407: function toggleGridControlsVisibility(presetValue) {
5408:     const gridControlsEl = document.querySelector('.grid-controls');
5409:     const cardSortingControls = document.getElementById('cardSortingControls');
5410: 
5411:     const showGrid = (presetValue === 'card-sorting' || presetValue === 'custom');
5412:     if (gridControlsEl) gridControlsEl.classList.toggle('hidden', !showGrid);
5413: 
5414:     const showSorting = (presetValue === 'card-sorting');
5415:     if (cardSortingControls) cardSortingControls.classList.toggle('hidden', !showSorting);
5416: }
5417: 
5418: /** 
5419:  * Snap/redistribute card places using current slider spacing values
5420:  */
5421: function snapCardPlacesToGrid(spacingX, spacingY) {
5422:     const places = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces;
5423:     if (!places || places.length === 0) return;
5424: 
5425:     const cols = appState.boardLayout.gridCols || 4;
5426:     const rows = appState.boardLayout.gridRows || Math.ceil(places.length / cols);
5427: 
5428:     const totalW = cols * spacingX;
5429:     const totalH = rows * spacingY;
5430:     const startX = (UI_WIDTH - totalW) / 2 + spacingX / 2;
5431:     const startY = (UI_HEIGHT - totalH) / 2 + spacingY / 2;
5432: 
5433:     places.forEach((place, idx) => {
5434:         const col = idx % cols;
5435:         const row = Math.floor(idx / cols);
5436:         place.x = startX + col * spacingX;
5437:         place.y = startY + row * spacingY;
5438:         place.col = col;
5439:         place.row = row;
5440:         place.rotation = 0;
5441:         // Recalculate zOrder based on new row/col
5442:         place.zOrder = (row * cols) + col;
5443:     });
5444: 
5445:     renderCardPlaceMarkers();
5446:     updateCardPlacesList();
5447:     updateGroupPanelVisibility();
5448:     setStatus(`Snapped ${places.length} cards to ${cols}×${rows} grid`);
5449: }
5450: 
5451: /** 
5452:  * Reset card sorting sliders to defaults and redistribute
5453:  */
5454: function handleGridResetDefault() {
5455:     const hSlider = document.getElementById('gridHSpacing');
5456:     const vSlider = document.getElementById('gridVSpacing');
5457:     const hValue = document.getElementById('gridHSpacingValue');
5458:     const vValue = document.getElementById('gridVSpacingValue');
5459: 
5460:     if (hSlider) { hSlider.value = 100; if (hValue) hValue.textContent = '100'; }
5461:     if (vSlider) { vSlider.value = 120; if (vValue) vValue.textContent = '120'; }
5462: 
5463:     snapCardPlacesToGrid(100, 120);
5464:     setStatus('Reset grid to default spacing');
5465: }
5466: 
5467: /** 
5468:  * Setup card sorting slider controls (H/V spacing) — similar to Pusoy slider pattern
5469:  */
5470: function setupCardSortingSliderControls() {
5471:     const hSlider = document.getElementById('gridHSpacing');
5472:     const vSlider = document.getElementById('gridVSpacing');
5473:     const hValue = document.getElementById('gridHSpacingValue');
5474:     const vValue = document.getElementById('gridVSpacingValue');
5475:     const resetBtn = document.getElementById('gridResetDefaultBtn');
5476: 
5477:     const updateGridFromSliders = () => {
5478:         const sx = hSlider ? parseInt(hSlider.value) : 100;
5479:         const sy = vSlider ? parseInt(vSlider.value) : 120;
5480:         if (hValue) hValue.textContent = String(sx);
5481:         if (vValue) vValue.textContent = String(sy);
5482: 
5483:         if (appState.boardLayout.boardStyle === 'card-sorting') {
5484:             snapCardPlacesToGrid(sx, sy);
5485:         }
5486:     };
5487: 
5488:     if (hSlider) hSlider.addEventListener('input', updateGridFromSliders);
5489:     if (vSlider) vSlider.addEventListener('input', updateGridFromSliders);
5490:     if (resetBtn) resetBtn.addEventListener('click', handleGridResetDefault);
5491: }

5493: // ============================================
5494: // DEALING CARD CONTROLS
5495: // ============================================
5496: 
5497: /**
5498:  * Setup dealing card toggle and draggable slot
5499:  * When enabled, a card-shaped marker appears on the table
5500:  * to indicate where cards will "deal from" in AE export
5501:  */
5502: function setupDealingCardControls() {
5503:     if (!dealingCardToggle) return;
5504: 
5505:     dealingCardToggle.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
5506:         appState.dealingCard.enabled = e.target.checked;
5507:         const dealSpeedRow = document.getElementById('dealSpeedRow');
5508:         if (e.target.checked) {
5509:             renderDealingSlot();
5510:             if (dealSpeedRow) dealSpeedRow.classList.remove('hidden');
5511:             updateDealTimeEstimate();
5512:             setStatus('Dealing Card enabled — drag the deck marker to position');
5513:         } else {
5514:             removeDealingSlot();
5515:             if (dealSpeedRow) dealSpeedRow.classList.add('hidden');
5516:             setStatus('Dealing Card disabled');
5517:         }
5518:     });
5519: }
5520: 
5521: /**
5522:  * Update the estimated dealing duration display
5523:  * Formula matches AE: ((numCards-1) * staggerFrames + moveFrames + holdFrames) / fps
5524:  */
5525: function updateDealTimeEstimate() {
5526:     const el = document.getElementById('dealTimeEstimate');
5527:     if (!el) return;
5528:     const numCards = appState.tableCards.length;
5529:     if (numCards === 0) {
5530:         el.textContent = '';
5531:         return;
5532:     }
5533:     const stagger = appState.dealSpeed || 3;
5534:     const moveFrames = 10;  // MOVE_DURATION_FRAMES in AE
5535:     const holdFrames = Math.max(5, Math.round(30 / (3 / stagger)));  // Scale hold with speed
5536:     const totalFrames = Math.max(numCards - 1, 0) * stagger + moveFrames + holdFrames;
5537:     const seconds = (totalFrames / 30).toFixed(1);
5538:     el.textContent = '~' + seconds + 's';
5539: }
5540: 
5541: /**
5542:  * Render the dealing card slot marker on the game container
5543:  * This is a draggable deck-shaped element
5544:  */
5545: function renderDealingSlot() {
5546:     // Remove existing if any
5547:     removeDealingSlot();
5548: 
5549:     const marker = document.createElement('div');
5550:     marker.id = 'dealingSlotMarker';
5551:     marker.className = 'dealing-card-slot';
5552:     marker.innerHTML = '🃏<span>DEAL</span>';
5553:     marker.title = 'Drag to reposition dealing slot';
5554: 
5555:     // Delete button
5556:     const deleteBtn = document.createElement('button');
5557:     deleteBtn.className = 'marker-delete';
5558:     deleteBtn.textContent = '✕';
5559:     deleteBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
5560:         e.stopPropagation();
5561:         appState.dealingCard.enabled = false;
5562:         if (dealingCardToggle) dealingCardToggle.checked = false;
5563:         removeDealingSlot();
5564:         updateDealingSlotButton();
5565:         setStatus('Dealing Card removed');
5566:     });
5567:     marker.appendChild(deleteBtn);
5568: 
5569:     // Position using UI coordinates → DOM pixel coordinates
5570:     const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
5571:     const scaleX = containerRect.width / UI_WIDTH;
5572:     const scaleY = containerRect.height / UI_HEIGHT;
5573: 
5574:     marker.style.left = (appState.dealingCard.x * scaleX) + 'px';
5575:     marker.style.top = (appState.dealingCard.y * scaleY) + 'px';
5576: 
5577:     // Make draggable
5578:     let isDragging = false;
5579:     let offsetX = 0, offsetY = 0;
5580: 
5581:     marker.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
5582:         e.preventDefault();
5583:         e.stopPropagation();
5584:         isDragging = true;
5585:         // When .dragging is added, transform: translate(-50%, -50%) is removed
5586:         // Compensate by adjusting left/top so the marker doesn't jump
5587:         const markerW = marker.offsetWidth;
5588:         const markerH = marker.offsetHeight;
5589:         const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
5590:         const currentLeft = parseFloat(marker.style.left) || 0;
5591:         const currentTop = parseFloat(marker.style.top) || 0;
5592:         // Before dragging: CSS position is center, transform shifts -50%,-50%
5593:         // After dragging: no transform, so position should be at top-left corner
5594:         const adjustedLeft = currentLeft - markerW / 2;
5595:         const adjustedTop = currentTop - markerH / 2;
5596:         marker.style.left = adjustedLeft + 'px';
5597:         marker.style.top = adjustedTop + 'px';
5598:         marker.classList.add('dragging');
5599:         // Offset from mouse to marker top-left corner
5600:         offsetX = e.clientX - containerRect.left - adjustedLeft;
5601:         offsetY = e.clientY - containerRect.top - adjustedTop;
5602:     });
5603: 
5604:     document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
5605:         if (!isDragging) return;
5606:         const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
5607:         const x = e.clientX - containerRect.left - offsetX;
5608:         const y = e.clientY - containerRect.top - offsetY;
5609: 
5610:         marker.style.left = x + 'px';
5611:         marker.style.top = y + 'px';
5612: 
5613:         // Update UI coordinates
5614:         const scaleX = containerRect.width / UI_WIDTH;
5615:         const scaleY = containerRect.height / UI_HEIGHT;
5616:         appState.dealingCard.x = Math.round(x / scaleX);
5617:         appState.dealingCard.y = Math.round(y / scaleY);
5618:     });
5619: 
5620:     document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
5621:         if (isDragging) {
5622:             isDragging = false;
5623:             // Convert back to center-based positioning (CSS transform: translate(-50%, -50%))
5624:             const currentLeft = parseFloat(marker.style.left) || 0;
5625:             const currentTop = parseFloat(marker.style.top) || 0;
5626:             const markerW = marker.offsetWidth;
5627:             const markerH = marker.offsetHeight;
5628:             marker.style.left = (currentLeft + markerW / 2) + 'px';
5629:             marker.style.top = (currentTop + markerH / 2) + 'px';
5630:             marker.classList.remove('dragging');
5631:             console.log('[DealingCard] Position:', appState.dealingCard.x, appState.dealingCard.y);
5632:         }
5633:     });
5634: 
5635:     gameContainer.appendChild(marker);
5636: }

5644: }
