5737: /**
5738:  * Save current layout as preset JSON
5739:  * Serializes full board state: cardPlaces (with zone, clonerId), slotGroups, boardStyle, pusoyConfig
5740:  */
5741: function handleSavePreset() {
5742:     const name = presetName.value.trim() || 'Custom Layout';
5743: 
5744:     const presetData = {
5745:         name: name,
5746:         type: appState.boardLayout.type,
5747:         boardStyle: appState.boardLayout.boardStyle,
5748:         description: `Saved preset: ${name}`,
5749:         gridCols: appState.boardLayout.gridCols,
5750:         gridRows: appState.boardLayout.gridRows,
5751:         cardPlaces: appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.map(p => {
5752:             const placeData = {
5753:                 id: p.id,
5754:                 x: Math.round(p.x),
5755:                 y: Math.round(p.y),
5756:                 col: p.col,
5757:                 row: p.row,
5758:                 rotation: p.rotation || 0,
5759:                 zOrder: p.zOrder,
5760:                 label: p.label,
5761:                 zone: p.zone || null
5762:             };
5763:             // Serialize community zone fields
5764:             if (p.isCommunityZone) {
5765:                 placeData.isCommunityZone = true;
5766:                 placeData.czMode = p.czMode || 'row';
5767:                 placeData.czWidth = p.czWidth || 300;
5768:                 placeData.czHeight = p.czHeight || 120;
5769:             }
5770:             // Serialize cloner reference
5771:             if (p.clonerId) placeData.clonerId = p.clonerId;
5772:             return placeData;
5773:         }),
5774:         // Serialize slot groups (cloner groups, pusoy packs, user groups)
5775:         slotGroups: (appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || []).map(g => {
5776:             const group = { ...g };
5777:             if (g.clonerConfig) group.clonerConfig = { ...g.clonerConfig };
5778:             return group;
5779:         }),
5780:         // Save Pusoy slider values if applicable
5781:         pusoyConfig: null
5782:     };
5783: 
5784:     // Capture Pusoy slider state
5785:     if (presetData.boardStyle === 'pusoy') {
5786:         const s = document.getElementById('pusoySpacing');
5787:         const c = document.getElementById('pusoyCurvature');
5788:         const l = document.getElementById('pusoyLayerGap');
5789:         presetData.pusoyConfig = {
5790:             spacing: s ? parseInt(s.value) : 150,
5791:             curvature: c ? parseInt(c.value) : 50,
5792:             layerGap: l ? parseInt(l.value) : 30
5793:         };
5794:     }
5795: 
5796:     // Always save to localStorage for persistence
5797:     saveLayoutToStorage(name, presetData);
5798:     refreshSavedLayoutsDropdown();
5799: 
5800:     // Also try to save to file system (CEP mode)
5801:     if (fs && appState.decksFolder) {
5802:         const presetsFolder = appState.decksFolder.replace('/decks', '/presets');
5803:         const filename = name.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-') + '.json';
5804:         const filepath = presetsFolder + '/' + filename;
5805: 
5806:         try {
5807:             // Ensure presets folder exists
5808:             if (!fs.existsSync(presetsFolder)) {
5809:                 fs.mkdirSync(presetsFolder, { recursive: true });
5810:             }
5811: 
5812:             fs.writeFileSync(filepath, JSON.stringify(presetData, null, 2));
5813:             debugLog(`[SaveLayout] Also saved to filesystem: ${filepath}`);
5814:         } catch (e) {
5815:             console.error('[SaveLayout] Filesystem write failed:', e);
5816:         }
5817:     }
5818: 
5819:     setStatus(`Layout saved: ${name}`, 'success');
5820:     debugLog(`[SaveLayout] Saved "${name}" — ${presetData.cardPlaces.length} places, ${presetData.slotGroups.length} groups`);
5821: }
5822: 
5823: /**
5824:  * Download preset as JSON file (browser fallback)
5825:  */
5826: function downloadPresetJSON(data, filename) {
5827:     const jsonStr = JSON.stringify(data, null, 2);
5828:     const blob = new Blob([jsonStr], { type: 'application/json' });
5829:     const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
5830: 
5831:     const a = document.createElement('a');
5832:     a.href = url;
5833:     a.download = filename;
5834:     a.click();
5835: 
5836:     URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
5837:     setStatus(`Preset downloaded: ${filename}`, 'success');
5838: }
5839: 
5840: // ============================================
5841: // SAVED LAYOUTS (localStorage persistence)
5842: // ============================================
5843: 
5844: const SAVED_LAYOUTS_KEY = 'autonim_savedLayouts';
5845: 
5846: /**
5847:  * Save a layout to localStorage
5848:  * @param {string} name - Layout name (key)
5849:  * @param {object} data - Full preset data object
5850:  */
5851: function saveLayoutToStorage(name, data) {
5852:     try {
5853:         const layouts = loadSavedLayouts();
5854:         layouts[name] = data;
5855:         localStorage.setItem(SAVED_LAYOUTS_KEY, JSON.stringify(layouts));
5856:         debugLog(`[SaveLayout] Saved "${name}" to localStorage (${Object.keys(layouts).length} total)`);
5857:     } catch (e) {
5858:         console.error('[SaveLayout] Failed to save to localStorage:', e);
5859:     }
5860: }
5861: 
5862: /**
5863:  * Load all saved layouts from localStorage
5864:  * @returns {object} { name: layoutData } map
5865:  */
5866: function loadSavedLayouts() {
5867:     try {
5868:         const json = localStorage.getItem(SAVED_LAYOUTS_KEY);
5869:         return json ? JSON.parse(json) : {};
5870:     } catch (e) {
5871:         console.error('[SaveLayout] Failed to read saved layouts:', e);
5872:         return {};
5873:     }
5874: }
5875: 
5876: /**
5877:  * Delete a saved layout from localStorage
5878:  * @param {string} name - Layout name to delete
5879:  */
5880: function deleteSavedLayout(name) {
5881:     try {
5882:         const layouts = loadSavedLayouts();
5883:         delete layouts[name];
5884:         localStorage.setItem(SAVED_LAYOUTS_KEY, JSON.stringify(layouts));
5885:         debugLog(`[SaveLayout] Deleted "${name}" from localStorage`);
5886:     } catch (e) {
5887:         console.error('[SaveLayout] Failed to delete layout:', e);
5888:     }
5889: }
5890: 
5891: /**
5892:  * Refresh the preset dropdown with user-saved layouts from localStorage
5893:  * Adds saved layouts after a separator below built-in presets
5894:  */
5895: function refreshSavedLayoutsDropdown() {
5896:     const select = document.getElementById('presetSelect');
5897:     if (!select) return;
5898: 
5899:     // Remove existing saved layout options and separator
5900:     select.querySelectorAll('.saved-layout-option, .saved-layout-separator').forEach(el => el.remove());
5901: 
5902:     const layouts = loadSavedLayouts();
5903:     const names = Object.keys(layouts);
5904:     if (names.length === 0) return;
5905: 
5906:     // Add separator
5907:     const separator = document.createElement('option');
5908:     separator.disabled = true;
5909:     separator.textContent = '── Saved Layouts ──';
5910:     separator.className = 'saved-layout-separator';
5911:     select.appendChild(separator);
5912: 
5913:     // Add each saved layout
5914:     names.forEach(name => {
5915:         const option = document.createElement('option');
5916:         option.value = `saved:${name}`;
5917:         option.textContent = `📁 ${name}`;
5918:         option.className = 'saved-layout-option';
5919:         select.appendChild(option);
5920:     });
5921: 
5922:     debugLog(`[SaveLayout] Dropdown refreshed with ${names.length} saved layout(s)`);
5923: }
5924: 
5925: // ============================================
5926: // BOARD AUTOSAVE / RESTORE
5927: // ============================================
5928: 
5929: const AUTOSAVE_KEY = 'autonim_boardLayout';
5930: 
5931: /**
5932:  * Get the autosave file path for CEP mode
5933:  * @returns {string|null} File path or null if not in CEP
5934:  */
5935: function getAutosaveFilePath() {
5936:     if (!fs || !csInterface) return null;
5937:     try {
5938:         const extPath = csInterface.getSystemPath(SystemPath.EXTENSION);
5939:         return extPath + '/assets/autosave-board.json';
5940:     } catch (e) {
5941:         return null;
5942:     }
5943: }
5944: 
5945: /**
5946:  * Auto-save current board layout state
5947:  * Called when leaving board-setting phase
5948:  */
5949: function autoSaveBoardLayout() {
5950:     try {
5951:         const data = {
5952:             name: appState.boardLayout.name || 'Autosave',
5953:             boardStyle: appState.boardLayout.boardStyle,
5954:             type: appState.boardLayout.type,
5955:             gridCols: appState.boardLayout.gridCols,
5956:             gridRows: appState.boardLayout.gridRows,
5957:             cardPlaces: appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.map(p => {
5958:                 const place = {
5959:                     id: p.id, x: Math.round(p.x), y: Math.round(p.y),
5960:                     col: p.col, row: p.row,
5961:                     rotation: p.rotation || 0,
5962:                     zOrder: p.zOrder, label: p.label,
5963:                     zone: p.zone || null
5964:                 };
5965:                 if (p.isCommunityZone) {
5966:                     place.isCommunityZone = true;
5967:                     place.czMode = p.czMode || 'row';
5968:                     place.czWidth = p.czWidth || 300;
5969:                     place.czHeight = p.czHeight || 120;
5970:                 }
5971:                 if (p.clonerId) place.clonerId = p.clonerId;
5972:                 return place;
5973:             }),
5974:             slotGroups: (appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || []).map(g => {
5975:                 const group = { ...g };
5976:                 if (g.clonerConfig) group.clonerConfig = { ...g.clonerConfig };
5977:                 return group;
5978:             }),
5979:             // Save Pusoy slider values if applicable
5980:             pusoyConfig: null
5981:         };
5982: 
5983:         // Capture Pusoy slider state
5984:         if (data.boardStyle === 'pusoy') {
5985:             const s = document.getElementById('pusoySpacing');
5986:             const c = document.getElementById('pusoyCurvature');
5987:             const l = document.getElementById('pusoyLayerGap');
5988:             data.pusoyConfig = {
5989:                 spacing: s ? parseInt(s.value) : 150,
5990:                 curvature: c ? parseInt(c.value) : 50,
5991:                 layerGap: l ? parseInt(l.value) : 30
5992:             };
5993:         }
5994: 
5995:         const json = JSON.stringify(data, null, 2);
5996: 
5997:         // CEP mode: write to filesystem
5998:         const filepath = getAutosaveFilePath();
5999:         if (filepath && fs) {
6000:             fs.writeFileSync(filepath, json);
6001:             debugLog(`[Autosave] Saved board layout to ${filepath}`);
6002:         }
6003: 
6004:         // Also save to localStorage as fallback / browser mode
6005:         try {
6006:             localStorage.setItem(AUTOSAVE_KEY, json);
6007:         } catch (e) { /* ignore quota errors */ }
6008: 
6009:     } catch (e) {
6010:         console.error('[Autosave] Failed to save board layout:', e);
6011:     }
6012: }
6013: 
6014: /**
6015:  * Attempt to restore board layout from autosave
6016:  * @returns {boolean} true if restored successfully
6017:  */
6018: function autoRestoreBoardLayout() {
6019:     try {
6020:         let json = null;
6021: 
6022:         // Try filesystem first (CEP mode)
6023:         const filepath = getAutosaveFilePath();
6024:         if (filepath && fs && fs.existsSync(filepath)) {
6025:             json = fs.readFileSync(filepath, 'utf8');
6026:             debugLog('[Autosave] Loaded board from filesystem');
6027:         }
6028: 
6029:         // Fallback to localStorage (browser mode)
6030:         if (!json) {
6031:             json = localStorage.getItem(AUTOSAVE_KEY);
6032:             if (json) debugLog('[Autosave] Loaded board from localStorage');
6033:         }
6034: 
6035:         if (!json) return false;
6036: 
6037:         const data = JSON.parse(json);
6038:         if (!data.cardPlaces || data.cardPlaces.length === 0) return false;
6039: 
6040:         // Restore board layout
6041:         appState.boardLayout = {
6042:             type: data.type || 'grid',
6043:             name: data.name || 'Restored Layout',
6044:             boardStyle: data.boardStyle || 'custom',
6045:             gridCols: data.gridCols || 4,
6046:             gridRows: data.gridRows || 3,
6047:             cardPlaces: data.cardPlaces,
6048:             slotGroups: data.slotGroups || []
6049:         };
6050: 
6051:         // Restore Pusoy slider values
6052:         if (data.pusoyConfig) {
6053:             const s = document.getElementById('pusoySpacing');
6054:             const c = document.getElementById('pusoyCurvature');
6055:             const l = document.getElementById('pusoyLayerGap');
6056:             if (s) s.value = data.pusoyConfig.spacing;
6057:             if (c) c.value = data.pusoyConfig.curvature;
6058:             if (l) l.value = data.pusoyConfig.layerGap;
6059:         }
6060: 
6061:         // Update preset selector to match restored layout
6062:         const presetSelect = document.getElementById('presetSelect');
6063:         if (presetSelect && data.boardStyle) {
6064:             const option = presetSelect.querySelector(`option[value="${data.boardStyle}"]`);
6065:             if (option) presetSelect.value = data.boardStyle;
6066:         }
6067: 
6068:         if (data.type === 'grid') gameContainer.classList.add('grid-mode');
6069:         debugLog(`[Autosave] Restored "${data.name}" with ${data.cardPlaces.length} places`);
6070:         return true;
6071: 
6072:     } catch (e) {
6073:         console.error('[Autosave] Failed to restore board layout:', e);
6074:         return false;
6075:     }
6076: }
6077: 
6078: /**
6079:  * Render card place markers on the game container
6080:  */
6081: function renderCardPlaceMarkers() {
6082:     // Clear existing markers
6083:     clearCardPlaceMarkers();
6084: 
6085:     if (appState.boardLayout.type !== 'grid' || appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.length === 0) {
6086:         return;
6087:     }
6088: 
6089:     // Render markers in gameContainer (not pokerTable) so they appear above the table
6090:     if (!gameContainer) return;
6091: 
6092:     // Get poker table position for offset calculation
6093:     const pokerTable = document.getElementById('pokerTable');
6094:     if (!pokerTable) return;
6095: 
6096:     const tableRect = pokerTable.getBoundingClientRect();
6097:     const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
6098:     const tableWidth = pokerTable.offsetWidth;
6099:     const tableHeight = pokerTable.offsetHeight;
6100: 
6101:     // Calculate offset from gameContainer to pokerTable
6102:     const offsetX = tableRect.left - containerRect.left;
6103:     const offsetY = tableRect.top - containerRect.top;
6104: 
6105:     // Scale factors to convert UI coordinates (1280x720) to actual DOM size
6106:     const scaleX = tableWidth / UI_WIDTH;
6107:     const scaleY = tableHeight / UI_HEIGHT;
6108: 
6109:     appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.forEach((place, index) => {
6110:         const marker = document.createElement('div');
6111:         marker.className = 'card-place-marker';
6112:         marker.dataset.placeId = place.id;
6113:         marker.dataset.zone = `grid-${place.id}`;
6114: 
6115:         // Scale UI coordinates to DOM pixels, then position relative to gameContainer
6116:         const scaledX = place.x * scaleX;
6117:         const scaledY = place.y * scaleY;
6118: 
6119:         if (place.isCommunityZone) {
6120:             // Community zone: use czWidth/czHeight scaled
6121:             marker.classList.add('community-zone-marker');
6122:             const markerW = (place.czWidth || 300) * scaleX;
6123:             const markerH = (place.czHeight || 120) * scaleY;
6124:             marker.style.width = `${markerW}px`;
6125:             marker.style.height = `${markerH}px`;
6126:             marker.style.left = `${offsetX + scaledX - markerW / 2}px`;
6127:             marker.style.top = `${offsetY + scaledY - markerH / 2}px`;
6128:         } else {
6129:             // Normal slot: card-sized
6130:             marker.style.left = `${offsetX + scaledX - (CARD_WIDTH * scaleX) / 2}px`;
6131:             marker.style.top = `${offsetY + scaledY - (CARD_HEIGHT * scaleY) / 2}px`;
6132:         }
6133: 
6134:         // Apply rotation and z-order for Pusoy layout
6135:         if (place.rotation) {
6136:             marker.style.transform = `rotate(${place.rotation}deg)`;
6137:         }
6138:         if (place.zOrder !== undefined) {
6139:             marker.style.zIndex = String(computeFinalZOrder(place) + 10);
6140:         }
6141: 
6142:         // Group color coding
6143:         var placeGroup = getGroupForPlace(place.id);
6144:         if (placeGroup) {
6145:             marker.style.borderColor = placeGroup.color;
6146:             marker.title = placeGroup.name + ' (z:' + computeFinalZOrder(place) + ')';
6147:         }
6148: 
6149:         // Place number / label
6150:         const number = document.createElement('span');
6151:         number.className = 'place-number';
6152:         number.textContent = place.label || String(index + 1);
6153:         marker.appendChild(number);
6154: 
6155:         // Community zone: add mode badge + cycle button
6156:         if (place.isCommunityZone) {
6157:             const modeBadge = document.createElement('span');
6158:             modeBadge.className = 'cz-mode-badge';
6159:             modeBadge.textContent = (place.czMode || 'row').toUpperCase();
6160:             marker.appendChild(modeBadge);
6161: 
6162:             // Mode cycle button
6163:             const modeBtn = document.createElement('button');
6164:             modeBtn.className = 'cz-mode-btn';
6165:             modeBtn.textContent = '🔄';
6166:             modeBtn.title = 'Cycle mode: Row → Pile → Stack';
6167:             modeBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
6168:                 e.stopPropagation();
6169:                 const modes = ['row', 'pile', 'stack'];
6170:                 const currentIdx = modes.indexOf(place.czMode || 'row');
6171:                 place.czMode = modes[(currentIdx + 1) % modes.length];
6172:                 modeBadge.textContent = place.czMode.toUpperCase();
6173:                 debugLog(`[CommunityZone] ${place.id} mode → ${place.czMode}`);
6174:             });
6175:             marker.appendChild(modeBtn);
6176: 
6177:             // Resize handle (bottom-right)
6178:             const resizeHandle = document.createElement('div');
6179:             resizeHandle.className = 'cz-resize-handle';
6180:             resizeHandle.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => startResizeCommunityZone(e, place, marker, scaleX, scaleY));
6181:             marker.appendChild(resizeHandle);
6182:         }
6183: 
6184:         // Delete button
6185:         const deleteBtn = document.createElement('button');
6186:         deleteBtn.className = 'marker-delete';
6187:         deleteBtn.textContent = '✕';
6188:         deleteBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
6189:             e.stopPropagation();
6190:             deleteCardPlace(place.id);
6191:         });
6192:         marker.appendChild(deleteBtn);
6193: 
6194:         // Add zone-cards container to receive visual cards!
6195:         const cardsContainer = document.createElement('div');
6196:         cardsContainer.className = 'zone-cards';
6197:         cardsContainer.style.pointerEvents = 'none'; // Don't block dragging the marker itself
6198:         marker.appendChild(cardsContainer);
6199: 
6200:         // Rotation handle (bottom-left) — only for normal slots, not CZ
6201:         if (!place.isCommunityZone) {
6202:             const rotateHandle = document.createElement('div');
6203:             rotateHandle.className = 'marker-rotate';
6204:             rotateHandle.title = 'Drag to rotate';
6205:             rotateHandle.textContent = '↻';
6206:             rotateHandle.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => startRotateMarker(e, place, marker));
6207:             marker.appendChild(rotateHandle);
6208:         }
6209: 
6210:         // Make draggable (pass event for group drag detection)
6211:         marker.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
6212:             if (e.target.classList.contains('marker-delete') || e.target.classList.contains('cz-mode-btn') || e.target.classList.contains('cz-resize-handle') || e.target.classList.contains('marker-rotate')) return;
6213:             startDragMarker(e, place, marker);
6214:         });
6215: 
6216:         // Click to select (Shift+Click for multi-select)
6217:         marker.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
6218:             if (e.target.classList.contains('marker-delete') || e.target.classList.contains('cz-mode-btn')) return;
6219: 
6220:             if (e.shiftKey) {
6221:                 // Shift+Click: toggle this marker in multi-select
6222:                 // If multi-select is empty but there's a single selected marker, add it first
6223:                 if (appState.selectedCardPlaces.length === 0 && appState.selectedCardPlace) {
6224:                     appState.selectedCardPlaces.push(appState.selectedCardPlace);
6225:                     const prevMarker = document.querySelector(`.card-place-marker[data-place-id="${appState.selectedCardPlace.id}"]`);
6226:                     if (prevMarker) prevMarker.classList.add('multi-selected');
6227:                 }
6228:                 const idx = appState.selectedCardPlaces.indexOf(place);
6229:                 if (idx >= 0) {
6230:                     appState.selectedCardPlaces.splice(idx, 1);
6231:                     marker.classList.remove('multi-selected');
6232:                 } else {
6233:                     appState.selectedCardPlaces.push(place);
6234:                     marker.classList.add('multi-selected');
6235:                 }
6236:                 // Also select for CZ panel
6237:                 selectCardPlace(place, marker);
6238:                 updateCreateGroupBtnState();
6239:                 if (typeof syncTransformIndicator === 'function') syncTransformIndicator();
6240:                 debugLog(`[MultiSelect] ${appState.selectedCardPlaces.length} slots selected`);
6241:             } else {
6242:                 // Normal click: single select, clear multi-select
6243:                 appState.selectedCardPlaces = [];
6244:                 document.querySelectorAll('.card-place-marker.multi-selected').forEach(m => m.classList.remove('multi-selected'));
6245:                 selectCardPlace(place, marker);
6246:                 updateCreateGroupBtnState();
6247:                 if (typeof syncTransformIndicator === 'function') syncTransformIndicator();
6248:             }
6249:         });
6250: 
6251:         // Apply multi-selected class if in selection
6252:         if (appState.selectedCardPlaces.includes(place)) {
6253:             marker.classList.add('multi-selected');
6254:         }
6255: 
6256:         gameContainer.appendChild(marker);
6257:     });
6258:     
6259:     if (typeof renderGroupPencils === 'function') renderGroupPencils();
6260: }
6261: 
6262: /**
6263:  * Clear all card place markers from DOM
6264:  */
6265: function clearCardPlaceMarkers() {
6266:     const markers = document.querySelectorAll('.card-place-marker');
6267:     markers.forEach(m => m.remove());
6268:     
6269:     // Also clear any floating tools/watermarks from board-setting mode
6270:     document.querySelectorAll('.group-pencil-btn, .clone-btn, .group-tools-float, .quadrant-number-watermark').forEach(b => b.remove());
6271:     const svgOverlay = document.getElementById('tableQuadrantsOverlay');
6272:     if (svgOverlay) svgOverlay.querySelectorAll('text').forEach(t => t.remove());
6273: }
6274: 
6275: /**
6276:  * Render card drop zones for Setup mode (non-editable)
6277:  */
6278: function renderCardDropZones() {
6279:     // Clear existing drop zones
6280:     clearCardDropZones();
6281: 
6282:     if (appState.boardLayout.type !== 'grid' || appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.length === 0) {
6283:         return;
6284:     }
6285: 
6286:     if (!gameContainer) return;
6287: 
6288:     // Get poker table position for offset calculation
6289:     const pokerTable = document.getElementById('pokerTable');
6290:     if (!pokerTable) return;
6291: 
6292:     const tableRect = pokerTable.getBoundingClientRect();
6293:     const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
6294:     const tableWidth = pokerTable.offsetWidth;
6295:     const tableHeight = pokerTable.offsetHeight;
6296: 
6297:     const offsetX = tableRect.left - containerRect.left;
6298:     const offsetY = tableRect.top - containerRect.top;
6299: 
6300:     // Scale factors to convert UI coordinates (1280x720) to actual DOM size
6301:     const scaleX = tableWidth / UI_WIDTH;
6302:     const scaleY = tableHeight / UI_HEIGHT;
6303: 
6304:     // --- SETUP PHASE OVERRIDE LOGIC ---
6305:     const isSetupFlatten = (appState.phase === 'setup');
6306:     const placeToGroup = {};
6307:     const placeToLocalIndex = {};
6308:     const groupCardCounts = {};
6309: 
6310:     if (isSetupFlatten && appState.boardLayout.slotGroups) {
6311:         appState.boardLayout.slotGroups.forEach((group, gIdx) => {
6312:             groupCardCounts[gIdx] = group.slotIds.length;
6313:             group.slotIds.forEach((id, localIdx) => {
6314:                 placeToGroup[id] = gIdx;
6315:                 placeToLocalIndex[id] = localIdx;
6316:             });
6317: 
6318:             if (group.slotIds.length > 0) {
6319:                 const totalInGroup = group.slotIds.length;
6320:                 const spacing = 80;
6321:                 
6322:                 // Calculate exactly where the flattened first card box will be rendered
6323:                 const visualStartX = (UI_WIDTH - (totalInGroup - 1) * spacing) / 2;
6324:                 const visualY = 120 + (gIdx * 115);
6325:                 
6326:                 const labelEl = document.createElement('div');
6327:                 labelEl.className = 'setup-row-label';
6328:                 // Soften the color and adjust the size
6329:                 labelEl.innerHTML = `<span style="color: rgba(255,255,255,0.7); font-size: 52px; font-weight: 800; text-shadow: 0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,0.8); line-height: 1;">${gIdx + 1}</span>`;
6330:                 labelEl.style.position = 'absolute';
6331:                 
6332:                 // Place exactly relative to the center of the first card slot
6333:                 // The slot width is ~80 UI pixels, so going -75 from center puts it right beside it
6334:                 const domX = (visualStartX - 75) * scaleX + offsetX; 
6335:                 const domY = visualY * scaleY + offsetY;
6336:                 
6337:                 labelEl.style.left = domX + 'px';
6338:                 labelEl.style.top = domY + 'px'; // Exact vertical center tracking
6339:                 labelEl.style.transform = 'translate(-50%, -50%)'; // Center pivot
6340:                 labelEl.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
6341:                 labelEl.style.zIndex = '50';
6342:                 labelEl.style.display = 'flex';
6343:                 labelEl.style.alignItems = 'center';
6344:                 labelEl.style.justifyContent = 'center';
6345:                 labelEl.style.width = '60px';
6346:                 gameContainer.appendChild(labelEl);
6347:             }
6348:         });
6349:     }
6350: 
6351:     appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.forEach((place, index) => {
6352:         const zone = document.createElement('div');
6353:         zone.className = 'card-drop-zone';
6354:         zone.dataset.placeId = place.id;
6355:         zone.dataset.zone = `grid-${place.id}`;
6356:         
6357:         let finalX = place.x;
6358:         let finalY = place.y;
6359:         let finalRot = place.rotation || 0;
6360: 
6361:         if (isSetupFlatten && !place.isCommunityZone) {
6362:             const gIdx = placeToGroup[place.id];
6363:             const localIdx = placeToLocalIndex[place.id];
6364:             if (gIdx !== undefined && localIdx !== undefined) {
6365:                 const totalInGroup = groupCardCounts[gIdx];
6366:                 const spacing = 80;
6367:                 // Center the group horizontally across UI_WIDTH
6368:                 const startX = (UI_WIDTH - (totalInGroup - 1) * spacing) / 2;
6369:                 finalX = startX + localIdx * spacing;
6370:                 // Distribute groups vertically (approx. 115 spacing per row)
6371:                 finalY = 120 + (gIdx * 115);
6372:                 finalRot = 0;
6373: 
6374:                 // Colorize the drop zone solidly to contrast against the transparent table
6375:                 if (appState.boardLayout.slotGroups[gIdx]) {
6376:                     const groupColor = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups[gIdx].color;
6377:                     const mixPercent = 20 + localIdx * 5; // 20% Base -> darker mix
6378:                     zone.style.borderColor = `color-mix(in srgb, ${groupColor} 100%, black)`;
6379:                     zone.style.background = `color-mix(in srgb, ${groupColor} ${mixPercent}%, #222)`;
6380:                     zone.style.opacity = '1';
6381:                 }
6382:             }
6383:         }
6384: 
6385:         zone.dataset.rotation = String(finalRot);
6386: 
6387:         // Scale UI coordinates to DOM pixels, then position relative to gameContainer
6388:         const scaledX = finalX * scaleX;
6389:         const scaledY = finalY * scaleY;
6390: 
6391:         if (place.isCommunityZone) {
6392:             // Community zone: use czWidth/czHeight
6393:             zone.classList.add('community-zone-drop');
6394:             zone.dataset.czMode = place.czMode || 'row';
6395:             const zoneW = (place.czWidth || 300) * scaleX;
6396:             const zoneH = (place.czHeight || 120) * scaleY;
6397:             zone.style.width = `${zoneW}px`;
6398:             zone.style.height = `${zoneH}px`;
6399:             zone.style.left = `${offsetX + scaledX - zoneW / 2}px`;
6400:             zone.style.top = `${offsetY + scaledY - zoneH / 2}px`;
6401:         } else {
6402:             // Normal slot: card-sized (keep css dimensions to match markers)
6403:             zone.style.left = `${offsetX + scaledX - (CARD_WIDTH * scaleX) / 2}px`;
6404:             zone.style.top = `${offsetY + scaledY - (CARD_HEIGHT * scaleY) / 2}px`;
6405:         }
6406: 
6407:         // Apply rotation and z-order for Pusoy layout
6408:         if (finalRot) {
6409:             zone.style.transform = `rotate(${finalRot}deg)`;
6410:         }
6411:         if (place.zOrder !== undefined) {
6412:             zone.style.zIndex = String(computeFinalZOrder(place) + 10); // +10 to ensure above table
6413:         }
6414: 
6415:         // Zone label
6416:         const label = document.createElement('span');
6417:         label.className = 'zone-number';
6418:         label.textContent = place.label || String(index + 1);
6419:         zone.appendChild(label);
6420: 
6421:         // Community zone: show mode indicator
6422:         if (place.isCommunityZone) {
6423:             const modeLabel = document.createElement('span');
6424:             modeLabel.className = 'cz-drop-mode';
6425:             modeLabel.textContent = (place.czMode || 'row').toUpperCase();
6426:             zone.appendChild(modeLabel);
6427:         }
6428: 
6429:         // Cards container
6430:         const cardsContainer = document.createElement('div');
6431:         cardsContainer.className = 'zone-cards';
6432:         zone.appendChild(cardsContainer);
6433: 
6434:         // Add drop event handlers
6435:         zone.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
6436:             e.preventDefault();
6437:             e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move';
6438:             zone.classList.add('drag-over');
6439:         });
6440: 
6441:         zone.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
6442:             zone.classList.remove('drag-over');
6443:         });
6444: 
6445:         zone.addEventListener('drop', (e) => handleZoneDrop(e, zone));
6446: 
6447:         // Shift+Click to multi-select drop zones
6448:         zone.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
6449:             if (!e.shiftKey) return;
6450:             e.stopPropagation();
6451:             const placeId = place.id;
6452:             const idx = appState.selectedDropZones.indexOf(placeId);
6453:             if (idx >= 0) {
6454:                 appState.selectedDropZones.splice(idx, 1);
6455:                 zone.classList.remove('zone-multi-selected');
6456:             } else {
6457:                 appState.selectedDropZones.push(placeId);
6458:                 zone.classList.add('zone-multi-selected');
6459:             }
6460:         });
6461: 
6462:         // Right-click to show slot fill context menu
6463:         zone.addEventListener('contextmenu', (e) => {
6464:             e.preventDefault();
6465:             e.stopPropagation();
6466:             const placeId = place.id;
6467:             // If zone not already selected, single-select it
6468:             if (!appState.selectedDropZones.includes(placeId)) {
6469:                 clearDropZoneSelection();
6470:                 appState.selectedDropZones.push(placeId);
6471:                 zone.classList.add('zone-multi-selected');
6472:             }
6473:             showSlotContextMenu(e);
6474:         });
6475: 
6476:         gameContainer.appendChild(zone);
6477: 
6478:         // Restore multi-selected state after render
6479:         if (appState.selectedDropZones.includes(place.id)) {
6480:             zone.classList.add('zone-multi-selected');
6481:         }
6482:     });
6483: 
6484:     // Restore existing cards in grid zones
6485:     restoreGridCards();
6486: }
6487: 
6488: /**
6489:  * Restore cards that are already in grid zones after re-rendering drop zones
6490:  */
6491: function restoreGridCards() {
6492:     const gridCards = appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.zone && c.zone.startsWith('grid-'));
6493: 
6494:     gridCards.forEach(card => {
6495:         const zoneElement = document.querySelector(`.card-drop-zone[data-zone="${card.zone}"]`);
6496:         if (zoneElement) {
6497:             createZoneCardElement(card, zoneElement);
6498:         }
6499:     });
6500: }
6501: 
6502: /**
6503:  * Clear all card drop zones from DOM
6504:  */
6505: function clearCardDropZones() {
6506:     const zones = document.querySelectorAll('.card-drop-zone');
6507:     zones.forEach(z => z.remove());
6508:     
6509:     // Also clean up setup row labels
6510:     const labels = document.querySelectorAll('.setup-row-label');
6511:     labels.forEach(l => l.remove());
6512: }

6518: /**
6519:  * Clear multi-select state for drop zones
6520:  */
6521: function clearDropZoneSelection() {
6522:     appState.selectedDropZones = [];
6523:     document.querySelectorAll('.card-drop-zone.zone-multi-selected').forEach(z => {
6524:         z.classList.remove('zone-multi-selected');
6525:     });
6526: }
6527: 
6528: /**
6529:  * Get selected empty slots (no card placed yet), sorted by cardPlaces index
6530:  */
6531: function getSelectedEmptySlots() {
6532:     const selected = appState.selectedDropZones;
6533:     if (!selected.length) return [];
6534: 
6535:     // Get the ordered list of cardPlaces, filtered to selected + empty
6536:     return appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.filter(place => {
6537:         if (!selected.includes(place.id)) return false;
6538:         // Check if zone already has a card
6539:         const zoneName = 'grid-' + place.id;
6540:         return !appState.tableCards.some(c => c.zone === zoneName);
6541:     });
6542: }
6543: 
6544: /**
6545:  * Show the slot fill context menu at mouse position
6546:  */
6547: function showSlotContextMenu(e) {
6548:     if (!slotContextMenu || !gameContainer) return;
6549:     hideSlotContextMenu();
6550: 
6551:     const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
6552:     let x = e.clientX - containerRect.left;
6553:     let y = e.clientY - containerRect.top;
6554: 
6555:     // Clamp to container bounds
6556:     const menuW = 140;
6557:     const menuH = 80;
6558:     if (x + menuW > containerRect.width) x = containerRect.width - menuW;
6559:     if (y + menuH > containerRect.height) y = containerRect.height - menuH;
6560: 
6561:     slotContextMenu.style.left = x + 'px';
6562:     slotContextMenu.style.top = y + 'px';
6563:     slotContextMenu.classList.remove('hidden');
6564: }
6565: 
6566: /**
6567:  * Hide the slot fill context menu
6568:  */
6569: function hideSlotContextMenu() {
6570:     if (slotContextMenu) slotContextMenu.classList.add('hidden');
6571: }
6572: 
6573: /**
6574:  * Auto fill selected empty slots with random cards from tray
6575:  */
6576: function fillSlotsAuto() {
6577:     hideSlotContextMenu();
6578: 
6579:     const emptySlots = getSelectedEmptySlots();
6580:     if (emptySlots.length === 0) {
6581:         setStatus('No empty slots selected', 'warning');
6582:         clearDropZoneSelection();
6583:         return;
6584:     }
6585: 
6586:     // Get available tray cards
6587:     const available = appState.trayCards.filter(c => c.inTray);
6588:     if (available.length === 0) {
6589:         setStatus('No cards available in tray', 'warning');
6590:         return;
6591:     }
6592: 
6593:     // Shuffle available cards (Fisher-Yates)
6594:     const shuffled = [...available];
6595:     for (let i = shuffled.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
6596:         const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
6597:         [shuffled[i], shuffled[j]] = [shuffled[j], shuffled[i]];
6598:     }
6599: 
6600:     // Take min(emptySlots, available) cards
6601:     const count = Math.min(emptySlots.length, shuffled.length);
6602:     const cardsToPlace = shuffled.slice(0, count);
6603: 
6604:     // Bulk place
6605:     appState._bulkApplying = true;
6606:     for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
6607:         const place = emptySlots[i];
6608:         const card = cardsToPlace[i];
6609:         const zoneName = 'grid-' + place.id;
6610:         const rotation = place.rotation || 0;
6611:         const zoneElement = document.querySelector(`.card-drop-zone[data-zone="${zoneName}"]`);
6612:         if (zoneElement) {
6613:             placeCardInZone(card, zoneName, rotation, zoneElement);
6614:         }
6615:     }
6616:     appState._bulkApplying = false;
6617: 
6618:     renderCardTray();
6619:     hideInstructions();
6620:     updateUI();
6621:     clearDropZoneSelection();
6622: 
6623:     const msg = count < emptySlots.length
6624:         ? `Auto filled ${count}/${emptySlots.length} slots (tray ran out)`
6625:         : `Auto filled ${count} slots`;
6626:     setStatus(msg, 'success');
6627: }
6628: 
6629: /**
6630:  * Show manual fill overlay
6631:  */
6632: function showManualFillOverlay() {
6633:     hideSlotContextMenu();
6634:     if (!manualFillOverlay) return;
6635: 
6636:     const emptySlots = getSelectedEmptySlots();
6637:     if (emptySlots.length === 0) {
6638:         setStatus('No empty slots selected', 'warning');
6639:         clearDropZoneSelection();
6640:         return;
6641:     }
6642: 
6643:     // Update slot count display
6644:     if (manualFillSlotCount) {
6645:         manualFillSlotCount.textContent = `${emptySlots.length} slot${emptySlots.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
6646:     }
6647: 
6648:     // Reset input and error
6649:     if (manualFillInput) manualFillInput.value = '';
6650:     if (manualFillError) {
6651:         manualFillError.textContent = '';
6652:         manualFillError.classList.add('hidden');
6653:     }
6654: 
6655:     manualFillOverlay.classList.remove('hidden');
6656:     setTimeout(() => { if (manualFillInput) manualFillInput.focus(); }, 50);
6657: }
6658: 
6659: /**
6660:  * Hide manual fill overlay
6661:  */
6662: function hideManualFillOverlay() {
6663:     if (manualFillOverlay) manualFillOverlay.classList.add('hidden');
6664: }
6665: 
6666: /**
6667:  * Execute manual fill — parse input, validate, then bulk place
6668:  * All-or-nothing: if any card is invalid, nothing gets placed
6669:  */
6670: function executeManualFill() {
6671:     if (!manualFillInput) return;
6672: 
6673:     const raw = manualFillInput.value.trim();
6674:     if (!raw) {
6675:         showManualFillError('Please enter card codes');
6676:         return;
6677:     }
6678: 
6679:     // Parse input: split by space, comma, or semicolon
6680:     const codes = raw.split(/[\s,;]+/).filter(s => s.length > 0);
6681:     if (codes.length === 0) {
6682:         showManualFillError('Please enter card codes');
6683:         return;
6684:     }
6685: 
6686:     const emptySlots = getSelectedEmptySlots();
6687:     if (emptySlots.length === 0) {
6688:         showManualFillError('No empty slots available');
6689:         return;
6690:     }
6691: 
6692:     // Check count mismatch
6693:     if (codes.length > emptySlots.length) {
6694:         showManualFillError(`Too many cards: ${codes.length} entered, but only ${emptySlots.length} empty slot${emptySlots.length > 1 ? 's' : ''} selected`);
6695:         return;
6696:     }
6697: 
6698:     // Get available tray cards
6699:     const trayAvailable = appState.trayCards.filter(c => c.inTray);
6700: 
6701:     // Resolve all card codes (all-or-nothing validation)
6702:     const resolvedCards = [];
6703:     const errors = [];
6704:     const usedBaseNames = new Set();
6705: 
6706:     for (let i = 0; i < codes.length; i++) {
6707:         const code = codes[i];
6708:         const card = typeof resolveCardName === 'function'
6709:             ? resolveCardName(code, trayAvailable)
6710:             : trayAvailable.find(c => c.name === code);
6711: 
6712:         if (!card) {
6713:             errors.push(`"${code}" — card not found`);
6714:             continue;
6715:         }
6716: 
6717:         // Check duplicate in this batch
6718:         if (usedBaseNames.has(card.name)) {
6719:             errors.push(`"${code}" — duplicate card`);
6720:             continue;
6721:         }
6722: 
6723:         usedBaseNames.add(card.name);
6724:         resolvedCards.push(card);
6725:     }
6726: 
6727:     // If any errors, show them all and abort
6728:     if (errors.length > 0) {
6729:         showManualFillError(errors.join('\n'));
6730:         return;
6731:     }
6732: 
6733:     // All valid — bulk place
6734:     hideManualFillOverlay();
6735: 
6736:     appState._bulkApplying = true;
6737:     for (let i = 0; i < resolvedCards.length; i++) {
6738:         const place = emptySlots[i];
6739:         const card = resolvedCards[i];
6740:         const zoneName = 'grid-' + place.id;
6741:         const rotation = place.rotation || 0;
6742:         const zoneElement = document.querySelector(`.card-drop-zone[data-zone="${zoneName}"]`);
6743:         if (zoneElement) {
6744:             placeCardInZone(card, zoneName, rotation, zoneElement);
6745:         }
6746:     }
6747:     appState._bulkApplying = false;
6748: 
6749:     renderCardTray();
6750:     hideInstructions();
6751:     updateUI();
6752:     clearDropZoneSelection();
6753:     setStatus(`Manually filled ${resolvedCards.length} slot${resolvedCards.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}`, 'success');
6754: }
6755: 
6756: /**
6757:  * Show error message in manual fill overlay
6758:  */
6759: function showManualFillError(msg) {
6760:     if (manualFillError) {
6761:         manualFillError.textContent = msg;
6762:         manualFillError.classList.remove('hidden');
6763:     }
6764: }
6765: 
6766: /**
6767:  * Delete a card place by ID
6768:  */
6769: function deleteCardPlace(placeId) {
6770:     appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.filter(p => p.id !== placeId);
6771: 
6772:     // Remove from any group
6773:     removeSlotFromAllGroups(placeId);
6774:     cleanupEmptyGroups();
6775: 
6776:     // Re-label remaining places (preserve community zone labels)
6777:     let normalIdx = 0;
6778:     appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.forEach((p) => {
6779:         if (!p.isCommunityZone) {
6780:             normalIdx++;
6781:             p.label = String(normalIdx);
6782:         }
6783:     });
6784: 
6785:     updateCardPlacesList();
6786:     renderCardPlaceMarkers();
6787:     updateGroupPanelVisibility();
6788:     setStatus('Card place deleted');
6789: }
6790: 
6791: /**
6792:  * Select a card place marker
6793:  */
6794: function selectCardPlace(place, markerElement) {
6795:     // Deselect previous
6796:     document.querySelectorAll('.card-place-marker.selected').forEach(m => m.classList.remove('selected'));
6797: 
6798:     appState.selectedCardPlace = place;
6799:     if (markerElement) {
6800:         markerElement.classList.add('selected');
6801:     }
6802: 
6803:     // Show CZ settings panel if community zone
6804:     const czPanel = document.getElementById('czSettingsPanel');
6805:     if (czPanel && place.isCommunityZone) {
6806:         czPanel.classList.remove('hidden');
6807: 
6808:         // Populate settings
6809:         const nameEl = document.getElementById('czSettingName');
6810:         if (nameEl) nameEl.textContent = place.label || place.id;
6811: 
6812:         // Mode buttons
6813:         czPanel.querySelectorAll('.cz-mode-option').forEach(btn => {
6814:             btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.mode === (place.czMode || 'row'));
6815:         });
6816: 
6817:         // Width/Height sliders
6818:         const wSlider = document.getElementById('czWidthSlider');
6819:         const hSlider = document.getElementById('czHeightSlider');
6820:         const wValue = document.getElementById('czWidthValue');
6821:         const hValue = document.getElementById('czHeightValue');
6822:         if (wSlider) { wSlider.value = place.czWidth || 300; }
6823:         if (hSlider) { hSlider.value = place.czHeight || 120; }
6824:         if (wValue) { wValue.textContent = place.czWidth || 300; }
6825:         if (hValue) { hValue.textContent = place.czHeight || 120; }
6826:     } else if (czPanel) {
6827:         czPanel.classList.add('hidden');
6828:     }
6829: 
6830:     // Enable cloner button when a slot is selected
6831:     updateClonerBtnState();
6832: }
6833: 
6834: /**
6835:  * Deselect any selected card place marker and hide CZ settings
6836:  */
6837: function deselectCardPlace() {
6838:     document.querySelectorAll('.card-place-marker.selected').forEach(m => m.classList.remove('selected'));
6839:     document.querySelectorAll('.card-place-marker.multi-selected').forEach(m => m.classList.remove('multi-selected'));
6840:     appState.selectedCardPlace = null;
6841:     appState.selectedCardPlaces = [];
6842:     const czPanel = document.getElementById('czSettingsPanel');
6843:     if (czPanel) czPanel.classList.add('hidden');
6844: 
6845:     // Disable cloner button when nothing selected
6846:     updateClonerBtnState();
6847: 
6848:     if (typeof syncTransformIndicator === 'function') syncTransformIndicator();
6849: }

6851: /**
6852:  * Update the cloner button enabled/disabled state
6853:  * Cloner requires exactly one slot to be selected as source
6854:  */
6855: function updateClonerBtnState() {
6856:     var clonerBtn = document.getElementById('clonerBtn');
6857:     if (clonerBtn) {
6858:         clonerBtn.disabled = !appState.selectedCardPlace;
6859:     }
6860: }
