6862: /**
6863:  * Initialize CZ settings panel event listeners
6864:  */
6865: function initCZSettingsPanel() {
6866:     const czPanel = document.getElementById('czSettingsPanel');
6867:     if (!czPanel) return;
6868: 
6869:     // Mode buttons
6870:     czPanel.querySelectorAll('.cz-mode-option').forEach(btn => {
6871:         btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
6872:             const place = appState.selectedCardPlace;
6873:             if (!place || !place.isCommunityZone) return;
6874: 
6875:             place.czMode = btn.dataset.mode;
6876:             czPanel.querySelectorAll('.cz-mode-option').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
6877:             btn.classList.add('active');
6878:             renderCardPlaceMarkers();
6879:             // Re-select to keep panel open
6880:             const marker = document.querySelector(`.card-place-marker[data-place-id="${place.id}"]`);
6881:             if (marker) selectCardPlace(place, marker);
6882:             debugLog(`[CommunityZone] ${place.id} mode → ${place.czMode}`);
6883:         });
6884:     });
6885: 
6886:     // Width slider
6887:     const wSlider = document.getElementById('czWidthSlider');
6888:     const wValue = document.getElementById('czWidthValue');
6889:     if (wSlider) {
6890:         wSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
6891:             const place = appState.selectedCardPlace;
6892:             if (!place || !place.isCommunityZone) return;
6893:             place.czWidth = parseInt(wSlider.value);
6894:             if (wValue) wValue.textContent = wSlider.value;
6895:             renderCardPlaceMarkers();
6896:             const marker = document.querySelector(`.card-place-marker[data-place-id="${place.id}"]`);
6897:             if (marker) {
6898:                 marker.classList.add('selected');
6899:             }
6900:         });
6901:     }
6902: 
6903:     // Height slider
6904:     const hSlider = document.getElementById('czHeightSlider');
6905:     const hValue = document.getElementById('czHeightValue');
6906:     if (hSlider) {
6907:         hSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
6908:             const place = appState.selectedCardPlace;
6909:             if (!place || !place.isCommunityZone) return;
6910:             place.czHeight = parseInt(hSlider.value);
6911:             if (hValue) hValue.textContent = hSlider.value;
6912:             renderCardPlaceMarkers();
6913:             const marker = document.querySelector(`.card-place-marker[data-place-id="${place.id}"]`);
6914:             if (marker) {
6915:                 marker.classList.add('selected');
6916:             }
6917:         });
6918:     }
6919: 
6920:     // Click on table/container to deselect
6921:     const pokerTable = document.getElementById('pokerTable');
6922:     if (pokerTable) {
6923:         pokerTable.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
6924:             // Only deselect if clicking directly on the table (not on a marker)
6925:             if (e.target === pokerTable || e.target.classList.contains('table-felt') || e.target.classList.contains('table-border-ring')) {
6926:                 if (appState.phase === 'board-setting') {
6927:                     deselectCardPlace();
6928:                 }
6929:             }
6930:         });
6931:     }
6932: 
6933:     // Lasso selection: mousedown on gameContainer (board-setting phase)
6934:     if (gameContainer) {
6935:         let lassoRect = null;
6936:         let lassoStartX = 0, lassoStartY = 0;
6937:         let isLassoing = false;
6938: 
6939:         gameContainer.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
6940:             if (appState.phase !== 'board-setting' && appState.phase !== 'setup') return;
6941:             if (e.button !== 0) return;
6942:             // Only start lasso if clicking on table/felt (not on markers, buttons, cards, etc.)
6943:             const target = e.target;
6944:             if (target.closest('.card-place-marker') || target.closest('.dealing-card-slot') || target.closest('button')) return;
6945:             // In setup phase: don't start lasso if clicking on a card or filled zone
6946:             if (appState.phase === 'setup' && (target.closest('.zone-card') || target.closest('.card'))) return;
6947: 
6948:             const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
6949:             lassoStartX = e.clientX - containerRect.left;
6950:             lassoStartY = e.clientY - containerRect.top;
6951:             isLassoing = true;
6952: 
6953:             // Create lasso rect element
6954:             lassoRect = document.createElement('div');
6955:             lassoRect.className = 'selection-rect';
6956:             lassoRect.style.left = `${lassoStartX}px`;
6957:             lassoRect.style.top = `${lassoStartY}px`;
6958:             lassoRect.style.width = '0px';
6959:             lassoRect.style.height = '0px';
6960:             gameContainer.appendChild(lassoRect);
6961:         });
6962: 
6963:         document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
6964:             if (!isLassoing || !lassoRect) return;
6965:             
6966:             // Fix for stuck drag: if left mouse button is no longer pressed (e.g. released outside window)
6967:             if (e.buttons !== 1) {
6968:                 // Abort lasso
6969:                 isLassoing = false;
6970:                 if (lassoRect) lassoRect.remove();
6971:                 lassoRect = null;
6972:                 return;
6973:             }
6974: 
6975:             const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
6976:             const currentX = e.clientX - containerRect.left;
6977:             const currentY = e.clientY - containerRect.top;
6978: 
6979:             const left = Math.min(lassoStartX, currentX);
6980:             const top = Math.min(lassoStartY, currentY);
6981:             const width = Math.abs(currentX - lassoStartX);
6982:             const height = Math.abs(currentY - lassoStartY);
6983: 
6984:             lassoRect.style.left = `${left}px`;
6985:             lassoRect.style.top = `${top}px`;
6986:             lassoRect.style.width = `${width}px`;
6987:             lassoRect.style.height = `${height}px`;
6988:         });
6989: 
6990:         document.addEventListener('mouseup', (e) => {
6991:             if (!isLassoing || !lassoRect) return;
6992:             isLassoing = false;
6993: 
6994:             const rectBounds = lassoRect.getBoundingClientRect();
6995:             lassoRect.remove();
6996:             lassoRect = null;
6997: 
6998:             // Minimum size threshold to avoid accidental clicks
6999:             if (rectBounds.width < 5 && rectBounds.height < 5) return;
7000: 
7001:             if (appState.phase === 'setup') {
7002:                 // Setup phase: select empty drop zones and show fill context menu
7003:                 clearDropZoneSelection();
7004:                 const dropZones = document.querySelectorAll('.card-drop-zone');
7005:                 dropZones.forEach(zone => {
7006:                     const zoneBounds = zone.getBoundingClientRect();
7007:                     if (zoneBounds.left < rectBounds.right &&
7008:                         zoneBounds.right > rectBounds.left &&
7009:                         zoneBounds.top < rectBounds.bottom &&
7010:                         zoneBounds.bottom > rectBounds.top) {
7011:                         const zoneName = zone.dataset.zone;
7012:                         if (!zoneName) return;
7013:                         const placeId = zoneName.replace('grid-', '');
7014:                         // Only select EMPTY slots (no card in this zone)
7015:                         const hasCard = appState.tableCards.some(c => c.zone === zoneName);
7016:                         if (!hasCard) {
7017:                             appState.selectedDropZones.push(placeId);
7018:                             zone.classList.add('zone-multi-selected');
7019:                         }
7020:                     }
7021:                 });
7022: 
7023:                 if (appState.selectedDropZones.length > 0) {
7024:                     debugLog(`[LassoSelect] Selected ${appState.selectedDropZones.length} empty slots`);
7025:                     // Show fill context menu at mouse position
7026:                     showSlotContextMenu(e);
7027:                 }
7028:             } else {
7029:                 // Board-setting phase: select markers
7030:                 const markers = document.querySelectorAll('.card-place-marker');
7031:                 appState.selectedCardPlaces = [];
7032:                 markers.forEach(marker => {
7033:                     const markerBounds = marker.getBoundingClientRect();
7034:                     if (markerBounds.left < rectBounds.right &&
7035:                         markerBounds.right > rectBounds.left &&
7036:                         markerBounds.top < rectBounds.bottom &&
7037:                         markerBounds.bottom > rectBounds.top) {
7038:                         const placeId = marker.dataset.placeId;
7039:                         const place = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.find(p => p.id === placeId);
7040:                         if (place) {
7041:                             appState.selectedCardPlaces.push(place);
7042:                             marker.classList.add('multi-selected');
7043:                         }
7044:                     } else {
7045:                         marker.classList.remove('multi-selected');
7046:                     }
7047:                 });
7048: 
7049:                 if (appState.selectedCardPlaces.length > 0) {
7050:                     debugLog(`[LassoSelect] Selected ${appState.selectedCardPlaces.length} markers`);
7051:                 }
7052:                 updateCreateGroupBtnState();
7053:                 if (typeof syncTransformIndicator === 'function') syncTransformIndicator();
7054:             }
7055:         });
7056:     }
7057: 
7058:     // Ctrl+Z: Undo marker positions, rotation, and group operations (board-setting phase)
7059:     document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
7060:         if (appState.phase !== 'board-setting') return;
7061:         if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'z') {
7062:             e.preventDefault();
7063: 
7064:             // Try marker undo stack first (position/rotation changes OR delete undo)
7065:             if (appState.markerUndoStack.length > 0) {
7066:                 const snapshot = appState.markerUndoStack.pop();
7067: 
7068:                 // Delete undo: restore full cardPlaces + slotGroups
7069:                 if (snapshot.type === 'delete') {
7070:                     appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces = snapshot.cardPlaces;
7071:                     appState.boardLayout.slotGroups = snapshot.slotGroups;
7072:                     renderCardPlaceMarkers();
7073:                     updateCardPlacesList();
7074:                     updateGroupPanelVisibility();
7075:                     debugLog(`[Undo] Restored ${snapshot.cardPlaces.length} markers after delete`);
7076:                 }
7077:                 // Position/rotation undo
7078:                 else {
7079:                     snapshot.forEach(saved => {
7080:                         const place = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.find(p => p.id === saved.id);
7081:                         if (place) {
7082:                             place.x = saved.x;
7083:                             place.y = saved.y;
7084:                             place.rotation = saved.rotation || 0;
7085:                             // Restore CZ dimensions if present
7086:                             if (saved.czWidth !== undefined) place.czWidth = saved.czWidth;
7087:                             if (saved.czHeight !== undefined) place.czHeight = saved.czHeight;
7088:                         }
7089:                     });
7090:                     renderCardPlaceMarkers();
7091:                     updateCardPlacesList();
7092:                     debugLog(`[Undo] Restored marker state (${appState.markerUndoStack.length} left)`);
7093:                 }
7094:             }
7095:             // Otherwise try group undo stack
7096:             else if (typeof undoGroupAction === 'function') {
7097:                 undoGroupAction();
7098:                 renderGroupPanel();
7099:                 renderCardPlaceMarkers();
7100:                 debugLog('[Undo] Restored group state');
7101:             }
7102:         }
7103: 
7104:         // Delete/Backspace: delete selected markers (multi-select or single)
7105:         if (e.key === 'Delete' || e.key === 'Backspace') {
7106:             // Don't delete if focus is in a text input/textarea (allow range/checkbox/radio)
7107:             if (e.target.tagName === 'TEXTAREA') return;
7108:             if (e.target.tagName === 'INPUT' && !['range', 'checkbox', 'radio'].includes(e.target.type)) return;
7109: 
7110:             const toDelete = appState.selectedCardPlaces.length > 0
7111:                 ? [...appState.selectedCardPlaces]
7112:                 : (appState.selectedCardPlace ? [appState.selectedCardPlace] : []);
7113:             if (toDelete.length === 0) return;
7114: 
7115:             e.preventDefault();
7116: 
7117:             // Push full cardPlaces + slotGroups snapshot for undo
7118:             appState.markerUndoStack.push({
7119:                 type: 'delete',
7120:                 cardPlaces: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces)),
7121:                 slotGroups: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || []))
7122:             });
7123: 
7124:             toDelete.forEach(p => deleteCardPlace(p.id));
7125:             deselectCardPlace();
7126:             debugLog(`[Delete] Removed ${toDelete.length} marker(s)`);
7127:             setStatus(`Deleted ${toDelete.length} card place(s)`);
7128:         }
7129:     });
7130: }
7131: 
7132: /**
7133:  * Start dragging a marker (supports group drag for multi-selected markers)
7134:  */
7135: function startDragMarker(e, place, marker) {
7136:     if (e.button !== 0) return; // Left click only
7137: 
7138:     e.preventDefault();
7139:     marker.classList.add('dragging');
7140: 
7141:     const pokerTable = document.getElementById('pokerTable');
7142:     const tableRect = pokerTable.getBoundingClientRect();
7143:     const containerRect = gameContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
7144:     const tableWidth = pokerTable.offsetWidth;
7145:     const tableHeight = pokerTable.offsetHeight;
7146: 
7147:     // Calculate offset from gameContainer to pokerTable
7148:     const offsetX = tableRect.left - containerRect.left;
7149:     const offsetY = tableRect.top - containerRect.top;
7150: 
7151:     // Scale factors: UI coordinates (1280x720) → DOM pixels
7152:     const scaleX = tableWidth / UI_WIDTH;
7153:     const scaleY = tableHeight / UI_HEIGHT;
7154: 
7155:     const startX = e.clientX;
7156:     const startY = e.clientY;
7157: 
7158:     // Save position+rotation snapshot for undo (before any movement)
7159:     const undoSnapshot = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.map(p => ({ id: p.id, x: p.x, y: p.y, rotation: p.rotation || 0 }));
7160:     let hasMoved = false;
7161: 
7162:     // Check if this is a group drag (marker is in multi-select)
7163:     const isGroupDrag = appState.selectedCardPlaces.includes(place) && appState.selectedCardPlaces.length > 1;
7164: 
7165:     // For group drag: store initial positions for all selected markers
7166:     let groupData = [];
7167:     if (isGroupDrag) {
7168:         groupData = appState.selectedCardPlaces.map(p => {
7169:             const markerW = p.isCommunityZone ? (p.czWidth || 300) * scaleX : CARD_WIDTH;
7170:             const markerH = p.isCommunityZone ? (p.czHeight || 120) * scaleY : CARD_HEIGHT;
7171:             const markerEl = document.querySelector(`.card-place-marker[data-place-id="${p.id}"]`);
7172:             return {
7173:                 place: p,
7174:                 marker: markerEl,
7175:                 startLeft: offsetX + p.x * scaleX - markerW / 2,
7176:                 startTop: offsetY + p.y * scaleY - markerH / 2,
7177:                 markerW,
7178:                 markerH
7179:             };
7180:         });
7181:     } else {
7182:         // Single drag
7183:         const markerW = place.isCommunityZone ? (place.czWidth || 300) * scaleX : CARD_WIDTH;
7184:         const markerH = place.isCommunityZone ? (place.czHeight || 120) * scaleY : CARD_HEIGHT;
7185:         groupData = [{
7186:             place,
7187:             marker,
7188:             startLeft: offsetX + place.x * scaleX - markerW / 2,
7189:             startTop: offsetY + place.y * scaleY - markerH / 2,
7190:             markerW,
7191:             markerH
7192:         }];
7193:     }
7194: 
7195:     function onMouseMove(moveE) {
7196:         hasMoved = true;
7197:         const dx = moveE.clientX - startX;
7198:         const dy = moveE.clientY - startY;
7199: 
7200:         groupData.forEach(item => {
7201:             // New position in container coordinates
7202:             let newLeft = item.startLeft + dx;
7203:             let newTop = item.startTop + dy;
7204: 
7205:             // Constrain to game container bounds
7206:             newLeft = Math.max(0, Math.min(containerRect.width - item.markerW, newLeft));
7207:             newTop = Math.max(0, Math.min(containerRect.height - item.markerH, newTop));
7208: 
7209:             // Update marker position
7210:             if (item.marker) {
7211:                 item.marker.style.left = `${newLeft}px`;
7212:                 item.marker.style.top = `${newTop}px`;
7213:             }
7214: 
7215:             // Convert DOM pixels back to UI coordinates for storage (center point)
7216:             item.place.x = (newLeft - offsetX + item.markerW / 2) / scaleX;
7217:             item.place.y = (newTop - offsetY + item.markerH / 2) / scaleY;
7218:         });
7219: 
7220:         // Update cloner preview if cloner is active and source is being dragged
7221:         if (typeof clonerState !== 'undefined' && clonerState.active && clonerState.sourcePlace) {
7222:             clonerState.sourceX = clonerState.sourcePlace.x;
7223:             clonerState.sourceY = clonerState.sourcePlace.y;
7224:             if (typeof updateClonerPreview === 'function') updateClonerPreview();
7225:         }
7226:     }
7227: 
7228:     function onMouseUp() {
7229:         marker.classList.remove('dragging');
7230:         document.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove);
7231:         document.removeEventListener('mouseup', onMouseUp);
7232:         // Push undo snapshot only if marker actually moved
7233:         if (hasMoved) {
7234:             appState.markerUndoStack.push(undoSnapshot);
7235:             if (appState.markerUndoStack.length > 50) appState.markerUndoStack.shift();
7236:         }
7237:         if (isGroupDrag) {
7238:             debugLog(`[GroupDrag] Moved ${groupData.length} markers`);
7239:         } else {
7240:             debugLog(`[DragMarker] Place ${place.id} → UI(${Math.round(place.x)}, ${Math.round(place.y)})`);
7241:         }
7242:         updateCardPlacesList();
7243:     }
7244: 
7245:     document.addEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove);
7246:     document.addEventListener('mouseup', onMouseUp);
7247: }
7248: 
7249: /**
7250:  * Start rotating a card place marker by dragging the rotation handle
7251:  * Calculates angle from mouse position relative to marker center
7252:  * Shift = snap to 15° increments
7253:  */
7254: function startRotateMarker(e, place, marker) {
7255:     e.preventDefault();
7256:     e.stopPropagation();
7257: 
7258:     marker.classList.add('rotating');
7259: 
7260:     // Get marker center in viewport coordinates
7261:     const markerRect = marker.getBoundingClientRect();
7262:     const centerX = markerRect.left + markerRect.width / 2;
7263:     const centerY = markerRect.top + markerRect.height / 2;
7264: 
7265:     // Calculate initial angle offset so rotation starts from current angle
7266:     const startMouseAngle = Math.atan2(e.clientY - centerY, e.clientX - centerX) * 180 / Math.PI;
7267:     const startRotation = place.rotation || 0;
7268: 
7269:     // Save undo snapshot
7270:     const undoSnapshot = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.map(p => ({ id: p.id, x: p.x, y: p.y, rotation: p.rotation || 0 }));
7271:     let hasRotated = false;
7272: 
7273:     function onMouseMove(moveE) {
7274:         hasRotated = true;
7275:         const mouseAngle = Math.atan2(moveE.clientY - centerY, moveE.clientX - centerX) * 180 / Math.PI;
7276:         let newRotation = startRotation + (mouseAngle - startMouseAngle);
7277: 
7278:         // Normalize to -180..180
7279:         while (newRotation > 180) newRotation -= 360;
7280:         while (newRotation < -180) newRotation += 360;
7281: 
7282:         // Shift = snap to 15° increments
7283:         if (moveE.shiftKey) {
7284:             newRotation = Math.round(newRotation / 15) * 15;
7285:         }
7286: 
7287:         place.rotation = Math.round(newRotation);
7288:         marker.style.transform = `rotate(${place.rotation}deg)`;
7289:     }
7290: 
7291:     function onMouseUp() {
7292:         marker.classList.remove('rotating');
7293:         document.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove);
7294:         document.removeEventListener('mouseup', onMouseUp);
7295:         if (hasRotated) {
7296:             appState.markerUndoStack.push(undoSnapshot);
7297:             if (appState.markerUndoStack.length > 50) appState.markerUndoStack.shift();
7298:         }
7299:         debugLog(`[RotateMarker] Place ${place.id} → ${place.rotation}°`);
7300:         updateCardPlacesList();
7301:     }
7302: 
7303:     document.addEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove);
7304:     document.addEventListener('mouseup', onMouseUp);
7305: }
7306: 
7307: /**
7308:  * Start resizing a community zone marker
7309:  * Resizes from CENTER (anchor at center, not top-left)
7310:  */
7311: function startResizeCommunityZone(e, place, marker, scaleX, scaleY) {
7312:     e.preventDefault();
7313:     e.stopPropagation();
7314: 
7315:     const startX = e.clientX;
7316:     const startY = e.clientY;
7317:     const startW = (place.czWidth || 300) * scaleX;
7318:     const startH = (place.czHeight || 120) * scaleY;
7319:     const startLeft = parseFloat(marker.style.left);
7320:     const startTop = parseFloat(marker.style.top);
7321: 
7322:     // Push undo snapshot before resize (includes CZ dimensions)
7323:     const undoSnapshot = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.map(p => ({
7324:         id: p.id, x: p.x, y: p.y, rotation: p.rotation || 0,
7325:         czWidth: p.czWidth, czHeight: p.czHeight
7326:     }));
7327:     let hasResized = false;
7328: 
7329:     marker.classList.add('resizing');
7330: 
7331:     function onMouseMove(moveE) {
7332:         const dx = moveE.clientX - startX;
7333:         const dy = moveE.clientY - startY;
7334: 
7335:         const newW = Math.max(CARD_WIDTH * 2, startW + dx);
7336:         const newH = Math.max(CARD_HEIGHT, startH + dy);
7337:         hasResized = true;
7338: 
7339:         // Adjust left/top to keep center fixed (grow from center, not top-left)
7340:         const deltaW = newW - startW;
7341:         const deltaH = newH - startH;
7342:         marker.style.left = `${startLeft - deltaW / 2}px`;
7343:         marker.style.top = `${startTop - deltaH / 2}px`;
7344:         marker.style.width = `${newW}px`;
7345:         marker.style.height = `${newH}px`;
7346: 
7347:         // Store back in UI coordinates
7348:         place.czWidth = Math.round(newW / scaleX);
7349:         place.czHeight = Math.round(newH / scaleY);
7350:     }
7351: 
7352:     function onMouseUp() {
7353:         marker.classList.remove('resizing');
7354:         document.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove);
7355:         document.removeEventListener('mouseup', onMouseUp);
7356:         if (hasResized) {
7357:             appState.markerUndoStack.push(undoSnapshot);
7358:             if (appState.markerUndoStack.length > 50) appState.markerUndoStack.shift();
7359:         }
7360:         debugLog(`[CommunityZone] ${place.id} resized → ${place.czWidth}×${place.czHeight} UI px`);
7361:         // Re-render to apply final state
7362:         renderCardPlaceMarkers();
7363:     }
7364: 
7365:     document.addEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove);
7366:     document.addEventListener('mouseup', onMouseUp);
7367: }
7368: 
7369: /**
7370:  * Update the card places list in the director panel
7371:  */
7372: function updateCardPlacesList() {
7373:     if (!cardPlacesList) return;
7374: 
7375:     const count = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.length;
7376:     cardPlacesList.innerHTML = `<div class="list-header">Card Places (${count})</div>`;
7377: 
7378:     appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.forEach((place, index) => {
7379:         const item = document.createElement('div');
7380:         item.className = 'card-place-item';
7381:         const isCZ = place.isCommunityZone;
7382:         const labelText = isCZ
7383:             ? `📦 ${place.label || 'CZ'} (${(place.czMode || 'row').toUpperCase()})`
7384:             : (place.label || index + 1);
7385:         item.innerHTML = `
7386:             <span class="place-label">${labelText}</span>
7387:             <span class="place-coords">(${Math.round(place.x)}, ${Math.round(place.y)})${isCZ ? ` ${place.czWidth}×${place.czHeight}` : ''}</span>
7388:             <button class="delete-place-btn" data-place-id="${place.id}">✕</button>
7389:         `;
7390: 
7391:         // Delete button handler
7392:         item.querySelector('.delete-place-btn').addEventListener('click', () => {
7393:             deleteCardPlace(place.id);
7394:         });
7395: 
7396:         cardPlacesList.appendChild(item);
7397:     });
7398: }
7399: 
7400: /**
7401:  * Toggle visibility between cardPlacesList and slotGroupPanel
7402:  * Panel is ALWAYS visible (for createGroupBtn access) — BUG #1 fix
7403:  * Card places list hidden when groups exist, shown otherwise
7404:  */
7405: function updateGroupPanelVisibility() {
7406:     var groupPanel = document.getElementById('slotGroupPanel');
7407:     var placesList = document.getElementById('cardPlacesList');
7408:     if (!groupPanel || !placesList) return;
7409: 
7410:     // Panel always visible in board-setting mode
7411:     groupPanel.classList.remove('hidden');
7412: 
7413:     var hasGroups = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups && appState.boardLayout.slotGroups.length > 0;
7414:     if (hasGroups) {
7415:         placesList.classList.add('hidden');
7416:         renderGroupPanel();
7417:     } else {
7418:         placesList.classList.remove('hidden');
7419:         // Show empty hint in group list
7420:         var groupList = document.getElementById('groupList');
7421:         if (groupList) {
7422:             groupList.innerHTML = '<div class="group-ungrouped">No groups yet — select 2+ markers then click + Group</div>';
7423:         }
7424:     }
7425:     updateCreateGroupBtnState();
7426: }
7427: 
7428: /**
7429:  * Render the group panel with drag-to-reorder support
7430:  * Groups displayed in reverse order: top item = highest groupOrder = front/closest to camera
7431:  */
7432: function renderGroupPanel() {
7433:     var groupList = document.getElementById('groupList');
7434:     if (!groupList) return;
7435:     groupList.innerHTML = '';
7436: 
7437:     var groups = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || [];
7438:     if (groups.length === 0) return;
7439: 
7440:     // Display in reverse: highest groupOrder at top (= "front" like Photoshop)
7441:     var sorted = groups.slice().sort(function (a, b) { return b.groupOrder - a.groupOrder; });
7442: 
7443:     sorted.forEach(function (group, displayIdx) {
7444:         var item = document.createElement('div');
7445:         item.className = 'group-item';
7446:         item.dataset.groupId = group.id;
7447:         item.dataset.groupIndex = String(groups.indexOf(group));
7448:         item.draggable = true;
7449:         item.style.borderLeftColor = group.color;
7450: 
7451:         // Color dot
7452:         var dot = document.createElement('span');
7453:         dot.className = 'group-color-dot';
7454:         dot.style.backgroundColor = group.color;
7455:         item.appendChild(dot);
7456: 
7457:         // Editable name
7458:         var name = document.createElement('span');
7459:         name.className = 'group-name';
7460:         name.textContent = group.name;
7461:         name.addEventListener('dblclick', function () {
7462:             name.contentEditable = 'true';
7463:             name.focus();
7464:             // Select all text
7465:             var range = document.createRange();
7466:             range.selectNodeContents(name);
7467:             var sel = window.getSelection();
7468:             sel.removeAllRanges();
7469:             sel.addRange(range);
7470:         });
7471:         name.addEventListener('blur', function () {
7472:             name.contentEditable = 'false';
7473:             var newName = name.textContent.trim();
7474:             if (newName && newName !== group.name) {
7475:                 renameSlotGroup(group.id, newName);
7476:             } else {
7477:                 name.textContent = group.name;
7478:             }
7479:         });
7480:         name.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
7481:             if (e.key === 'Enter') {
7482:                 e.preventDefault();
7483:                 name.blur();
7484:             }
7485:         });
7486:         item.appendChild(name);
7487: 
7488:         // Slot count
7489:         var count = document.createElement('span');
7490:         count.className = 'group-slot-count';
7491:         count.textContent = '(' + group.slotIds.length + ')';
7492:         item.appendChild(count);
7493: 
7494:         // Actions
7495:         var actions = document.createElement('div');
7496:         actions.className = 'group-actions';
7497: 
7498:         // Edit button for cloner groups
7499:         if (group.clonerConfig) {
7500:             var editBtn = document.createElement('button');
7501:             editBtn.className = 'edit-group';
7502:             editBtn.textContent = '✏️';
7503:             editBtn.title = 'Edit cloner settings';
7504:             editBtn.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
7505:                 e.stopPropagation();
7506:                 editCloner(group.id);
7507:             });
7508:             actions.appendChild(editBtn);
7509:         }
7510: 
7511:         var deleteBtn = document.createElement('button');
7512:         deleteBtn.className = 'delete-group';
7513:         deleteBtn.textContent = '✕';
7514:         deleteBtn.title = group.clonerConfig ? 'Delete cloner group & all slots' : 'Delete group';
7515:         deleteBtn.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
7516:             e.stopPropagation();
7517:             if (group.clonerConfig) {
7518:                 deleteClonerGroup(group.id);
7519:             } else {
7520:                 deleteSlotGroup(group.id);
7521:             }
7522:             renderGroupPanel();
7523:             renderCardPlaceMarkers();
7524:         });
7525:         actions.appendChild(deleteBtn);
7526:         item.appendChild(actions);
7527: 
7528:         // Hover: highlight markers on board
7529:         item.addEventListener('mouseenter', function () {
7530:             highlightGroupMarkers(group.id, true);
7531:         });
7532:         item.addEventListener('mouseleave', function () {
7533:             highlightGroupMarkers(group.id, false);
7534:         });
7535: 
7536:         // Click: toggle-select all markers in this group
7537:         item.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
7538:             // Don't trigger on delete button or name editing
7539:             if (e.target.closest('.group-actions') || e.target.closest('.group-name[contenteditable="true"]')) return;
7540: 
7541:             // Check if this group's slots are already fully selected
7542:             var allSelected = group.slotIds.length > 0 && group.slotIds.every(function (sid) {
7543:                 return appState.selectedCardPlaces.some(function (p) { return p.id === sid; });
7544:             });
7545: 
7546:             if (allSelected) {
7547:                 // Unselect: remove this group's slots from selection
7548:                 appState.selectedCardPlaces = appState.selectedCardPlaces.filter(function (p) {
7549:                     return group.slotIds.indexOf(p.id) < 0;
7550:                 });
7551:                 item.classList.remove('selected');
7552:             } else {
7553:                 // Select: add all group's slots (avoid duplicates)
7554:                 group.slotIds.forEach(function (sid) {
7555:                     var alreadyIn = appState.selectedCardPlaces.some(function (p) { return p.id === sid; });
7556:                     if (!alreadyIn) {
7557:                         var place = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces.find(function (p) { return p.id === sid; });
7558:                         if (place) appState.selectedCardPlaces.push(place);
7559:                     }
7560:                 });
7561:                 item.classList.add('selected');
7562:             }
7563: 
7564:             // Update marker visual state on board
7565:             document.querySelectorAll('.card-place-marker').forEach(function (m) {
7566:                 var pid = m.dataset.placeId;
7567:                 if (appState.selectedCardPlaces.some(function (p) { return p.id === pid; })) {
7568:                     m.classList.add('multi-selected');
7569:                 } else {
7570:                     m.classList.remove('multi-selected');
7571:                 }
7572:             });
7573: 
7574:             // Sync other group items' selected state
7575:             groupList.querySelectorAll('.group-item').forEach(function (gi) {
7576:                 var gid = gi.dataset.groupId;
7577:                 var grp = groups.find(function (g) { return g.id === gid; });
7578:                 if (!grp) return;
7579:                 var grpAllSelected = grp.slotIds.length > 0 && grp.slotIds.every(function (sid) {
7580:                     return appState.selectedCardPlaces.some(function (p) { return p.id === sid; });
7581:                 });
7582:                 if (grpAllSelected) {
7583:                     gi.classList.add('selected');
7584:                 } else {
7585:                     gi.classList.remove('selected');
7586:                 }
7587:             });
7588: 
7589:             updateCreateGroupBtnState();
7590:             debugLog('[GroupPanel] Click ' + group.name + ' → ' + appState.selectedCardPlaces.length + ' selected');
7591:         });
7592: 
7593:         // HTML5 Drag-to-reorder
7594:         item.addEventListener('dragstart', function (e) {
7595:             e.dataTransfer.setData('text/plain', String(groups.indexOf(group)));
7596:             e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
7597:             item.classList.add('dragging');
7598:         });
7599:         item.addEventListener('dragend', function () {
7600:             item.classList.remove('dragging');
7601:             // Remove all drag-over states
7602:             groupList.querySelectorAll('.drag-over').forEach(function (el) {
7603:                 el.classList.remove('drag-over');
7604:             });
7605:         });
7606:         item.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
7607:             e.preventDefault();
7608:             e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move';
7609:             item.classList.add('drag-over');
7610:         });
7611:         item.addEventListener('dragleave', function () {
7612:             item.classList.remove('drag-over');
7613:         });
7614:         item.addEventListener('drop', function (e) {
7615:             e.preventDefault();
7616:             item.classList.remove('drag-over');
7617:             var fromIndex = parseInt(e.dataTransfer.getData('text/plain'), 10);
7618:             var toIndex = groups.indexOf(group);
7619:             if (fromIndex !== toIndex && !isNaN(fromIndex)) {
7620:                 reorderSlotGroups(fromIndex, toIndex);
7621:                 renderGroupPanel();
7622:                 renderCardPlaceMarkers();
7623:             }
7624:         });
7625: 
7626:         groupList.appendChild(item);
7627:     });
7628: 
7629:     // Show ungrouped count
7630:     var allSlotIds = [];
7631:     groups.forEach(function (g) {
7632:         allSlotIds = allSlotIds.concat(g.slotIds);
7633:     });
7634:     var ungroupedCount = (appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces || []).filter(function (p) {
7635:         return allSlotIds.indexOf(p.id) < 0;
7636:     }).length;
7637:     if (ungroupedCount > 0) {
7638:         var ungroupedDiv = document.createElement('div');
7639:         ungroupedDiv.className = 'group-ungrouped';
7640:         ungroupedDiv.textContent = ungroupedCount + ' ungrouped slot' + (ungroupedCount > 1 ? 's' : '');
7641:         groupList.appendChild(ungroupedDiv);
7642:     }
7643: 
7644:     updateCreateGroupBtnState();
7645: }
7646: 
7647: /**
7648:  * Update the create group button enabled/disabled state
7649:  * Called from shift-click handler, renderGroupPanel, and updateGroupPanelVisibility
7650:  */
7651: function updateCreateGroupBtnState() {
7652:     var createBtn = document.getElementById('createGroupBtn');
7653:     if (createBtn) {
7654:         createBtn.disabled = !appState.selectedCardPlaces || appState.selectedCardPlaces.length < 2;
7655:     }
7656: }
7657: 
7658: /**
7659:  * Highlight or unhighlight markers belonging to a group on the board
7660:  * @param {string} groupId
7661:  * @param {boolean} highlight
7662:  */
7663: function highlightGroupMarkers(groupId, highlight) {
7664:     var groups = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || [];
7665:     var group = groups.find(function (g) { return g.id === groupId; });
7666:     if (!group) return;
7667: 
7668:     group.slotIds.forEach(function (slotId) {
7669:         var marker = document.querySelector('.card-place-marker[data-place-id="' + slotId + '"]');
7670:         if (marker) {
7671:             if (highlight) {
7672:                 marker.classList.add('group-highlight');
7673:             } else {
7674:                 marker.classList.remove('group-highlight');
7675:             }
7676:         }
7677:     });
7678: }
7679: 
7680: /**
7681:  * Show/hide the group order section in Record phase
7682:  */
7683: function updateGroupOrderSectionVisibility() {
7684:     var section = document.getElementById('groupOrderSection');
7685:     if (!section) return;
7686:     var hasGroups = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups && appState.boardLayout.slotGroups.length > 0;
7687:     if (hasGroups) {
7688:         section.classList.remove('hidden');
7689:         renderGroupOrderStrip();
7690:     } else {
7691:         section.classList.add('hidden');
7692:     }
7693: }
7694: 
7695: /**
7696:  * Render group order chips in Record mode — drag to reorder for this step
7697:  * Order: left = back (lowest groupOrder), right = front (highest)
7698:  */
7699: function renderGroupOrderStrip() {
7700:     var strip = document.getElementById('groupOrderStrip');
7701:     if (!strip) return;
7702:     strip.innerHTML = '';
7703: 
7704:     var groups = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || [];
7705:     if (groups.length === 0) return;
7706: 
7707:     // Build working order: start from current order, apply pending overrides
7708:     var workingGroups = groups.map(function (g) {
7709:         var order = g.groupOrder;
7710:         if (appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides && appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides[g.id] !== undefined) {
7711:             order = appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides[g.id];
7712:         }
7713:         return { id: g.id, name: g.name, color: g.color, workingOrder: order };
7714:     });
7715:     workingGroups.sort(function (a, b) { return a.workingOrder - b.workingOrder; });
7716: 
7717:     workingGroups.forEach(function (wg, displayIdx) {
7718:         var chip = document.createElement('div');
7719:         chip.className = 'group-order-chip';
7720:         chip.style.backgroundColor = wg.color;
7721:         chip.dataset.groupId = wg.id;
7722:         chip.dataset.displayIdx = String(displayIdx);
7723:         chip.draggable = true;
7724: 
7725:         // Order number
7726:         var orderSpan = document.createElement('span');
7727:         orderSpan.className = 'chip-order';
7728:         orderSpan.textContent = String(displayIdx);
7729:         chip.appendChild(orderSpan);
7730: 
7731:         // Name
7732:         var nameSpan = document.createElement('span');
7733:         nameSpan.textContent = wg.name;
7734:         chip.appendChild(nameSpan);
7735: 
7736:         // Drag handlers
7737:         chip.addEventListener('dragstart', function (e) {
7738:             e.dataTransfer.setData('text/plain', String(displayIdx));
7739:             e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
7740:             chip.classList.add('dragging');
7741:         });
7742:         chip.addEventListener('dragend', function () {
7743:             chip.classList.remove('dragging');
7744:             strip.querySelectorAll('.drag-over').forEach(function (el) { el.classList.remove('drag-over'); });
7745:         });
7746:         chip.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
7747:             e.preventDefault();
7748:             e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move';
7749:             chip.classList.add('drag-over');
7750:         });
7751:         chip.addEventListener('dragleave', function () {
7752:             chip.classList.remove('drag-over');
7753:         });
7754:         chip.addEventListener('drop', function (e) {
7755:             e.preventDefault();
7756:             chip.classList.remove('drag-over');
7757:             var fromIdx = parseInt(e.dataTransfer.getData('text/plain'), 10);
7758:             var toIdx = displayIdx;
7759:             if (fromIdx !== toIdx && !isNaN(fromIdx)) {
7760:                 // Reorder workingGroups locally
7761:                 var moved = workingGroups.splice(fromIdx, 1)[0];
7762:                 workingGroups.splice(toIdx, 0, moved);
7763:                 // Build overrides map
7764:                 var overrides = {};
7765:                 workingGroups.forEach(function (wg2, i) {
7766:                     overrides[wg2.id] = i;
7767:                 });
7768: 
7769:                 if (appState.isEditingStep) {
7770:                     // During active step edit: store as pending, attach on finish
7771:                     appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides = overrides;
7772:                 } else {
7773:                     // Not editing: auto-create standalone group-reorder step
7774:                     var reorderStep = {
7775:                         stepId: scenarioData.scenario.length + 1,
7776:                         duration: stepDuration ? parseFloat(stepDuration.value) : 1.0,
7777:                         actions: [],
7778:                         groupOrderOverrides: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(overrides))
7779:                     };
7780: 
7781:                     // Apply overrides to actual group.groupOrder
7782:                     var groups2 = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || [];
7783:                     groups2.forEach(function (g) {
7784:                         if (overrides[g.id] !== undefined) {
7785:                             g.groupOrder = overrides[g.id];
7786:                         }
7787:                     });
7788: 
7789:                     // Take snapshot for replay
7790:                     var snap = takeSnapshot();
7791:                     scenarioData.scenario.push(reorderStep);
7792:                     stepSnapshots.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(snap)));
7793: 
7794:                     totalSteps.textContent = scenarioData.scenario.length;
7795:                     renderTimeline();
7796:                     updateUI();
7797:                     setStatus('Step ' + reorderStep.stepId + ' auto-created: group order changed', 'success');
7798:                 }
7799:                 renderGroupOrderStrip();
7800:             }
7801:         });
7802: 
7803:         strip.appendChild(chip);
7804:     });
7805: }
7806: 
7807: // ============================================
7808: // TIMELINE MODULES INTEGRATION
7809: // ============================================
7810: 
7811: // Module instances (lazy init)
7812: let timelineModules = null;
7813: let timelineUI = null;
7814: 
7815: /**
7816:  * Initialize timeline modules integration
7817:  * This is called from init() and sets up all new timeline functionality
7818:  */
7819: function initTimelineModulesIntegration() {
7820:     // Check if modules are available
7821:     if (typeof TIMELINE_FEATURE_FLAGS === 'undefined') {
7822:         console.log('[Timeline] Modules not loaded - skipping initialization');
7823:         return;
7824:     }
7825: 
7826:     if (!TIMELINE_FEATURE_FLAGS.ENABLED) {
7827:         console.log('[Timeline] Modules disabled via feature flag');
7828:         return;
7829:     }
7830: 
7831:     console.log('[Timeline] Initializing modules integration...');
7832: 
7833:     try {
7834:         // Initialize core modules
7835:         timelineModules = initTimelineModules(
7836:             scenarioData,
7837:             stepSnapshots,
7838:             restoreFromSnapshot
7839:         );
7840: 
7841:         if (!timelineModules) {
7842:             console.warn('[Timeline] Module initialization returned null');
7843:             return;
7844:         }
7845: 
7846:         // Initialize Timeline UI if container exists
7847:         const timelineBar = document.getElementById('timelineBar');
7848:         if (timelineBar && TIMELINE_FEATURE_FLAGS.TIMELINE_UI) {
7849:             timelineUI = new TimelineUI(timelineBar, {
7850:                 timelineManager: timelineModules.timelineManager,
7851:                 playbackController: timelineModules.playbackController,
7852:                 onStepSelect: handleTimelineStepSelect,
7853:                 onStepEdit: handleTimelineStepEdit,
7854:                 onStepMove: handleTimelineStepMove
7855:             });
7856: 
7857:             // Handle clear timeline
7858:             timelineUI.on('clearTimeline', function () {
7859:                 scenarioData.scenario = [];
7860:                 stepSnapshots = [];
7861:                 pendingChangeSnapshot = null; // Clear stale snapshot to prevent ghost steps
7862:                 if (timelineModules.timelineManager) {
7863:                     timelineModules.timelineManager.clearSteps();
7864:                 }
7865:                 timelineUI.render();
7866:                 totalSteps.textContent = '0';
7867:                 if (typeof restoreToInitialState === 'function') {
7868:                     restoreToInitialState();
7869:                 }
7870:                 // Re-save initial state so new recordings start fresh
7871:                 if (typeof saveInitialStateForExport === 'function') {
7872:                     saveInitialStateForExport();
7873:                 }
7874:                 // Save a fresh snapshot[0] for the new recording session
7875:                 stepSnapshots.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(scenarioData.initialState)));
7876:                 setStatus('Timeline cleared');
7877:                 console.log('[Timeline] All steps cleared');
7878:             });
7879: 
7880:             // Initial render
7881:             timelineUI.render();
7882:             console.log('[Timeline] UI initialized');
7883:         }
7884: 
7885:         // Hook into existing functions to sync with timeline modules
7886:         hookTimelineFunctions();
7887: 
7888:         // Run tests in development
7889:         if (typeof TIMELINE_FEATURE_FLAGS !== 'undefined' && location.hostname === 'localhost') {
7890:             // Uncomment to run tests automatically
7891:             // timelineModules.runTests();
7892:         }
7893: 
7894:         console.log('[Timeline] Integration complete');
7895: 
7896:     } catch (error) {
7897:         console.error('[Timeline] Error initializing modules:', error);
7898:     }
7899: }
7900: 
7901: /**
7902:  * Hook into existing functions to sync timeline modules
7903:  */
7904: function hookTimelineFunctions() {
7905:     if (!timelineModules) return;
7906: 
7907:     const { timelineManager, snapshotManager, stepPropertyManager } = timelineModules;
7908: 
7909:     // Hook handleFinishStep to sync with timeline manager
7910:     const originalHandleFinishStep = handleFinishStep;
7911:     handleFinishStep = function () {
7912:         // Call original implementation
7913:         originalHandleFinishStep();
7914: 
7915:         // Sync with timeline modules after step is created
7916:         syncTimelineModulesWithSteps();
7917:     };
7918: 
7919:     // Hook property changes for per-step property storage
7920:     if (TIMELINE_FEATURE_FLAGS.PER_STEP_PROPS) {
7921:         const originalHandlePropertyChange = handlePropertyChange;
7922:         handlePropertyChange = function () {
7923:             // Store in per-step manager during editing
7924:             if (appState.isEditingStep && appState.selectedCard) {
7925:                 const cardId = appState.selectedCard.id;
7926:                 const stepIndex = appState.currentStepIndex;
7927: 
7928:                 stepPropertyManager.setPendingProperty(cardId, 'flip', {
7929:                     enabled: flipCardCheck.checked,
7930:                     toFaceUp: appState.selectedCard.isFaceUp
7931:                 });
7932: 
7933:                 stepPropertyManager.setPendingProperty(cardId, 'slam', {
7934:                     enabled: slamEffectCheck.checked
7935:                 });
7936: 
7937:                 stepPropertyManager.setPendingProperty(cardId, 'spin', {
7938:                     enabled: spinEffectCheck.checked
7939:                 });
7940:             }
7941: 
7942:             // Still call original to update card object
7943:             originalHandlePropertyChange();
7944:         };
7945:     }
7946: 
7947:     // Hook handleAutoStepYes to sync with snapshotManager
7948:     const originalHandleAutoStepYes = handleAutoStepYes;
7949:     handleAutoStepYes = function () {
7950:         // Call original implementation
7951:         originalHandleAutoStepYes();
7952: 
7953:         // Sync with timeline modules after step is created
7954:         syncTimelineModulesWithSteps();
7955:     };
7956: 
7957:     // Hook handleFinishStep that we already defined above also needs to sync
7958:     // The handleFinishStep hook is already defined above, but let's make sure
7959:     // auto-step also triggers timeline UI update
7960: 
7961:     console.log('[Timeline] Functions hooked');
7962: }
7963: 
7964: /**
7965:  * Get step color (cycling through palette)
7966:  */
7967: function getStepColor(stepId) {
7968:     const colors = ['#4CAF50', '#2196F3', '#FF9800', '#E91E63', '#9C27B0', '#00BCD4', '#FF5722'];
7969:     return colors[(stepId - 1) % colors.length];
7970: }
7971: 
7972: /**
7973:  * Handle timeline step selection
7974:  */
7975: function handleTimelineStepSelect(step, index) {
7976:     console.log('[Timeline] Step selected:', step.stepId);
7977: 
7978:     // Jump playback to this step
7979:     if (timelineModules && timelineModules.playbackController) {
7980:         timelineModules.playbackController.jumpToStep(index);
7981:     }
7982: 
7983:     // Highlight in existing timeline preview
7984:     const existingBlocks = document.querySelectorAll('.timeline-step');
7985:     existingBlocks.forEach(block => block.classList.remove('selected'));
7986: }
7987: 
7988: /**
7989:  * Handle timeline step edit request
7990:  */
7991: function handleTimelineStepEdit(step, index) {
7992:     console.log('[Timeline] Edit requested for step:', step.stepId);
7993: 
7994:     // Show warning if there are subsequent steps
7995:     if (index < scenarioData.scenario.length - 1) {
7996:         showWarningModal(`Editing Step ${step.stepId} may affect subsequent steps. Continue?`, () => {
7997:             startEditingStep(index);
7998:         });
7999:     } else {
8000:         startEditingStep(index);
8001:     }
8002: }
8003: 
8004: /**
8005:  * Start editing an existing step
8006:  */
8007: function startEditingStep(stepIndex) {
8008:     if (appState.isEditingStep) {
8009:         setStatus('Finish current step first', 'error');
8010:         return;
8011:     }
8012: 
8013:     // Restore to state before this step
8014:     const snapshot = stepSnapshots[stepIndex];
8015:     if (snapshot) {
8016:         restoreFromSnapshot(snapshot);
8017:     }
8018: 
8019:     // Enter edit mode
8020:     appState.isEditingStep = true;
8021:     appState.currentStepIndex = stepIndex;
8022: 
8023:     const step = scenarioData.scenario[stepIndex];
8024:     currentStep = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(step));
8025:     startSnapshot = snapshot;
8026: 
8027:     // Update UI
8028:     if (stepDuration) stepDuration.value = step.duration || 1.0;
8029:     if (finishStepBtn) {
8030:         finishStepBtn.disabled = false;
8031:         finishStepBtn.textContent = '✓ Update Step';
8032:     }
8033:     if (addStepBtn) addStepBtn.disabled = true;
8034:     if (recordingIndicator) recordingIndicator.classList.add('active');
8035:     if (currentStepNum) currentStepNum.textContent = step.stepId;
8036: 
8037:     setStatus(`Editing Step ${step.stepId} - Move cards and click Update`, 'recording');
8038: }

8063: /**
8064:  * Sync timeline modules with current step data
8065:  * Called after any step is created or modified
8066:  */
8067: function syncTimelineModulesWithSteps() {
8068:     if (!timelineModules) {
8069:         console.log('[Timeline] No modules to sync');
8070:         return;
8071:     }
8072: 
8073:     const { snapshotManager, timelineManager } = timelineModules;
8074: 
8075:     // Sync snapshots from stepSnapshots array to snapshotManager
8076:     if (stepSnapshots.length > 0) {
8077:         console.log('[Timeline] Syncing', stepSnapshots.length, 'snapshots');
8078:         snapshotManager.loadFromArray(stepSnapshots);
8079:     }
8080: 
8081:     // Sync step timing
8082:     if (scenarioData.scenario.length > 0) {
8083:         let currentTime = 0;
8084:         scenarioData.scenario.forEach((step) => {
8085:             if (step.startTime === undefined) {
8086:                 step.startTime = currentTime;
8087:             }
8088:             if (step.endTime === undefined) {
8089:                 step.endTime = step.startTime + (step.duration || 1.0);
8090:             }
8091:             if (!step.label) step.label = `Step ${step.stepId}`;
8092:             if (!step.color) step.color = getStepColor(step.stepId);
8093:             currentTime = step.endTime;
8094:         });
8095: 
8096:         // Update timeline total duration
8097:         if (scenarioData.timeline) {
8098:             scenarioData.timeline.totalDuration = currentTime;
8099:         }
8100:     }
8101: 
8102:     // Update timeline UI
8103:     if (timelineUI) {
8104:         timelineUI.render();
8105:     }
8106: 
8107:     console.log('[Timeline] Sync complete. Steps:', scenarioData.scenario.length, 'Snapshots:', snapshotManager.getSnapshotCount());
8108: }

8171: /**
8172:  * Toggle card selection for grouping
8173:  * Called when clicking a card in grouping mode
8174:  * Each selection/deselection triggers auto-step popup to record as separate step
8175:  */
8176: function toggleCardGroupSelection(card) {
8177:     console.log('[GroupSelect] Before - groupedCards:', appState.groupedCards.length);
8178: 
8179:     // Take snapshot BEFORE the selection change (for recording)
8180:     const snapshotBeforeChange = takeSnapshot();
8181: 
8182:     const index = appState.groupedCards.findIndex(c => c.id === card.id);
8183: 
8184:     if (index === -1) {
8185:         // Add to group (SELECT)
8186:         appState.groupedCards.push(card);
8187:         card.element?.classList.add('grouped');
8188:         console.log('[GroupSelect] Added card:', card.id, 'groupedCards:', appState.groupedCards.length);
8189:     } else {
8190:         // Remove from group (DESELECT)
8191:         appState.groupedCards.splice(index, 1);
8192:         card.element?.classList.remove('grouped');
8193:         console.log('[GroupSelect] Removed card:', card.id, 'groupedCards:', appState.groupedCards.length);
8194:     }
8195: 
8196:     // Update count display
8197:     updateGroupCount();
8198: 
8199:     console.log('[GroupSelect] After - groupedCards:', appState.groupedCards.length);
8200: 
8201:     // Trigger auto-step popup for this selection change (Record mode only)
8202:     if (appState.phase === 'record' && !appState.isEditingStep) {
8203:         showAutoStepPopup(card, snapshotBeforeChange);
8204:     }
8205: }

8229: /**
8230:  * Start the auto-record countdown
8231:  */
8232: function startAutoRecordCountdown() {
8233:     // Cancel any existing countdown
8234:     cancelAutoRecordCountdown();
8235: 
8236:     appState.countdownValue = appState.autoRecordDelay;
8237: 
8238:     // Show countdown display
8239:     if (countdownDisplay) countdownDisplay.classList.remove('hidden');
8240:     if (countdownTimer) countdownTimer.textContent = appState.countdownValue;
8241:     if (countdownBarFill) countdownBarFill.style.width = '100%';
8242: 
8243:     // Start interval timer
8244:     appState.countdownTimer = setInterval(() => {
8245:         appState.countdownValue--;
8246: 
8247:         // Update timer display
8248:         if (countdownTimer) countdownTimer.textContent = appState.countdownValue;
8249: 
8250:         // Update progress bar
8251:         if (countdownBarFill) {
8252:             const progress = (appState.countdownValue / appState.autoRecordDelay) * 100;
8253:             countdownBarFill.style.width = `${progress}%`;
8254:         }
8255: 
8256:         // Countdown finished — auto-accept step
8257:         if (appState.countdownValue <= 0) {
8258:             cancelAutoRecordCountdown();
8259:             handleAutoStepYes();
8260:         }
8261:     }, 1000);
8262: }
8263: 
8264: /**
8265:  * Cancel the auto-record countdown
8266:  */
8267: function cancelAutoRecordCountdown() {
8268:     if (appState.countdownTimer) {
8269:         clearInterval(appState.countdownTimer);
8270:         appState.countdownTimer = null;
8271:     }
8272:     appState.countdownValue = 0;
8273: 
8274:     // Hide countdown display
8275:     if (countdownDisplay) countdownDisplay.classList.add('hidden');
8276: }
8277: 
8278: /**
8279:  * Auto-save step with grouped cards
8280:  */
8281: function autoSaveGroupedStep() {
8282:     if (appState.groupedCards.length === 0) {
8283:         setStatus('No cards selected', 'error');
8284:         return;
8285:     }
8286: 
8287:     // Get the snapshot before changes
8288:     const startSnap = pendingChangeSnapshot || takeSnapshot();
8289: 
8290:     // Take current snapshot (after selections)
8291:     const endSnap = takeSnapshot();
8292: 
8293:     // Compute actions from start to end
8294:     const actions = computeActions(startSnap, endSnap);
8295: 
8296:     // Create the step
8297:     const newStep = {
8298:         stepId: scenarioData.scenario.length + 1,
8299:         duration: stepDuration ? parseFloat(stepDuration.value) : 1.0,
8300:         actions: actions
8301:     };
8302: 
8303:     // BUG #4 fix: attach pending group order overrides
8304:     if (appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides) {
8305:         newStep.groupOrderOverrides = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides));
8306:         var groups = appState.boardLayout.slotGroups || [];
8307:         groups.forEach(function (g) {
8308:             if (appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides[g.id] !== undefined) {
8309:                 g.groupOrder = appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides[g.id];
8310:             }
8311:         });
8312:         appState.pendingGroupOrderOverrides = null;
8313:     }
8314: 
8315:     // Add to scenario
8316:     scenarioData.scenario.push(newStep);
8317: 
8318:     // Save snapshot for replay
8319:     stepSnapshots.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(endSnap)));
8320: 
8321:     // Update UI
8322:     totalSteps.textContent = scenarioData.scenario.length;
8323:     renderTimeline();
8324: 
8325:     // Clear state
8326:     clearGroupedCards();
8327:     pendingChangeSnapshot = null;
8328: 
8329:     setStatus(`Step ${newStep.stepId} saved with ${actions.length} actions (auto-recorded)`, 'success');
8330:     updateUI();
8331: }
8332: 
8333: /**
8334:  * Show/hide grouping section based on phase
8335:  */
8336: function updateGroupingSectionVisibility() {
8337:     if (groupingSection) {
8338:         if (appState.phase === 'record') {
8339:             groupingSection.classList.remove('hidden');
8340:         } else {
8341:             groupingSection.classList.add('hidden');
8342:             // Disable grouping when leaving record phase
8343:             if (appState.groupingMode) {
8344:                 appState.groupingMode = false;
8345:                 if (groupingModeToggle) groupingModeToggle.checked = false;
8346:                 document.body.classList.remove('grouping-mode-active');
8347:                 clearGroupedCards();
8348:                 cancelAutoRecordCountdown();
8349:             }
8350:         }
8351:     }
8352: }

8354: /**
8355:  * Handle dropping all grouped cards to a zone
8356:  * @param {HTMLElement} zone - Target zone element
8357:  */
8358: function handleGroupedCardsDrop(zone) {
8359:     console.log('[GroupDrop] Called with zone:', zone?.dataset?.zone, 'groupedCards:', appState.groupedCards.length);
8360:     if (appState.groupedCards.length === 0) return;
8361: 
8362:     // Use pendingChangeSnapshot if available (captured when first card was selected)
8363:     // Otherwise take a new snapshot
8364:     const snapshotBeforeMove = pendingChangeSnapshot || takeSnapshot();
8365:     console.log('[GroupDrop] snapshotBeforeMove exists:', !!snapshotBeforeMove);
8366: 
8367:     const zoneName = zone.dataset.zone;
8368:     const rotation = parseInt(zone.dataset.rotation) || 0;
8369: 
8370:     // Collect old zones for later re-render
8371:     const oldZones = new Set();
8372: 
8373:     // Move each grouped card to the target zone
8374:     appState.groupedCards.forEach(card => {
8375:         if (card.zone && card.zone !== zoneName) {
8376:             oldZones.add(card.zone);
8377:         }
8378:         if (card.element) {
8379:             card.element.remove();
8380:         }
8381:         card.zone = zoneName;
8382:         card.rotation = rotation;
8383: 
8384:         const flipCheckbox = document.querySelector(`#flip${zoneName.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + zoneName.slice(1)}`);
8385:         if (flipCheckbox) {
8386:             card.isFaceUp = flipCheckbox.checked;
8387:         }
8388:     });
8389: 
8390:     // Recalculate positions for old zones
8391:     oldZones.forEach(oldZoneName => {
8392:         const oldZoneCards = appState.tableCards.filter(c => c.zone === oldZoneName);
8393:         oldZoneCards.forEach((c, idx) => {
8394:             c.zonePosition = idx;
8395:         });
8396:         const oldZoneElement = document.querySelector(
8397:             `.player-zone[data-zone="${oldZoneName}"], .community-zone[data-zone="${oldZoneName}"], .card-drop-zone[data-zone="${oldZoneName}"]`
8398:         );
8399:         if (oldZoneElement) {
8400:             rerenderZoneCards(oldZoneName, oldZoneElement);
8401:         }
8402:     });
8403: 
8404:     // Assign consecutive positions in new zone
8405:     const existingCardsInZone = appState.tableCards.filter(
8406:         c => c.zone === zoneName && !appState.groupedCards.some(gc => gc.id === c.id)
8407:     );
8408:     let nextPos = existingCardsInZone.length;
8409: 
8410:     appState.groupedCards.forEach(card => {
8411:         card.zonePosition = nextPos++;
8412:         createZoneCardElement(card, zone);
8413:     });
8414: 
8415:     const movedCount = appState.groupedCards.length;
8416:     updateUI();
8417:     setStatus(`Moved ${movedCount} cards to ${zoneName} zone`);
8418:     console.log('[GroupDrop] Moved', movedCount, 'cards to', zoneName);
8419: 
8420:     // Clear grouped cards after move
8421:     clearGroupedCards();
8422: 
8423:     // Show auto-step popup if in record mode
8424:     console.log('[GroupDrop] phase:', appState.phase, 'isEditingStep:', appState.isEditingStep, 'autoStepPopup:', !!autoStepPopup);
8425:     if (appState.phase === 'record' && !appState.isEditingStep) {
8426:         console.log('[GroupDrop] Calling showAutoStepPopup');
8427:         showAutoStepPopup(null, snapshotBeforeMove);
8428:     }
8429: }

8466: // ============================================
