8469: 
8470: /**
8471:  * Handle ref image file selection
8472:  */
8473: function handleRefImageAttach(e) {
8474:     const files = Array.from(e.target.files || []);
8475:     if (files.length === 0) return;
8476: 
8477:     // Limit to 3 images
8478:     const maxImages = 3;
8479:     const remaining = maxImages - aiRefImages.length;
8480:     const toAdd = files.slice(0, remaining);
8481: 
8482:     for (const file of toAdd) {
8483:         const reader = new FileReader();
8484:         reader.onload = function (evt) {
8485:             const base64 = evt.target.result.split(',')[1]; // Remove data:image/...;base64, prefix
8486:             const mimeType = file.type || 'image/jpeg';
8487:             aiRefImages.push({ data: base64, mimeType: mimeType, name: file.name });
8488:             renderAttachPreview();
8489:         };
8490:         reader.readAsDataURL(file);
8491:     }
8492: 
8493:     // Reset input so same file can be re-selected
8494:     e.target.value = '';
8495: }
8496: 
8497: /**
8498:  * Handle ref video file selection
8499:  */
8500: function handleRefVideoAttach(e) {
8501:     const file = e.target.files && e.target.files[0];
8502:     if (!file) return;
8503: 
8504:     aiVideoFile = file;
8505:     aiVideoFrames = [];
8506:     renderAttachPreview();
8507: 
8508:     // Extract frames from video
8509:     extractVideoFrames(file).then(function (frames) {
8510:         aiVideoFrames = frames;
8511:         renderAttachPreview();
8512:         debugLog('[AI] Extracted ' + frames.length + ' frames from video: ' + file.name);
8513:     }).catch(function (err) {
8514:         console.error('[AI] Video frame extraction failed:', err);
8515:         debugLog('[AI] Video frame extraction failed: ' + err.message);
8516:     });
8517: 
8518:     e.target.value = '';
8519: }
8520: 
8521: /**
8522:  * Extract frames from a video file using HTML5 canvas
8523:  */
8524: function extractVideoFrames(file, maxFrames) {
8525:     maxFrames = maxFrames || 10;
8526:     return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
8527:         const url = URL.createObjectURL(file);
8528:         const video = document.createElement('video');
8529:         video.muted = true;
8530:         video.preload = 'auto';
8531: 
8532:         video.onloadedmetadata = function () {
8533:             const duration = video.duration;
8534:             if (!duration || duration <= 0) {
8535:                 URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
8536:                 return reject(new Error('Invalid video duration'));
8537:             }
8538: 
8539:             const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
8540:             const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
8541: 
8542:             // Scale down for smaller payload (max 640px wide)
8543:             const scale = Math.min(1, 640 / video.videoWidth);
8544:             canvas.width = Math.round(video.videoWidth * scale);
8545:             canvas.height = Math.round(video.videoHeight * scale);
8546: 
8547:             const frameCount = Math.min(maxFrames, Math.floor(duration));
8548:             const interval = duration / (frameCount + 1);
8549:             const frames = [];
8550:             let currentFrame = 0;
8551: 
8552:             function captureFrame() {
8553:                 if (currentFrame >= frameCount) {
8554:                     URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
8555:                     resolve(frames);
8556:                     return;
8557:                 }
8558: 
8559:                 const seekTime = interval * (currentFrame + 1);
8560:                 video.currentTime = seekTime;
8561:             }
8562: 
8563:             video.onseeked = function () {
8564:                 ctx.drawImage(video, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
8565:                 const dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.7);
8566:                 const base64 = dataUrl.split(',')[1];
8567:                 frames.push({ data: base64, mimeType: 'image/jpeg' });
8568:                 currentFrame++;
8569:                 captureFrame();
8570:             };
8571: 
8572:             captureFrame();
8573:         };
8574: 
8575:         video.onerror = function () {
8576:             URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
8577:             reject(new Error('Failed to load video'));
8578:         };
8579: 
8580:         video.src = url;
8581:     });
8582: }
8583: 
8584: /**
8585:  * Render attachment preview area
8586:  */
8587: function renderAttachPreview() {
8588:     if (!aiAttachPreview) return;
8589: 
8590:     var html = '';
8591: 
8592:     for (var i = 0; i < aiRefImages.length; i++) {
8593:         var img = aiRefImages[i];
8594:         html += '<div class="ai-attach-item">' +
8595:             '<img src="data:' + img.mimeType + ';base64,' + img.data + '" alt="ref">' +
8596:             '<span>' + (img.name || 'Image ' + (i + 1)) + '</span>' +
8597:             '<button class="ai-attach-remove" data-type="image" data-index="' + i + '" title="Remove">×</button>' +
8598:             '</div>';
8599:     }
8600: 
8601:     if (aiVideoFile) {
8602:         var frameInfo = aiVideoFrames.length > 0 ? ' (' + aiVideoFrames.length + ' frames)' : ' (extracting...)';
8603:         html += '<div class="ai-attach-item">' +
8604:             '<span>🎬 ' + aiVideoFile.name + frameInfo + '</span>' +
8605:             '<button class="ai-attach-remove" data-type="video" data-index="0" title="Remove">×</button>' +
8606:             '</div>';
8607:     }
8608: 
8609:     if (html) {
8610:         aiAttachPreview.innerHTML = html;
8611:         aiAttachPreview.classList.remove('hidden');
8612: 
8613:         aiAttachPreview.querySelectorAll('.ai-attach-remove').forEach(function (btn) {
8614:             btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
8615:                 var type = this.getAttribute('data-type');
8616:                 var idx = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-index'));
8617:                 if (type === 'image') aiRefImages.splice(idx, 1);
8618:                 else { aiVideoFile = null; aiVideoFrames = []; }
8619:                 renderAttachPreview();
8620:             });
8621:         });
8622:     } else {
8623:         aiAttachPreview.innerHTML = '';
8624:         aiAttachPreview.classList.add('hidden');
8625:     }
8626: }
8627: 
8628: /**
8629:  * Get the API base URL from config
8630:  */
8631: function getAPIBaseUrl() {
8632:     if (typeof API_BASE_URL !== 'undefined' && API_BASE_URL) {
8633:         return API_BASE_URL;
8634:     }
8635:     return 'https://banner-generator-ai.vercel.app';
8636: }
8637: 
8638: /**
8639:  * Handle AI Generate button click
8640:  */
8641: async function handleAIGenerate() {
8642:     var brief = aiBriefInput ? aiBriefInput.value.trim() : '';
8643:     if (!brief) {
8644:         showAIError('Please describe your desired card layout.');
8645:         return;
8646:     }
8647: 
8648:     var availableCards = (appState.trayCards || []).filter(function (c) { return c.inTray !== false; });
8649:     if (availableCards.length === 0) {
8650:         showAIError('No cards available. Load a deck first.');
8651:         return;
8652:     }
8653: 
8654:     // BUG FIX: Read target layout from dropdown and load it BEFORE collecting slot IDs.
8655:     // Without this, selecting "Pusoy" while board is "Poker" sends Poker slot IDs to AI,
8656:     // causing all card placements to fail (slot IDs don't exist in the response layout).
8657:     var targetPreset = aiPresetSelect ? aiPresetSelect.value : 'current';
8658:     if (targetPreset !== 'current') {
8659:         var psEl = document.getElementById('presetSelect');
8660:         if (psEl) {
8661:             psEl.value = targetPreset;
8662:             handleLoadPreset();
8663:             debugLog('[AI] Switched board to target layout: ' + targetPreset);
8664:         }
8665:     }
8666: 
8667:     var slots = appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces || [];
8668:     if (slots.length === 0) {
8669:         showAIError('No card slots on the board. Load a preset first.');
8670:         return;
8671:     }
8672: 
8673:     var availableCardNames = availableCards.map(function (c) { return c.name; });
8674:     var availableSlotIds = slots.map(function (s) { return s.id; });
8675:     debugLog('[AI] Target preset: ' + targetPreset + ', slot IDs: ' + availableSlotIds.join(', '));
8676: 
8677:     // Check mode toggle
8678:     var aiModeRadio = document.querySelector('input[name="aiMode"]:checked');
8679:     var aiMode = aiModeRadio ? aiModeRadio.value : 'setup';
8680:     var isScenarioMode = aiMode === 'scenario';
8681: 
8682:     if (aiGenerateBtn) {
8683:         aiGenerateBtn.disabled = true;
8684:         aiGenerateBtn.classList.add('loading');
8685:     }
8686:     var attachInfo = '';
8687:     if (aiRefImages.length > 0) attachInfo += ' + ' + aiRefImages.length + ' ref image(s)';
8688:     if (aiVideoFrames.length > 0) attachInfo += ' + ' + aiVideoFrames.length + ' video frames';
8689:     showAIStatus(isScenarioMode ? '🎬 Generating scenario with AI...' + attachInfo : '🤖 Generating layout with AI...' + attachInfo);
8690:     hideAIError();
8691: 
8692:     try {
8693:         var token = typeof getToken === 'function' ? getToken() : localStorage.getItem('autonim_poker_token');
8694: 
8695:         var apiBase = getAPIBaseUrl();
8696:         var endpoint = isScenarioMode ? '/api/poker/ai-generate-scenario' : '/api/poker/ai-generate';
8697:         var response = await fetch(apiBase + endpoint, {
8698:             method: 'POST',
8699:             headers: {
8700:                 'Content-Type': 'application/json',
8701:                 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token
8702:             },
8703:             body: JSON.stringify({
8704:                 brief: brief,
8705:                 availableCards: availableCardNames,
8706:                 availableSlotIds: availableSlotIds,
8707:                 targetPreset: targetPreset,
8708:                 refImages: aiRefImages.length > 0 ? aiRefImages : undefined,
8709:                 videoFrames: aiVideoFrames.length > 0 ? aiVideoFrames : undefined
8710:             })
8711:         });
8712: 
8713:         if (!response.ok) {
8714:             var errData = await response.json().catch(function () { return {}; });
8715:             throw new Error(errData.error || 'Server error (' + response.status + ')');
8716:         }
8717: 
8718:         var result = await response.json();
8719:         console.log('[AI] Full response:', JSON.stringify(result, null, 2));
8720: 
8721:         if (isScenarioMode) {
8722:             // === SCENARIO MODE ===
8723:             if ((!result.initialSetup || result.initialSetup.length === 0) && (!result.steps || result.steps.length === 0)) {
8724:                 showAIError('AI returned no setup or steps. Try a more detailed brief.');
8725:                 return;
8726:             }
8727: 
8728:             showAIStatus('🎬 Applying scenario: ' + (result.initialSetup?.length || 0) + ' cards + ' + (result.steps?.length || 0) + ' steps...');
8729:             await applyAIScenario(result);
8730: 
8731:             // Build status
8732:             var statusParts = ['✅ Scenario applied! ' + (result.initialSetup?.length || 0) + ' cards, ' + (result.steps?.length || 0) + ' steps.'];
8733:             if (result.reasoning) statusParts.push('💭 AI: ' + result.reasoning);
8734:             if (result.debug) {
8735:                 var d = result.debug;
8736:                 var debugParts = ['Model: ' + d.model];
8737:                 if (d.warnings && d.warnings.length > 0) debugParts.push('⚠ ' + d.warnings.length + ' warnings');
8738:                 if (d.invalidCardRefs && d.invalidCardRefs.length > 0) debugParts.push('⚠ Invalid cards: ' + d.invalidCardRefs.join(', '));
8739:                 statusParts.push('📊 ' + debugParts.join(' | '));
8740:             }
8741:             showAIStatus(statusParts.join('\n'));
8742: 
8743:         } else {
8744:             // === SETUP MODE (existing behavior) ===
8745:             if (!result.cardAssignments || result.cardAssignments.length === 0) {
8746:                 showAIError('AI returned no card assignments. Try a different brief.');
8747:                 return;
8748:             }
8749: 
8750:             showAIStatus('✅ AI generated ' + result.cardAssignments.length + ' card placements. Applying...');
8751:             await applyAILayout(result);
8752: 
8753:             var statusParts = ['✅ Done! ' + result.cardAssignments.length + ' cards placed.'];
8754:             if (result.reasoning) statusParts.push('💭 AI: ' + result.reasoning);
8755:             if (result.debug) {
8756:                 var d = result.debug;
8757:                 var debugParts = ['Model: ' + d.model];
8758:                 if (d.invalidCards && d.invalidCards.length > 0) debugParts.push('⚠ Invalid cards: ' + d.invalidCards.join(', '));
8759:                 if (d.invalidSlots && d.invalidSlots.length > 0) debugParts.push('⚠ Invalid slots: ' + d.invalidSlots.join(', '));
8760:                 if (d.duplicatesRemoved > 0) debugParts.push('⚠ ' + d.duplicatesRemoved + ' duplicates removed');
8761:                 statusParts.push('📊 ' + debugParts.join(' | '));
8762:             }
8763:             showAIStatus(statusParts.join('\n'));
8764:             debugLog('[AI] Reasoning: ' + (result.reasoning || 'none'));
8765:         }
8766: 
8767:     } catch (error) {
8768:         console.error('[AI] Generate error:', error);
8769:         showAIError(error.message || 'AI generation failed. Please try again.');
8770:     } finally {
8771:         if (aiGenerateBtn) {
8772:             aiGenerateBtn.disabled = false;
8773:             aiGenerateBtn.classList.remove('loading');
8774:         }
8775:     }
8776: }
8777: 
8778: /**
8779:  * Apply AI-generated layout to the board
8780:  */
8781: async function applyAILayout(result) {
8782:     // NOTE: Do NOT re-load preset here. handleAIGenerate() already loaded the
8783:     // correct preset BEFORE collecting slot IDs and sending them to the API.
8784:     // Re-loading a different preset (e.g. server returning "pusoy" when user
8785:     // selected "poker") would cause slot ID mismatch and cards flying off-grid.
8786: 
8787:     handleResetTable();
8788:     await new Promise(function (r) { setTimeout(r, 100); });
8789: 
8790:     var placedCount = 0;
8791:     var errors = [];
8792: 
8793:     for (var i = 0; i < result.cardAssignments.length; i++) {
8794:         var assignment = result.cardAssignments[i];
8795:         var slotId = assignment.slotId;
8796:         var cardName = assignment.cardName;
8797:         var faceUp = assignment.faceUp;
8798: 
8799:         var card = null;
8800:         if (typeof resolveCardName === 'function') {
8801:             card = resolveCardName(cardName, appState.trayCards.filter(function (c) { return c.inTray !== false; }));
8802:         }
8803:         if (!card) {
8804:             card = appState.trayCards.find(function (c) {
8805:                 return c.inTray !== false && c.name === cardName;
8806:             });
8807:         }
8808:         if (!card) {
8809:             errors.push('Card not found: ' + cardName);
8810:             continue;
8811:         }
8812: 
8813:         var place = (appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces || []).find(function (p) { return p.id === slotId; });
8814:         if (!place) {
8815:             errors.push('Slot not found: ' + slotId);
8816:             continue;
8817:         }
8818: 
8819:         var zoneName = 'grid-' + slotId;
8820:         var zoneElement = document.querySelector('.card-drop-zone[data-zone="' + zoneName + '"]');
8821: 
8822:         if (zoneElement) {
8823:             card.isFaceUp = faceUp === true;
8824:             placeCardInZone(card, zoneName, place.rotation || 0, zoneElement);
8825:         } else {
8826:             card.isFaceUp = faceUp === true;
8827:             placeCardOnTable(card, place.x || 640, place.y || 360);
8828:         }
8829:         placedCount++;
8830:     }
8831: 
8832:     if (errors.length > 0) {
8833:         debugLog('[AI] Placement errors:', errors);
8834:         console.warn('[AI] Some cards could not be placed:', errors);
8835:     }
8836: 
8837:     debugLog('[AI] Applied layout: ' + placedCount + ' cards placed, ' + errors.length + ' errors');
8838:     setStatus('AI placed ' + placedCount + ' cards on the board', 'success');
8839: }
8840: 
8841: /**
8842:  * Find a card in the tray by name (supports fuzzy matching via resolveCardName)
8843:  */
8844: function findTrayCardByName(cardName) {
8845:     var card = null;
8846:     if (typeof resolveCardName === 'function') {
8847:         card = resolveCardName(cardName, appState.trayCards.filter(function (c) { return c.inTray !== false; }));
8848:     }
8849:     if (!card) {
8850:         card = appState.trayCards.find(function (c) {
8851:             return c.inTray !== false && c.name === cardName;
8852:         });
8853:     }
8854:     return card;
8855: }
8856: 
8857: /**
8858:  * Find a card on the table by name
8859:  */
8860: function findTableCardByName(cardName) {
8861:     return appState.tableCards.find(function (c) {
8862:         return c.name === cardName;
8863:     });
8864: }
8865: 
8866: /**
8867:  * Place a card silently into a slot (no popups, no status messages)
8868:  */
8869: function silentPlaceCard(cardName, slotId, faceUp) {
8870:     var card = findTrayCardByName(cardName);
8871:     if (!card) {
8872:         console.warn('[AI Scenario] Card not in tray: ' + cardName);
8873:         return false;
8874:     }
8875: 
8876:     var place = (appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces || []).find(function (p) { return p.id === slotId; });
8877:     if (!place) {
8878:         console.warn('[AI Scenario] Slot not found: ' + slotId);
8879:         return false;
8880:     }
8881: 
8882:     var zoneName = 'grid-' + slotId;
8883:     var zoneElement = document.querySelector('.card-drop-zone[data-zone="' + zoneName + '"]');
8884: 
8885:     var desiredFaceUp = faceUp === true;
8886:     card.isFaceUp = desiredFaceUp;
8887: 
8888:     if (zoneElement) {
8889:         placeCardInZone(card, zoneName, place.rotation || 0, zoneElement);
8890:     } else {
8891:         debugLog('[AI Scenario] Zone element NOT found for: ' + zoneName + ', falling back to placeCardOnTable(' + (place.x || 640) + ',' + (place.y || 360) + ')');
8892:         placeCardOnTable(card, place.x || 640, place.y || 360);
8893:     }
8894: 
8895:     // Re-set isFaceUp because placeCardInZone overrides it from UI checkboxes
8896:     card.isFaceUp = desiredFaceUp;
8897:     if (card.element) {
8898:         var img = card.element.querySelector('img');
8899:         if (img) {
8900:             img.src = desiredFaceUp ? (card.frontImageUrl || '') : (card.backImageUrl || '');
8901:         }
8902:         card.element.classList.toggle('face-up', desiredFaceUp);
8903:         card.element.classList.toggle('face-down', !desiredFaceUp);
8904:     }
8905:     return true;
8906: }
8907: 
8908: /**
8909:  * Apply AI-generated multi-step scenario to the board
8910:  * Creates initial setup + recording steps with proper snapshots
8911:  */
8912: async function applyAIScenario(result) {
8913:     // Save state for rollback on error
8914:     var savedScenario = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(scenarioData.scenario));
8915:     var savedSnapshots = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(stepSnapshots));
8916:     var wasRecordPhase = appState.phase === 'record';
8917: 
8918:     try {
8919:         // Suppress auto-step popups during bulk apply
8920:         appState._bulkApplying = true;
8921: 
8922:         // === STEP 0: Reset and apply initial setup ===
8923:         // NOTE: Do NOT re-load preset here. handleAIGenerate() already loaded
8924:         // the correct preset BEFORE collecting slot IDs. Re-loading a different
8925:         // preset from the server response would cause slot ID mismatch.
8926: 
8927:         handleResetTable();
8928:         await new Promise(function (r) { setTimeout(r, 100); });
8929: 
8930:         // Ensure grid drop zones are rendered before placement
8931:         if (appState.boardLayout.type === 'grid') {
8932:             renderCardDropZones();
8933:         }
8934: 
8935:         // Apply initial card placements
8936:         var setupCount = 0;
8937:         var setupErrors = [];
8938:         if (result.initialSetup && result.initialSetup.length > 0) {
8939:             for (var i = 0; i < result.initialSetup.length; i++) {
8940:                 var entry = result.initialSetup[i];
8941:                 if (silentPlaceCard(entry.card, entry.slot, entry.faceUp)) {
8942:                     setupCount++;
8943:                 } else {
8944:                     setupErrors.push(entry.card + ' → ' + entry.slot);
8945:                 }
8946:             }
8947:         }
8948: 
8949:         debugLog('[AI Scenario] Initial setup: ' + setupCount + ' cards placed, ' + setupErrors.length + ' errors');
8950:         if (setupErrors.length > 0) {
8951:             console.warn('[AI Scenario] Setup errors:', setupErrors);
8952:         }
8953: 
8954:         // Batch UI update after all cards placed
8955:         renderCardTray();
8956:         updateUI();
8957: 
8958:         // Switch to record phase (saveInitialState is SKIPPED due to _bulkApplying)
8959:         setPhase('record');
8960:         await new Promise(function (r) { setTimeout(r, 50); });
8961: 
8962:         // === Manually build scenarioData.initialState (since saveInitialState was skipped) ===
8963:         scenarioData.initialState = {};
8964:         appState.tableCards.forEach(function (card) {
8965:             scenarioData.initialState[card.id] = {
8966:                 x: card.x || 0,
8967:                 y: card.y || 0,
8968:                 rotation: card.rotation || 0,
8969:                 isFaceUp: card.isFaceUp,
8970:                 zone: card.zone,
8971:                 zonePosition: card.zonePosition || 0,
8972:                 zOrder: typeof computeZOrderForCard === 'function' ? computeZOrderForCard(card) : 0,
8973:                 flipAction: card.flipAction || false,
8974:                 slamEffect: card.slamEffect || false,
8975:                 isSelected: false
8976:             };
8977:         });
8978:         debugLog('[AI Scenario] Manual initialState built: ' + Object.keys(scenarioData.initialState).length + ' cards');
8979: 
8980:         // === Manually build snapshot management (since saveInitialState was skipped) ===
8981:         scenarioData.scenario = [];
8982:         stepSnapshots = [];
8983: 
8984:         // Build initial snapshot from current board state
8985:         var initialSnap = takeSnapshot();
8986:         stepSnapshots.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(initialSnap)));
8987: 
8988:         debugLog('[AI Scenario] Manual initial snapshot. tableCards=' + appState.tableCards.length + ', snapshot keys=' + Object.keys(initialSnap).length + ', stepSnapshots.length=' + stepSnapshots.length);
8989: 
8990:         // === APPLY STEPS SEQUENTIALLY ===
8991:         if (result.steps && result.steps.length > 0) {
8992:             for (var si = 0; si < result.steps.length; si++) {
8993:                 var step = result.steps[si];
8994:                 debugLog('[AI Scenario] Processing step ' + (si + 1) + ': "' + step.label + '"');
8995: 
8996:                 // Take snapshot BEFORE this step's changes
8997:                 var beforeSnapshot = takeSnapshot();
8998: 
8999:                 // Apply each action in this step
9000:                 for (var ai = 0; ai < step.actions.length; ai++) {
9001:                     var act = step.actions[ai];
9002:                     applyScenarioAction(act);
9003:                 }
9004: 
9005:                 // Wait for DOM updates
9006:                 await new Promise(function (r) { setTimeout(r, 30); });
9007: 
9008:                 // Take snapshot AFTER this step's changes
9009:                 var afterSnapshot = takeSnapshot();
9010: 
9011:                 // Compute internal actions from the diff
9012:                 var internalActions = computeActions(beforeSnapshot, afterSnapshot);
9013: 
9014:                 // Build the step object
9015:                 var stepObj = {
9016:                     stepId: si + 1,
9017:                     duration: step.duration || 1.0,
9018:                     actions: internalActions,
9019:                     label: step.label || ('Step ' + (si + 1))
9020:                 };
9021: 
9022:                 // Push to scenario
9023:                 scenarioData.scenario.push(stepObj);
9024:                 stepSnapshots.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(afterSnapshot)));
9025: 
9026:                 debugLog('[AI Scenario] Step ' + (si + 1) + ': ' + internalActions.length + ' internal actions | snapshots=' + stepSnapshots.length + ' scenario=' + scenarioData.scenario.length);
9027:             }
9028:         }
9029: 
9030:         // === VERIFY SNAPSHOT INVARIANT ===
9031:         debugLog('[AI Scenario] Pre-check: snapshots=' + stepSnapshots.length + ', scenario=' + scenarioData.scenario.length + ', expected=' + (scenarioData.scenario.length + 1));
9032:         if (stepSnapshots.length !== scenarioData.scenario.length + 1) {
9033:             console.error('[AI Scenario] INVARIANT VIOLATION: snapshots=' + stepSnapshots.length + ', steps=' + scenarioData.scenario.length + ', expected snapshots=' + (scenarioData.scenario.length + 1));
9034:             // Log stack trace for debugging
9035:             console.trace('[AI Scenario] Invariant violation trace');
9036:             throw new Error('Snapshot invariant violated');
9037:         }
9038: 
9039:         debugLog('[AI Scenario] ✓ Complete: ' + setupCount + ' cards, ' + scenarioData.scenario.length + ' steps. Snapshots: ' + stepSnapshots.length);
9040: 
9041:         // Reset editing state
9042:         appState.isEditingStep = false;
9043:         currentStep = null;
9044:         startSnapshot = null;
9045: 
9046:         // Update UI
9047:         if (typeof totalSteps !== 'undefined' && totalSteps) {
9048:             totalSteps.textContent = scenarioData.scenario.length;
9049:         }
9050:         if (typeof currentStepNum !== 'undefined' && currentStepNum) {
9051:             currentStepNum.textContent = '-';
9052:         }
9053:         if (typeof addStepBtn !== 'undefined' && addStepBtn) {
9054:             addStepBtn.disabled = false;
9055:         }
9056: 
9057:         renderTimeline();
9058:         renderGroupOrderStrip();
9059:         updateUI();
9060: 
9061:         setStatus('AI scenario: ' + setupCount + ' cards, ' + scenarioData.scenario.length + ' steps created', 'success');
9062: 
9063:     } catch (err) {
9064:         console.error('[AI Scenario] Apply failed:', err);
9065:         // Rollback
9066:         scenarioData.scenario = savedScenario;
9067:         stepSnapshots = savedSnapshots;
9068:         handleResetTable();
9069:         throw new Error('Scenario apply failed: ' + err.message);
9070:     } finally {
9071:         appState._bulkApplying = false;
9072:     }
9073: }
9074: 
9075: /**
9076:  * Apply a single AI scenario action to the current board state
9077:  */
9078: function applyScenarioAction(act) {
9079:     switch (act.action) {
9080:         case 'place': {
9081:             // Place a card from tray to a slot
9082:             var card = findTrayCardByName(act.card);
9083:             if (!card) {
9084:                 console.warn('[AI Scenario] Cannot place - card not in tray: ' + act.card);
9085:                 return;
9086:             }
9087:             var place = (appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces || []).find(function (p) { return p.id === act.to; });
9088:             if (!place) {
9089:                 console.warn('[AI Scenario] Cannot place - slot not found: ' + act.to);
9090:                 return;
9091:             }
9092:             var zoneName = 'grid-' + act.to;
9093:             var zoneElement = document.querySelector('.card-drop-zone[data-zone="' + zoneName + '"]');
9094:             card.isFaceUp = act.faceUp === true;
9095:             if (zoneElement) {
9096:                 placeCardInZone(card, zoneName, place.rotation || 0, zoneElement);
9097:             } else {
9098:                 placeCardOnTable(card, place.x || 640, place.y || 360);
9099:             }
9100:             // Re-set isFaceUp because placeCardInZone overrides it from UI checkboxes
9101:             card.isFaceUp = act.faceUp === true;
9102:             if (card.element) {
9103:                 var img = card.element.querySelector('img');
9104:                 if (img) {
9105:                     img.src = card.isFaceUp ? (card.frontImageUrl || '') : (card.backImageUrl || '');
9106:                 }
9107:                 card.element.classList.toggle('face-up', card.isFaceUp);
9108:                 card.element.classList.toggle('face-down', !card.isFaceUp);
9109:             }
9110:             break;
9111:         }
9112: 
9113:         case 'flip': {
9114:             // Flip a card in-place
9115:             var card = findTableCardByName(act.card);
9116:             if (!card) {
9117:                 console.warn('[AI Scenario] Cannot flip - card not on table: ' + act.card);
9118:                 return;
9119:             }
9120:             card.isFaceUp = act.faceUp === true;
9121:             // Re-render the card element
9122:             if (card.element) {
9123:                 if (card.isFaceUp) {
9124:                     card.element.classList.remove('face-down');
9125:                     card.element.classList.add('face-up');
9126:                 } else {
9127:                     card.element.classList.remove('face-up');
9128:                     card.element.classList.add('face-down');
9129:                 }
9130:                 // Update the image
9131:                 var img = card.element.querySelector('img');
9132:                 if (img) {
9133:                     img.src = card.isFaceUp ? (card.frontImageUrl || '') : (card.backImageUrl || '');
9134:                 }
9135:             }
9136:             break;
9137:         }
9138: 
9139:         case 'move': {
9140:             // Move card from current zone to new zone
9141:             var card = findTableCardByName(act.card);
9142:             if (!card) {
9143:                 console.warn('[AI Scenario] Cannot move - card not on table: ' + act.card);
9144:                 return;
9145:             }
9146:             var oldZone = card.zone;
9147: 
9148:             // Remove from current zone visually
9149:             if (card.element) {
9150:                 card.element.remove();
9151:                 card.element = null;
9152:             }
9153: 
9154:             // Remove from tableCards
9155:             var idx = appState.tableCards.indexOf(card);
9156:             if (idx > -1) appState.tableCards.splice(idx, 1);
9157: 
9158:             // Re-index remaining cards in old zone
9159:             if (oldZone) {
9160:                 appState.tableCards.filter(function (c) { return c.zone === oldZone; })
9161:                     .sort(function (a, b) { return (a.zonePosition || 0) - (b.zonePosition || 0); })
9162:                     .forEach(function (c, i) { c.zonePosition = i; });
9163:             }
9164: 
9165:             // Place in new zone
9166:             var targetSlotId = act.to;
9167:             var place = (appState.boardLayout.cardPlaces || []).find(function (p) { return p.id === targetSlotId; });
9168:             if (!place) {
9169:                 console.warn('[AI Scenario] Cannot move - target slot not found: ' + targetSlotId);
9170:                 return;
9171:             }
9172: 
9173:             if (act.faceUp !== undefined) card.isFaceUp = act.faceUp === true;
9174:             card.rotation = place.rotation || 0;
9175:             card.zone = 'grid-' + targetSlotId;
9176:             card.zonePosition = appState.tableCards.filter(function (c) { return c.zone === card.zone; }).length;
9177: 
9178:             appState.tableCards.push(card);
9179:             var zoneElement = document.querySelector('.card-drop-zone[data-zone="' + card.zone + '"]');
9180:             if (zoneElement) {
9181:                 createZoneCardElement(card, zoneElement);
9182:             }
9183:             break;
9184:         }
9185: 
9186:         case 'remove': {
9187:             // Remove card from board (return to tray)
9188:             var card = findTableCardByName(act.card);
9189:             if (!card) {
9190:                 console.warn('[AI Scenario] Cannot remove - card not on table: ' + act.card);
9191:                 return;
9192:             }
9193:             var oldZone = card.zone;
9194: 
9195:             // Remove element
9196:             if (card.element) {
9197:                 card.element.remove();
9198:                 card.element = null;
9199:             }
9200: 
9201:             // Remove from tableCards
9202:             var idx = appState.tableCards.indexOf(card);
9203:             if (idx > -1) appState.tableCards.splice(idx, 1);
9204: 
9205:             // Re-index remaining cards in old zone
9206:             if (oldZone) {
9207:                 appState.tableCards.filter(function (c) { return c.zone === oldZone; })
9208:                     .sort(function (a, b) { return (a.zonePosition || 0) - (b.zonePosition || 0); })
9209:                     .forEach(function (c, i) { c.zonePosition = i; });
9210:             }
9211: 
9212:             // Return to tray
9213:             card.inTray = true;
9214:             card.zone = null;
9215:             card.zonePosition = 0;
9216:             break;
9217:         }
9218: 
9219:         default:
9220:             console.warn('[AI Scenario] Unknown action: ' + act.action + ' for ' + act.card);
9221:     }
9222: }
9223: 
9224: function showAIStatus(msg) {
9225:     if (aiStatus) {
9226:         aiStatus.textContent = msg;
9227:         aiStatus.classList.remove('hidden');
9228:     }
9229: }
9230: 
9231: function hideAIStatus() {
9232:     if (aiStatus) aiStatus.classList.add('hidden');
9233: }
9234: 
9235: function showAIError(msg) {
9236:     if (aiError) {
9237:         aiError.textContent = '❌ ' + msg;
9238:         aiError.classList.remove('hidden');
9239:     }
9240:     hideAIStatus();
9241: }
9242: 
9243: function hideAIError() {
9244:     if (aiError) aiError.classList.add('hidden');
9245: }
